Lu Ye clearly saw numerous cultivators forming a defense line outside the domain, resisting the invading Insect Race. Around the battlefield, countless corpses and debris drifted.

This was undoubtedly a domain conflict, an invasion war.

Years ago, the four galaxies faced such invasions. Without Lu Ye bringing in the Dancing Girl, the domain might have been conquered by the Insect and Blood Races.

In the stellar space, insect hives like these seeking invasion targets were not particularly numerous, but they were not few either. Every such gigantic insect hive was equivalent to a drifting domain.

Before discovering a target to invade, the Insect Race rested and thrived. Once a target was found, they launched an all-out assault. Typically, life in the domain conquered by such insect hives was entirely wiped out. The Insect Race would remain in the domain for some years before exhausting its resources and departing, leaving the invaded domain in ruin, devoid of life.

Many dead stars in the stellar space originated in this manner.

Lu Ye neither knew which star system this was nor which domain was being invaded, but encountering such a situation, he decided not to stand idly by.

If he lacked the ability to intervene, so be it. But at this moment, he possessed the ability to intervene, and exterminate the Insect Race was undoubtedly the right action.

He immediately changed direction, piloting the core directly toward the gigantic insect hive.

Initially, neither side in the Void combat noticed anything amiss. The intensity of the battle left no room for distraction.

But as Lu Ye approached, his presence was eventually exposed.

The first to spot him was a Sun Blaze insect!

Outside the chaotic Void battlefield was a separate battleground — a Sun Blaze confrontation zone. There, two Sun Blaze insects joined forces against a human Sun Blaze, their strengths seemingly evenly matched. Faced with two opponents, the human Sun Blaze was clearly in a precarious situation.

Even so, it wasn't easy for the insect Sun Blaze to kill him.

As Lu Ye piloted the core closer to the battlefield, one of the Sun Blaze insects suddenly broke away from the fight and, with wings flapping behind it, rushed toward Lu Ye.

Before getting close, a powerful Divine Soul Power assaulted him.

Sitting atop the core, Lu Ye didn't even make a sound, but simply tilted his head and fell over.

Seeing this, the insect Sun Blaze couldn't help but snort, "Overestimating oneself!"

Though he dismissed Lu Ye as insignificant, the core beneath Lu Ye puzzled him due to its exceptional nature — it was no ordinary item — though what it truly was remained unknown.

Regardless of its nature, acquiring it seemed prudent. Thus thinking, he reached toward the core, ready to grasp it.

Already slumped on the core, Lu Ye abruptly opened his eyes, calmly staring at him, showing no signs of injury.

The insect Sun Blaze hesitated, but before he could react, a consuming force exploded, engulfing him entirely.

Next, his vision blurred, and the once raucous conflict vanished utterly, leaving him inexplicably in an unfamiliar world.

Looking around, he discovered four figures encircling him, and sensing their presence, he was greatly astonished — all four were at the Moon Jade Late Stage!



============================================================
Chapter 1810: Chapter 1810 1808: Divine Weapon Descends from the Heavens
============================================================

The sudden mysterious disappearance of the Insect Race Sun Blaze baffled another Insect Race Sun Blaze engaged in battle. Taking advantage of this distraction, the Human Race Sun Blaze finally turned the tide.

This Human Race Sun Blaze was previously in a tough spot, fighting two opponents at once. Now, regaining the upper hand, he counterattacked and entangled the enemy.

He didn't know who Lu Ye was, nor why an enemy Sun Blaze vanished so strangely, but he was sure of one thing: Lu Ye was of the Human Race and had helped him, for which he felt very grateful.

Facing just one opponent, the Insect Race Sun Blaze found it hard to disengage, growing increasingly anxious.

Seeing that the mountain-sized core was heading straight for the insect hive, the Insect Race Sun Blaze hurriedly shouted, "Stop him!"

The insect hive was the foundation of this Insect Race faction and could not be lost.

The Insect Race cultivators obeyed the order, mustering their strength and launching it at Lu Ye, creating a chaotic storm of spirit force and mana.

No one could underestimate such a dense wave of attacks.

But Lu Ye sat calmly atop the core, unmoving, completely disregarding the concentrated assault from all directions.

With a thought, a mysterious power emanated from the core world, forming an invisible barrier that enveloped the surrounding space.

This mysterious power was the innate force of the core world and not Lu Ye's mana.

After refining the core's origin, Lu Ye noticed he could not only pilot the core like a starboat but also freely command the core world's power for his use.

Relishing this incredible experience, which he never had before, he wouldn't have dared to recklessly charge into a battlefield of contending Sun Blazes without this confidence.

The oncoming strikes from the Insect Race were all blocked by the invisible barrier, unable to harm Lu Ye in the slightest.

Some Insect Race cultivators in front failed to evade and were directly smashed to pieces by the core.

The distance to the insect hive rapidly closed.

The massive insect hive ahead began showing signs of movement; clearly, the insects inside realized the shift in the situation and attempted to maneuver the hive out of harm's way.

However, moving such a colossal insect hive wasn't easy. Unlike Lu Ye, the Insect Race couldn't control their world core with such ease.

Under countless terrified Insect Race eyes, the core, over ten meters long, crashed directly into the giant insect hive.

With unstoppable speed, combined with the domain force's impact, a large dent appeared in the Insect Race cultivators' sight at the collision point.

In a crushing smash, the gigantic insect hive was punctured through, claiming countless Insect Race lives at that moment.

And it wasn't over. Almost the instant the core world broke away from the insect hive, the horrifying impact finally fully detonated inside!

In truth, the insect hive wasn't very sturdy at all and couldn't withstand such a shock. Having already been pierced through, the hive shattered to pieces under the expanding impact.

Numerous Insect Race cultivators watched, their eyes bloodshot with rage.

On the Human Race's side, however, spirits were notably lifted.

The sole Human Race Sun Blaze couldn't help but shout, "Kill!"

In this war, the most troubling issue for the Human Race wasn't just the disparity in numbers or Sun Blaze count, but the Insect Race's never-ending combat capability.

Once injured, the Insect Race would swiftly retreat to the insect hive to heal and then reemerge on the battlefield, rejuvenated.

In contrast, the Human Race couldn't enjoy such convenience.

As the disparity grew, the Human Race found it increasingly strenuous. Without any unexpected incidents, this battle was destined to end in a crushing defeat for the Human Race. Should this happen, their domain would surely fall, and all humans within would face utter annihilation.

No one anticipated that, in such a tense situation, a divine weapon would descend, steering an unknown artifact and directly shattering the Insect Race's insect hive!

This would undoubtedly ease the Human Race's pressure during the ensuing confrontations.

Moreover, this unexpected ally used some mysterious means to make one of the enemy's Sun Blazes disappear...

Countless humans gratefully looked towards the direction of Lu Ye, but how could they see him anymore? Lu Ye had already piloted the core to tens of thousands of miles away.

At that moment, under his control, the core stopped, and he flickered into the core world.

A fierce battle was raging!

Xiang Yin and her sister, Yang Ling, and Hu Dequan, four Moon Jade Late-Stage cultivators together fiercely clashed with the Insect Race Sun Blaze that had been devoured by this realm.

Under normal circumstances, four Moon Jade Late-Stage cultivators couldn't be opponents for a Sun Blaze, not even together. The prowess of a Sun Blaze overwhelmingly surpassed that of a Moon Jade, and the mere suppression at the Divine Soul level was unbreakable for Moon Jades.

Yet, on the battlefield within the core world, they managed to maintain a rough balance.

Xiang Yin and her sister fully employed the Blood Sea Technique to trap the Insect Race Sun Blaze within. Yang Ling and Hu Dequan hid inside, biding their time, launching surprise attacks every so often, and retreating immediately after a failed assault.

In the heat of battle, Yang Ling's Mental Consciousness surged as he transmitted to a few companions, "What's going on here? Why did an Insect Race Sun Blaze suddenly appear? Where did it come from? Brother Lu, explain a bit."

He had too many doubts.

After the struggle at Black Abyss ended, Sacred Blood Summit was eradicated, even the treasure blood of the Blood Ancestor suppressed. He and Hu Dequan only needed to wait patiently, and one day, the three parts of Mount Fangcun would reassemble in one place, allowing him to see his long-yearned Dao companion again.

Who would have thought that just now, he inexplicably ended up here, along with Xiang Yin and sister, and Hu Dequan.

And there, standing before him, was an Insect Race Sun Blaze!

Thus, a confused and chaotic battle erupted just like that.

He was puzzled, and the Insect Race Sun Blaze even more so, for from the Insect Race's perspective, the Blood Race was their natural ally. If they encountered each other in stellar space, even if they didn't celebrate with wine, they would at least show closeness. This was a profound friendship forged from countless times of fighting side by side over the years.

Therefore, he couldn't understand why there was a Blood Race ambushing him here. He tried to communicate with the other side but received no response. Annoyed, he could only prepare to kill the opponent first and talk later.

However, just as he was ready to do so, a chilling scene unfolded.

A mysterious power descended from the void, weighing on him like a mountain. If his strength weren't sufficient, he would kneel and crawl on the ground, unable to move.

It could be said that he could only exert sixty percent of his peak strength at this moment.

He exclaimed in shock, "Heaven and Earth Force!"

Someone was controlling the Heaven and Earth Force of this domain to suppress him!

This was simply unbelievable because to control a domain's Heaven and Earth Force, one had to become that domain's master and refine its Origin.

There were cultivators like this in stellar space, but they were extremely rare. Each one of them was a true World Lord; he couldn't comprehend how he was unlucky enough to encounter one.

Even though he could only exert sixty percent of his peak strength, and was trapped in the Blood Sea, he could still contend evenly with Xiang Yin and the others, occasionally even gaining the upper hand.

What he relied upon was no more than his deeper Divine Soul Power. His soul attacks were formless and invisible, making it hard for Xiang Yin and the others to defend against them. Over time, if he found a flaw, he might break them one by one.

During the time when the four Moon Jade Late-Stage cultivators were overwhelmed, Lu Ye's aura suddenly appeared.

The four rejoiced greatly.

In the next moment, sounds of fierce clashes emanated from the Blood Sea, accompanied by a muffled groan, causing the entire Blood Sea to boil as if it were about to erupt, nearly overwhelming Xiang Yin and sister.

At this time, the expression of the Insect Race Sun Blaze covered by the Blood Sea was uncertain.

He also noticed Lu Ye's arrival and naturally recognized him as the human Moon Jade he intended to eliminate, who suddenly broke into the battlefield.

Initially, seeing the other was only at the Moon Jade Mid-Stage level, he didn't take it seriously. But the instantaneous exchange made him realize one thing — this human Moon Jade's strength was absurdly strong, stronger than any Moon Jade he had ever encountered.

Fortunately, the opponent was just a Moon Jade. If they were both Sun Blazes, he feared the outcome would be grim for himself.

Was it him who controlled the Heaven and Earth Force of this domain? The Insect Race Sun Blaze's thoughts shifted, unable to decipher it, but regardless, this Moon Jade was highly suspicious, so he immediately charged towards Lu Ye's position, intending to eliminate him first.

Almost at the moment he moved, Lu Ye also invoked the Blood Sea Technique, merging his own Blood Sea with that of Xiang Yin and sister.

In an instant, the Blood Sea became even denser.

Sensing the clear intent to kill from the Insect Race Sun Blaze, Lu Ye brandished the Boulder Mountain Saber, his figure brazenly plundering forward.

The Brazen Plundering Technique was already elusive and now, with the Void Spirit Runes constantly constructing around him amidst the Blood Sea, it became even more spectrally bewitching.

The Insect Race Sun Blaze was stupefied because even with cultivation surpassing Lu Ye by a large realm, he could not easily track Lu Ye's movements at that moment.

The figure coming and going rapidly had no pattern whatsoever. Often, when he believed he had pinpointed him and struck, it hit nothing but air, allowing Lu Ye to seize the opportunity to close in and carve a shallow wound at his vulnerable spots with the Boulder Mountain Saber.

Not only that, but Xiang Yin and the others continued their relentless attacks, sticking to a strategy of hit-and-run, leaving no room for counterattack.

The Insect Race Sun Blaze was furious, feeling like a solitary lion, beset by skulking hyenas, unable to find an effective solution despite the situation.

In his prime, he could easily crush these few Moon Jades, but now he was suppressed by the Heaven and Earth Force.

Pressing down his anger, he calmly waited for an opportunity, aware that such an aggressive attack was bound to have a flaw. Once he caught it, he could decide the outcome in one strike.

In other words, he could afford countless mistakes, but the enemy could only afford one.

The advantage is mine!

But gradually, he sensed something was amiss.

His wounds were healing extremely slowly, seemingly entangled in a peculiar force that hindered recovery. Even his Sun Blaze physique found it hard to escape.



============================================================
Chapter 1811: Chapter 1811 1809: Overbearing Slaughter
============================================================

Even more chilling to the Insect Race Sun Blaze was the mysterious power emanating from the Blood Sea, pulling his blood from the wounds, rendering his attempts to block it with Mana fraught with difficulty.

The barghest's power, combined with the Blood Attraction Technique, was a tactic developed years ago by Lu Ye and Ma Shangsi, aimed precisely at strong enemies like this. Unable to deliver a fatal blow in one strike, they would wear them down slowly.

The barghest's power is crucial; without its ability to impede wound healing, the Blood Attraction Technique would be ineffective.

Although Ma Shangsi was not present, Xiang Yin and sister could easily perform the Blood Attraction Technique.

This marked the beginning of a fierce and frustrating battle for the Insect Race Sun Blaze - arguably the most arduous ordeal of his life. Although he possessed the power for a decisive strike, he could not pin down his enemy's position.

As time passed, the Insect Race Sun Blaze's body was in tatters, countless cuts inflicted by Lu Ye.

It must be said, Sun Blaze's physique is remarkably powerful, especially as a member of the Insect Race. As Lu Ye advanced to Moon Jade, the Boulder Mountain Saber, elevated to the level of a magic treasure, was sharp enough, and Lu Ye enhanced it with Divine Sharp Edge Spirit Runes. Yet, even with each slash, it was difficult to cause any significant damage, merely leaving superficial wounds.

Now, these superficial wounds on Sun Blaze have become a heavy burden!

An entire day's brutal battle left the Insect Race Sun Blaze's face pale, his aura significantly diminished, seemingly at his wits' end.

Not only him, but other Moon Jade cultivators besides Lu Ye struggled as well.

Firstly, such a confrontation drains huge amounts of energy, requiring the Moon Jade cultivators to remain tense and fully utilize their Mana. To persist for so long was a testament to their extraordinary foundation.

Secondly, each suffered multiple Divine Soul Shocks from the Insect Race Sun Blaze, an impact they found insurmountable and incomprehensible.

After repeated shocks, all four Moon Jade Late Stage cultivators felt dizzy, unsettled, and their actions sluggish.

Under Lu Ye's orders, the four had retreated early from the Blood Sea battlefield to prevent the enemy from seizing an opportunity for a fatal strike.

Now, within the turbulent Blood Sea, only Lu Ye remained to fight alone.

The moment of truth was near!

After leaving another mark on the Insect Race Sun Blaze, Lu Ye's expression turned solemn. Reaching into the Void, he grabbed a slender bone saber in his left hand.

The bone saber came from an Insect Race he had slain, likely a descendant of a Praying Mantis that had used the Great Windmill Secret Technique against him, only for Lu Ye to perfectly counter and kill him, leaving the foe in confusion.

His pair of bone sabers became Lu Ye's spoils of war.

The bone saber was actually part of the Insect Race's body, refined over countless years, extremely hard and incredibly sharp, rivaling the finest magic treasures in quality, though slightly inferior to the current Boulder Mountain Saber level.

The Brazen Plundering Technique can only continuously weaken an Insect Race Sun Blaze but cannot execute a true kill.

The Drawn Saber Slash, Lu Ye could not use, as he had been refining Origin since the Black Abyss battle, neglecting to nurture the Drawn Saber Slash Spirit Runes.

Currently, his most ferocious secret technique was the Great Windmill.

He had once used it to cut down a Sun Blaze influenced by Dancing Girl, history seemed poised to repeat itself.

With a gentle breath, the boundless Blood Sea surged toward him, disappearing in an instant.

On Lu Ye's surface, blood Qi surged, thin red mist enveloping, rapidly pushing his blood Qi to the limit, with Mana humming inside his body.

Suddenly freed, the Insect Race Sun Blaze barely responded before weakly facing Lu Ye, with his expression turning grim.

He realized Lu Ye intended to make a killing strike.

Soon, however, his face showed curiosity as he saw a peculiar blood mark emerge between Lu Ye's eyebrows.

"Body Flower?" Insect Race Sun Blaze strained his eyes, doubting his vision.

As a Sun Blaze, his experience was substantial, having heard whispers of such cultivation mysteries, including the Body Flower.

The legend states that a cultivator pushing the Constellation Realm to the extreme would condense the Body Flower.

Yet, he only heard of this without witnessing such a phenomenon, unsure of its truth, considering many prominent Insect Race Constellation Realm members existed but none displayed such development.

He had assumed it a myth until witnessing it firsthand.

Suddenly understanding why this human cultivator was so formidable - genuinely reaching the pinnacle of the Constellation Realm, achieving a feat few dared contemplate.

Intense danger surged within, as the Insect Race Sun Blaze sensed death's embrace and, facing such peril, let out a furious roar, pouring all effort into activating a Psyche Secret Technique.

It was a long-held trump card, untouched until this desperate gamble.

Simultaneously, Divine Soul Power erupted from Lu Ye, his right eye transforming into a blood-red hue, within which intricate spirit runes unfolded, rendering the eye grotesque and fearsome.

Blood Eye emerges!

This is the second time Lu Ye has used the Blood Eye Spirit Runes since he obtained them, the first time was an experiment, allowing him to slightly understand the mysteries of the Blood Eye Spirit Runes.

In line with the Blood Eye he saw within the marvel, this Blood Eye Spirit Runes, when activated, has an obvious effect of illusion, both mysterious and powerful.

The Insect Race Sun Blaze before him is not the guy affected by the Dancing Girl's power, restricted in action.

Nor is he the Lih Tian besieged by many Moon Jade cultivators, looking for death.

Even though Lu Ye utilizes the power of the Core World to suppress him, and even though he appears extremely weak at the moment, facing such an enemy, Lu Ye dares not be careless the slightest bit.

Thus, he brought out all his skills, even pushing his own strength to the extreme.

The emergence of the Body Flower is the most obvious sign, representing that Lu Ye's blood Qi has been pushed to the limit.

The Insect Race Sun Blaze instinctively met that single Blood Eye, and for an instant, his expression was momentarily dazed, as if he saw a gigantic giant standing tall, gazing down at him with one eye.

And again, as if seeing a scarlet rising in the sky, bathed in moonlight, the entire world drenched in blood.

Ultimately, being a Sun Blaze, even though Lu Ye activated the Blood Eye Spirit Runes, the impact on him was only for that instant.

The next moment, all the illusions before the Insect Race Sun Blaze vanished completely, however, his expression changed drastically.

Because his meticulously prepared killer move was interfered with for that instant, showing signs of collapse, leading directly to an extremely adverse consequence—Divine Sea turmoil, Divine Soul Power in utter chaos.

Just like a magic cultivator preparing to cast a large magic spell, interrupted at the critical moment, the mana upheaval will surely backlash against himself, the Insect Race Sun Blaze's current experience is roughly similar.

He opened his mouth to cry out miserably, his face filled with an expression of pain, instinctively raising his hand to hold his head.

Seeing this, Lu Ye had no hesitation, brazenly charged forward, as the saber gleamed, the Boulder Mountain Saber had slashed down!

His body turned with the fall of the Boulder Mountain Saber, as one slash ended, the bone saber emerged.

The initial few slashes could still be traced, but after a few slashes, there was only a wild storm formed by a continuous gleam of saber light, enveloping a vast area.

In the distance, Yang Ling and others who had long retreated from the battlefield looked on in astonishment, even Xiang Yin and her sister were no exception.

Though in the contest with the Red Talisman Society, Lu Ye had already showcased strength beyond his cultivation, they truly hadn't expected that what they witnessed wasn't the full extent.

Perhaps this is the true display of Lu Ye's power!

That utterly terrifying killing intent, the fierce and violent offense, is not something a Moon Jade can withstand, Yang Ling, though considering himself a strong one among the Moon Jade, secretly imagined that if facing such an offense, he might not last over two breaths…

The saber light gradually retracted, Lu Ye stood in place, maintaining the posture of holding the saber with both hands, his blood Qi boiling to the extreme, the blood mist on his body rose upwards.

Centered around him, within about 30 miles, crisscrossing ravines of horrifying depth emerged.

The Insect Race Sun Blaze was nowhere to be seen, only chunks of shattered remains on the ground held traces of him once alive.

Despite having expectations in their hearts, witnessing this scene felt like being in a dream for Yang Ling and others.

Moon Jade defeating Sun Blaze… How absurd a notion, yet it happened right beneath their gaze.

Yang Ling felt that this scene before him might never be forgotten for the rest of his life.

The sound of cracking continued, Lu Ye staggered slightly, and in that moment, countless flesh and blood within him seemed to rupture.

He put away the Boulder Mountain Saber and the bone saber, sat down cross-legged, took out an elixir pill to consume, silently recovering, his expression neither happy nor sad.

This Insect Race Sun Blaze was not the first Sun Blaze to die by his hand, and in this battle, the opponent couldn't exert his full strength, so there's nothing to be happy about.

If someday he can truly kill a Sun Blaze with genuine skill, that's worth celebrating.

That day will come, and it won't be too far off.

Several days later, after recovering, Lu Ye exchanged a few words with Yang Ling and others who were still healing, and then leaped out of the Core World.

Then he took out his starboat, headed back along the path he came from.

He wanted to see how the battlefield situation over there was, assuming that by dealing with one Sun Blaze and destroying the insect hive, the pressure on the domain's human race cultivators should be greatly alleviated, but some things still need to be seen with his own eyes.

Before Lu Ye could reach the original battlefield, a group of cultivators flew over from that direction, hurriedly, Mental Consciousness spread all around, seemingly seeking something.



============================================================
Chapter 1812: Chapter 1812 1810: Life Origin
============================================================

The cultivators approaching from the front were not in perfect condition, looking like they had just been through a great battle, with numerous traces of disarray.

Upon spotting Lu Ye approaching head-on, the leading Moon Jade immediately came forward, cupping his fists from afar: "Lin Ran from Life Origin, greetings Fellow Daoist!"

Lin Ran had seen Lu Ye from afar. After all, a few days ago, when Lu Ye had steered the core onto that scorched battlefield, he was seated cross-legged on it without concealing his form, so many cultivators had seen his figure from afar.

For the Life Origin World, having one of the two Sun Blaze from the Insect Race removed, and the insect hive breached, undoubtedly helped immensely. Otherwise, the Life Origin World might already be in ruins, so even though he didn't know Lu Ye's background or identity, he showed a grateful expression upon seeing him, as it was indeed a lifesaving favor.

The cultivators following behind him also bowed in unison.

Lu Ye returned the salute: "Jade Conch, Lu Ye!"

He initially intended to investigate the situation of the battle over there, but upon seeing Lin Ran and the others, he understood there was no need. If the battle had not already ended, these people would not have been able to come here, and their demeanor clearly indicated they were looking for his whereabouts.

Life Origin should have won.

Though he had a guess in his heart, Lu Ye still asked.

As expected, Lin Ran informed him that the Insect Race had retreated.

The biggest reliance of the Insect Race was the two Sun Blaze and the insect hive. One Sun Blaze mysteriously disappeared, and the insect hive was shattered, instantly losing their advantage.

Many cultivators from the Life Origin World rose to resist, killing countless from the Insect Race.

The remaining Sun Blaze from the Insect Race, seeing the unfavorable situation, immediately retreated, probably also wary of Lu Ye's side, as the disappearance of his companion was too bizarre. Without finding out the whereabouts or even the life and death of his companion, he dared not linger outside the Life Origin World.

Though the Life Origin World won this battle and preserved the domain, the losses were significant. The Sun Blaze from their world was heavily injured and is currently recuperating within the domain.

"I was sent by Master Uncle Qin Jiang to investigate, Fellow Daoist Lu, that Sun Blaze from the Insect Race..." Lin Ran looked at Lu Ye. The Qin Jiang he mentioned was undoubtedly the Sun Blaze cultivator of the Life Origin World.

Lu Ye replied, "Fellow Daoist need not worry, that Sun Blaze from the Insect Race is already dead."

Lin Ran and the human race cultivators were overjoyed, hastening to ask, "May I ask which senior helped?"

It wasn't that he underestimated Lu Ye, but Lu Ye's Moon Jade mid-stage cultivation was evident, and the gap with Sun Blaze was too large, making it impossible for him to have such means.

Lu Ye also realized this issue, and after a brief ponder, replied, "My esteemed master personally took action and slew him." Not wanting to claim it as his kill, he just concocted a story.

Lin Ran showed an expression of understanding, looking behind Lu Ye and asked, "May I ask where your master is now..."

Lu Ye promptly replied, "My master fought with the enemy, got injured, and is recuperating, ordering me to check on the progress of your battle."

Lin Ran's expression tightened, and with concern, he asked, "Are the injuries severe?"

"Not too severe."

"If Fellow Daoist doesn't mind, may I invite your master to the Life Origin World to heal? Our world will offer the best healing resources, and additionally, Master Uncle Qin Jiang wants to express his thanks in person."

Lu Ye shook his head and said, "There's no need. My master is... rather reclusive and not accustomed to interacting with others. Since the battle in your domain has ended, my master and I will take our leave, Fellow Daoist, take care!"

Lu Ye cupped his fists, turning to leave.

Lin Ran hurriedly exclaimed, "Fellow Daoist, please wait! Such a great kindness is beyond repayment; no matter what, please allow us to do something, otherwise, we won't be able to explain to Master Uncle Qin Jiang when we return."

Lu Ye paused, turning to look at him, intending to refuse, but suddenly recalled something, and said, "If that's the case, would Fellow Daoist mind collecting some fire-type resources? My master has great use for them!" He had exhausted all the fire-type resources on him as well as the Talent Tree's fuel reserves, initially planning to replenish them later, but now there's an opportunity to get some for temporary use.

Moreover, although he consumed little in this battle, it actually consumed the essence of the Core World!

The power sealing the Sun Blaze from the Insect Race came from the Core World's essence, which was also why Lu Ye eventually used the Great Windmill Secret Technique, for sealing a Sun Blaze exhausted the Core World's essence significantly, and the earlier the opponent was dealt with, the sooner this consumption would cease.

Otherwise, Lu Ye could slowly wear down that Sun Blaze without taking risks.

Once a world's essence is exhausted, recovering it is very troublesome. At this moment, Lu Ye only sought some fire-type resources from the Life Origin World, a trifling matter compared to the consumption of the domain's essence.

Lin Ran's eyes brightened, quickly nodding, "Fellow Daoist, please wait a moment."

Saying this, he took out an audio talisman to send a message, giving some instructions.

He soon looked at Lu Ye again, "Within the domain, we will collect fire-type resources with full effort, and they will be delivered within half a day."

During the wait, Lin Ran chatted with Lu Ye, repeatedly proposing to visit the fictitious master to express thanks in person, all of which Lu Ye deftly deflected.

Lu Ye also thought of a problem: "Though the battle is won, if the Insect Race comes back, how will you respond?"

The Sun Blaze from the Insect Race wasn't dead but had escaped, and there's no guarantee they won't find another insect hive and lead it back to the Life Origin World side.

This could take a long time, but it's very likely to happen someday.

Lin Ran couldn't help but sigh: "There is really no good countermeasure, we can only strive for cultivation. Hopefully, by the time that day arrives, this domain will have enough power to protect itself."

Lu Ye remained silent. This time he was fortunate to be in the right place, lending a hand to the Life Origin World, saving them from peril, but next time they might not have such luck. Indeed, they must rely on their own efforts.

The Insect and Blood Races are the most notorious races in the stellar space. Comparatively, the harm from the Insect Race is somewhat greater than that from the Blood Race, due to the living methods of these two races.

The Blood Race owns several domains, all transformed from the remains of Blood Ancestors after their death, generally fixed locations. Even if the Blood Race does campaign outward, they only capture living beings to raise them, ensuring the supply of Blood Food.

However, the Insect Race is different. This race does not have a fixed place for cultivation; they typically base their existence on insect hives, drifting through stellar space. If they encounter any potential targets along the way, they would initiate a war.

Though, there are exceptions to everything. Sometimes, there are also Blood Race members within insect hives. Cooperation between the two races is not uncommon.

Half a day later, a cultivator hurriedly arrived from the direction of the Life Origin World, bringing several storage rings to Lin Ran.

Lin Ran briefly inspected them and then handed them over to Lu Ye.

"Fellow Daoist, can't you invite your Master to our Life Origin World for healing?" Lin Ran still wanted to make a final effort.

Lu Ye shook his head: "I appreciate your goodwill, Fellow Daoist. My master and I have no fixed place, wandering everywhere. As fellow humans, it is natural to lend a helping hand when our companions are in trouble. But going to your domain for healing is unnecessary now. My Master is already in a meditative trance, and it's not appropriate to disturb abruptly."

Lin Ran lamented deeply: "Your Master's righteousness is admirable! We at Life Origin will remember it deeply, and if we meet again someday, we'll certainly repay."

"Until we meet again." Lu Ye clasped his fists, picked up those rings, and swiftly departed.

Lin Ran and the others watched as he left.

Moments later, Lu Ye returned to the core location, sat atop it, and with a focused mind, maneuvered the core to continue the journey.

While traveling, he refined the fire-type resources obtained from the Life Origin World. Within days, he completely refined them.

Inspecting the Talent Tree, Lu Ye felt somewhat relieved. The lack of fuel in the Talent Tree made him uneasy, but now he could breathe a bit easier.

However, the fuel at hand was not sufficient. The treasure blood mixed within the Origin wasn't completely refined. This issue must be resolved later, but first, he needed to settle the core.

A storage ring appeared again in his hand. This was left by the deceased Insect Race Sun Blaze.

The legacy of a Sun Blaze was full of anticipation for Lu Ye, who devoted himself to deciphering the restriction lock on the storage ring.

After more than half a day, when the restriction lock on the ring was broken, Lu Ye's examination made his face turn dark!

Because the legacy within the ring was worlds apart from his expectations; there was hardly anything valuable inside, not even much spirit jade or spirit crystal!

Upon reflection, this wasn't surprising.

The survival mode of the Insect Race dictates that their warriors wouldn't have many resources on hand. The resources they acquire are mostly invested into the insect hives. Insect hives can convert all acquired resources into nourishment, with Insect Race's cultivation, healing, and growth happening within them.

This is somewhat similar to how he stores fuel within the Talent Tree, except the insect hives reserve nourishment made from resources acquired by the Insect Race.

Now, the massive accumulation of nourishment has also vanished with the destruction of the insect hives.

Lu Ye felt quite helpless.

Heading forward, the core finally reached its predetermined location.

In the Void, Lu Ye's Mental Consciousness surged, utilizing the seven-color Divine Lotus within the Divine Sea to connect with the Soul Race ancestral land. As time passed, the vague connection grew increasingly stronger.

Until one moment, a portal suddenly opened in the void ahead.

Lu Ye maneuvered the core and rushed in through the portal.

After a whirlwind-like rotation, familiar scenery unfolded before his eyes once again.

The Soul Race ancestral land, arrived!

Simultaneously, at the eastern Mount Fangcun, Immortal Spirit Peak, Su Yuqing, who was cultivating with closed eyes, suddenly opened her eyes, revealing a puzzled expression.

Because just at that instant, she suddenly felt a strange anomaly, which she had never sensed before.

Not just her, on Misty Peak, Woo Qimo, who was watching the clouds roll by, also showed a look of suspicion and surprise simultaneously.

On Cloud Sea Peak, Chen Xuanhai stood with hands behind his back, suddenly raised his head to look at the sky, his eyebrows lifted. After a brief hesitation, he suddenly soared into the sky.

Feeling Chen Xuanhai's movement, Su Yuqing and Woo Qimo also flickered and rushed out toward the sky.

The three Sun Blaze cultivators had already developed a hypothesis, but to confirm whether this hypothesis was true, they had to see for themselves.

Even for such mighty figures as them, their expressions were filled with excitement and anticipation, for if the hypothesis were true, it would be a joyous event awaited by the Dwarf Race for countless years!



============================================================
Chapter 1811: Chapter 1811 1809: Overbearing Slaughter
============================================================

Even more chilling to the Insect Race Sun Blaze was the mysterious power emanating from the Blood Sea, pulling his blood from the wounds, rendering his attempts to block it with Mana fraught with difficulty.

The barghest's power, combined with the Blood Attraction Technique, was a tactic developed years ago by Lu Ye and Ma Shangsi, aimed precisely at strong enemies like this. Unable to deliver a fatal blow in one strike, they would wear them down slowly.

The barghest's power is crucial; without its ability to impede wound healing, the Blood Attraction Technique would be ineffective.

Although Ma Shangsi was not present, Xiang Yin and sister could easily perform the Blood Attraction Technique.

This marked the beginning of a fierce and frustrating battle for the Insect Race Sun Blaze - arguably the most arduous ordeal of his life. Although he possessed the power for a decisive strike, he could not pin down his enemy's position.

As time passed, the Insect Race Sun Blaze's body was in tatters, countless cuts inflicted by Lu Ye.

It must be said, Sun Blaze's physique is remarkably powerful, especially as a member of the Insect Race. As Lu Ye advanced to Moon Jade, the Boulder Mountain Saber, elevated to the level of a magic treasure, was sharp enough, and Lu Ye enhanced it with Divine Sharp Edge Spirit Runes. Yet, even with each slash, it was difficult to cause any significant damage, merely leaving superficial wounds.

Now, these superficial wounds on Sun Blaze have become a heavy burden!

An entire day's brutal battle left the Insect Race Sun Blaze's face pale, his aura significantly diminished, seemingly at his wits' end.

Not only him, but other Moon Jade cultivators besides Lu Ye struggled as well.

Firstly, such a confrontation drains huge amounts of energy, requiring the Moon Jade cultivators to remain tense and fully utilize their Mana. To persist for so long was a testament to their extraordinary foundation.

Secondly, each suffered multiple Divine Soul Shocks from the Insect Race Sun Blaze, an impact they found insurmountable and incomprehensible.

After repeated shocks, all four Moon Jade Late Stage cultivators felt dizzy, unsettled, and their actions sluggish.

Under Lu Ye's orders, the four had retreated early from the Blood Sea battlefield to prevent the enemy from seizing an opportunity for a fatal strike.

Now, within the turbulent Blood Sea, only Lu Ye remained to fight alone.

The moment of truth was near!

After leaving another mark on the Insect Race Sun Blaze, Lu Ye's expression turned solemn. Reaching into the Void, he grabbed a slender bone saber in his left hand.

The bone saber came from an Insect Race he had slain, likely a descendant of a Praying Mantis that had used the Great Windmill Secret Technique against him, only for Lu Ye to perfectly counter and kill him, leaving the foe in confusion.

His pair of bone sabers became Lu Ye's spoils of war.

The bone saber was actually part of the Insect Race's body, refined over countless years, extremely hard and incredibly sharp, rivaling the finest magic treasures in quality, though slightly inferior to the current Boulder Mountain Saber level.

The Brazen Plundering Technique can only continuously weaken an Insect Race Sun Blaze but cannot execute a true kill.

The Drawn Saber Slash, Lu Ye could not use, as he had been refining Origin since the Black Abyss battle, neglecting to nurture the Drawn Saber Slash Spirit Runes.

Currently, his most ferocious secret technique was the Great Windmill.

He had once used it to cut down a Sun Blaze influenced by Dancing Girl, history seemed poised to repeat itself.

With a gentle breath, the boundless Blood Sea surged toward him, disappearing in an instant.

On Lu Ye's surface, blood Qi surged, thin red mist enveloping, rapidly pushing his blood Qi to the limit, with Mana humming inside his body.

Suddenly freed, the Insect Race Sun Blaze barely responded before weakly facing Lu Ye, with his expression turning grim.

He realized Lu Ye intended to make a killing strike.

Soon, however, his face showed curiosity as he saw a peculiar blood mark emerge between Lu Ye's eyebrows.

"Body Flower?" Insect Race Sun Blaze strained his eyes, doubting his vision.

As a Sun Blaze, his experience was substantial, having heard whispers of such cultivation mysteries, including the Body Flower.

The legend states that a cultivator pushing the Constellation Realm to the extreme would condense the Body Flower.

Yet, he only heard of this without witnessing such a phenomenon, unsure of its truth, considering many prominent Insect Race Constellation Realm members existed but none displayed such development.

He had assumed it a myth until witnessing it firsthand.

Suddenly understanding why this human cultivator was so formidable - genuinely reaching the pinnacle of the Constellation Realm, achieving a feat few dared contemplate.

Intense danger surged within, as the Insect Race Sun Blaze sensed death's embrace and, facing such peril, let out a furious roar, pouring all effort into activating a Psyche Secret Technique.

It was a long-held trump card, untouched until this desperate gamble.

Simultaneously, Divine Soul Power erupted from Lu Ye, his right eye transforming into a blood-red hue, within which intricate spirit runes unfolded, rendering the eye grotesque and fearsome.

Blood Eye emerges!

This is the second time Lu Ye has used the Blood Eye Spirit Runes since he obtained them, the first time was an experiment, allowing him to slightly understand the mysteries of the Blood Eye Spirit Runes.

In line with the Blood Eye he saw within the marvel, this Blood Eye Spirit Runes, when activated, has an obvious effect of illusion, both mysterious and powerful.

The Insect Race Sun Blaze before him is not the guy affected by the Dancing Girl's power, restricted in action.

Nor is he the Lih Tian besieged by many Moon Jade cultivators, looking for death.

Even though Lu Ye utilizes the power of the Core World to suppress him, and even though he appears extremely weak at the moment, facing such an enemy, Lu Ye dares not be careless the slightest bit.

Thus, he brought out all his skills, even pushing his own strength to the extreme.

The emergence of the Body Flower is the most obvious sign, representing that Lu Ye's blood Qi has been pushed to the limit.

The Insect Race Sun Blaze instinctively met that single Blood Eye, and for an instant, his expression was momentarily dazed, as if he saw a gigantic giant standing tall, gazing down at him with one eye.

And again, as if seeing a scarlet rising in the sky, bathed in moonlight, the entire world drenched in blood.

Ultimately, being a Sun Blaze, even though Lu Ye activated the Blood Eye Spirit Runes, the impact on him was only for that instant.

The next moment, all the illusions before the Insect Race Sun Blaze vanished completely, however, his expression changed drastically.

Because his meticulously prepared killer move was interfered with for that instant, showing signs of collapse, leading directly to an extremely adverse consequence—Divine Sea turmoil, Divine Soul Power in utter chaos.

Just like a magic cultivator preparing to cast a large magic spell, interrupted at the critical moment, the mana upheaval will surely backlash against himself, the Insect Race Sun Blaze's current experience is roughly similar.

He opened his mouth to cry out miserably, his face filled with an expression of pain, instinctively raising his hand to hold his head.

Seeing this, Lu Ye had no hesitation, brazenly charged forward, as the saber gleamed, the Boulder Mountain Saber had slashed down!

His body turned with the fall of the Boulder Mountain Saber, as one slash ended, the bone saber emerged.

The initial few slashes could still be traced, but after a few slashes, there was only a wild storm formed by a continuous gleam of saber light, enveloping a vast area.

In the distance, Yang Ling and others who had long retreated from the battlefield looked on in astonishment, even Xiang Yin and her sister were no exception.

Though in the contest with the Red Talisman Society, Lu Ye had already showcased strength beyond his cultivation, they truly hadn't expected that what they witnessed wasn't the full extent.

Perhaps this is the true display of Lu Ye's power!

That utterly terrifying killing intent, the fierce and violent offense, is not something a Moon Jade can withstand, Yang Ling, though considering himself a strong one among the Moon Jade, secretly imagined that if facing such an offense, he might not last over two breaths…

The saber light gradually retracted, Lu Ye stood in place, maintaining the posture of holding the saber with both hands, his blood Qi boiling to the extreme, the blood mist on his body rose upwards.

Centered around him, within about 30 miles, crisscrossing ravines of horrifying depth emerged.

The Insect Race Sun Blaze was nowhere to be seen, only chunks of shattered remains on the ground held traces of him once alive.

Despite having expectations in their hearts, witnessing this scene felt like being in a dream for Yang Ling and others.

Moon Jade defeating Sun Blaze… How absurd a notion, yet it happened right beneath their gaze.

Yang Ling felt that this scene before him might never be forgotten for the rest of his life.

The sound of cracking continued, Lu Ye staggered slightly, and in that moment, countless flesh and blood within him seemed to rupture.

He put away the Boulder Mountain Saber and the bone saber, sat down cross-legged, took out an elixir pill to consume, silently recovering, his expression neither happy nor sad.

This Insect Race Sun Blaze was not the first Sun Blaze to die by his hand, and in this battle, the opponent couldn't exert his full strength, so there's nothing to be happy about.

If someday he can truly kill a Sun Blaze with genuine skill, that's worth celebrating.

That day will come, and it won't be too far off.

Several days later, after recovering, Lu Ye exchanged a few words with Yang Ling and others who were still healing, and then leaped out of the Core World.

Then he took out his starboat, headed back along the path he came from.

He wanted to see how the battlefield situation over there was, assuming that by dealing with one Sun Blaze and destroying the insect hive, the pressure on the domain's human race cultivators should be greatly alleviated, but some things still need to be seen with his own eyes.

Before Lu Ye could reach the original battlefield, a group of cultivators flew over from that direction, hurriedly, Mental Consciousness spread all around, seemingly seeking something.



============================================================
Chapter 1812: Chapter 1812 1810: Life Origin
============================================================

The cultivators approaching from the front were not in perfect condition, looking like they had just been through a great battle, with numerous traces of disarray.

Upon spotting Lu Ye approaching head-on, the leading Moon Jade immediately came forward, cupping his fists from afar: "Lin Ran from Life Origin, greetings Fellow Daoist!"

Lin Ran had seen Lu Ye from afar. After all, a few days ago, when Lu Ye had steered the core onto that scorched battlefield, he was seated cross-legged on it without concealing his form, so many cultivators had seen his figure from afar.

For the Life Origin World, having one of the two Sun Blaze from the Insect Race removed, and the insect hive breached, undoubtedly helped immensely. Otherwise, the Life Origin World might already be in ruins, so even though he didn't know Lu Ye's background or identity, he showed a grateful expression upon seeing him, as it was indeed a lifesaving favor.

The cultivators following behind him also bowed in unison.

Lu Ye returned the salute: "Jade Conch, Lu Ye!"

He initially intended to investigate the situation of the battle over there, but upon seeing Lin Ran and the others, he understood there was no need. If the battle had not already ended, these people would not have been able to come here, and their demeanor clearly indicated they were looking for his whereabouts.

Life Origin should have won.

Though he had a guess in his heart, Lu Ye still asked.

As expected, Lin Ran informed him that the Insect Race had retreated.

The biggest reliance of the Insect Race was the two Sun Blaze and the insect hive. One Sun Blaze mysteriously disappeared, and the insect hive was shattered, instantly losing their advantage.

Many cultivators from the Life Origin World rose to resist, killing countless from the Insect Race.

The remaining Sun Blaze from the Insect Race, seeing the unfavorable situation, immediately retreated, probably also wary of Lu Ye's side, as the disappearance of his companion was too bizarre. Without finding out the whereabouts or even the life and death of his companion, he dared not linger outside the Life Origin World.

Though the Life Origin World won this battle and preserved the domain, the losses were significant. The Sun Blaze from their world was heavily injured and is currently recuperating within the domain.

"I was sent by Master Uncle Qin Jiang to investigate, Fellow Daoist Lu, that Sun Blaze from the Insect Race..." Lin Ran looked at Lu Ye. The Qin Jiang he mentioned was undoubtedly the Sun Blaze cultivator of the Life Origin World.

Lu Ye replied, "Fellow Daoist need not worry, that Sun Blaze from the Insect Race is already dead."

Lin Ran and the human race cultivators were overjoyed, hastening to ask, "May I ask which senior helped?"

It wasn't that he underestimated Lu Ye, but Lu Ye's Moon Jade mid-stage cultivation was evident, and the gap with Sun Blaze was too large, making it impossible for him to have such means.

Lu Ye also realized this issue, and after a brief ponder, replied, "My esteemed master personally took action and slew him." Not wanting to claim it as his kill, he just concocted a story.

Lin Ran showed an expression of understanding, looking behind Lu Ye and asked, "May I ask where your master is now..."

Lu Ye promptly replied, "My master fought with the enemy, got injured, and is recuperating, ordering me to check on the progress of your battle."

Lin Ran's expression tightened, and with concern, he asked, "Are the injuries severe?"

"Not too severe."

"If Fellow Daoist doesn't mind, may I invite your master to the Life Origin World to heal? Our world will offer the best healing resources, and additionally, Master Uncle Qin Jiang wants to express his thanks in person."

Lu Ye shook his head and said, "There's no need. My master is... rather reclusive and not accustomed to interacting with others. Since the battle in your domain has ended, my master and I will take our leave, Fellow Daoist, take care!"

Lu Ye cupped his fists, turning to leave.

Lin Ran hurriedly exclaimed, "Fellow Daoist, please wait! Such a great kindness is beyond repayment; no matter what, please allow us to do something, otherwise, we won't be able to explain to Master Uncle Qin Jiang when we return."

Lu Ye paused, turning to look at him, intending to refuse, but suddenly recalled something, and said, "If that's the case, would Fellow Daoist mind collecting some fire-type resources? My master has great use for them!" He had exhausted all the fire-type resources on him as well as the Talent Tree's fuel reserves, initially planning to replenish them later, but now there's an opportunity to get some for temporary use.

Moreover, although he consumed little in this battle, it actually consumed the essence of the Core World!

The power sealing the Sun Blaze from the Insect Race came from the Core World's essence, which was also why Lu Ye eventually used the Great Windmill Secret Technique, for sealing a Sun Blaze exhausted the Core World's essence significantly, and the earlier the opponent was dealt with, the sooner this consumption would cease.

Otherwise, Lu Ye could slowly wear down that Sun Blaze without taking risks.

Once a world's essence is exhausted, recovering it is very troublesome. At this moment, Lu Ye only sought some fire-type resources from the Life Origin World, a trifling matter compared to the consumption of the domain's essence.

Lin Ran's eyes brightened, quickly nodding, "Fellow Daoist, please wait a moment."

Saying this, he took out an audio talisman to send a message, giving some instructions.

He soon looked at Lu Ye again, "Within the domain, we will collect fire-type resources with full effort, and they will be delivered within half a day."

During the wait, Lin Ran chatted with Lu Ye, repeatedly proposing to visit the fictitious master to express thanks in person, all of which Lu Ye deftly deflected.

Lu Ye also thought of a problem: "Though the battle is won, if the Insect Race comes back, how will you respond?"

The Sun Blaze from the Insect Race wasn't dead but had escaped, and there's no guarantee they won't find another insect hive and lead it back to the Life Origin World side.

This could take a long time, but it's very likely to happen someday.

Lin Ran couldn't help but sigh: "There is really no good countermeasure, we can only strive for cultivation. Hopefully, by the time that day arrives, this domain will have enough power to protect itself."

Lu Ye remained silent. This time he was fortunate to be in the right place, lending a hand to the Life Origin World, saving them from peril, but next time they might not have such luck. Indeed, they must rely on their own efforts.

The Insect and Blood Races are the most notorious races in the stellar space. Comparatively, the harm from the Insect Race is somewhat greater than that from the Blood Race, due to the living methods of these two races.

The Blood Race owns several domains, all transformed from the remains of Blood Ancestors after their death, generally fixed locations. Even if the Blood Race does campaign outward, they only capture living beings to raise them, ensuring the supply of Blood Food.

However, the Insect Race is different. This race does not have a fixed place for cultivation; they typically base their existence on insect hives, drifting through stellar space. If they encounter any potential targets along the way, they would initiate a war.

Though, there are exceptions to everything. Sometimes, there are also Blood Race members within insect hives. Cooperation between the two races is not uncommon.

Half a day later, a cultivator hurriedly arrived from the direction of the Life Origin World, bringing several storage rings to Lin Ran.

Lin Ran briefly inspected them and then handed them over to Lu Ye.

"Fellow Daoist, can't you invite your Master to our Life Origin World for healing?" Lin Ran still wanted to make a final effort.

Lu Ye shook his head: "I appreciate your goodwill, Fellow Daoist. My master and I have no fixed place, wandering everywhere. As fellow humans, it is natural to lend a helping hand when our companions are in trouble. But going to your domain for healing is unnecessary now. My Master is already in a meditative trance, and it's not appropriate to disturb abruptly."

Lin Ran lamented deeply: "Your Master's righteousness is admirable! We at Life Origin will remember it deeply, and if we meet again someday, we'll certainly repay."

"Until we meet again." Lu Ye clasped his fists, picked up those rings, and swiftly departed.

Lin Ran and the others watched as he left.

Moments later, Lu Ye returned to the core location, sat atop it, and with a focused mind, maneuvered the core to continue the journey.

While traveling, he refined the fire-type resources obtained from the Life Origin World. Within days, he completely refined them.

Inspecting the Talent Tree, Lu Ye felt somewhat relieved. The lack of fuel in the Talent Tree made him uneasy, but now he could breathe a bit easier.

However, the fuel at hand was not sufficient. The treasure blood mixed within the Origin wasn't completely refined. This issue must be resolved later, but first, he needed to settle the core.

A storage ring appeared again in his hand. This was left by the deceased Insect Race Sun Blaze.

The legacy of a Sun Blaze was full of anticipation for Lu Ye, who devoted himself to deciphering the restriction lock on the storage ring.

After more than half a day, when the restriction lock on the ring was broken, Lu Ye's examination made his face turn dark!

Because the legacy within the ring was worlds apart from his expectations; there was hardly anything valuable inside, not even much spirit jade or spirit crystal!

Upon reflection, this wasn't surprising.

The survival mode of the Insect Race dictates that their warriors wouldn't have many resources on hand. The resources they acquire are mostly invested into the insect hives. Insect hives can convert all acquired resources into nourishment, with Insect Race's cultivation, healing, and growth happening within them.

This is somewhat similar to how he stores fuel within the Talent Tree, except the insect hives reserve nourishment made from resources acquired by the Insect Race.

Now, the massive accumulation of nourishment has also vanished with the destruction of the insect hives.

Lu Ye felt quite helpless.

Heading forward, the core finally reached its predetermined location.

In the Void, Lu Ye's Mental Consciousness surged, utilizing the seven-color Divine Lotus within the Divine Sea to connect with the Soul Race ancestral land. As time passed, the vague connection grew increasingly stronger.

Until one moment, a portal suddenly opened in the void ahead.

Lu Ye maneuvered the core and rushed in through the portal.

After a whirlwind-like rotation, familiar scenery unfolded before his eyes once again.

The Soul Race ancestral land, arrived!

Simultaneously, at the eastern Mount Fangcun, Immortal Spirit Peak, Su Yuqing, who was cultivating with closed eyes, suddenly opened her eyes, revealing a puzzled expression.

Because just at that instant, she suddenly felt a strange anomaly, which she had never sensed before.

Not just her, on Misty Peak, Woo Qimo, who was watching the clouds roll by, also showed a look of suspicion and surprise simultaneously.

On Cloud Sea Peak, Chen Xuanhai stood with hands behind his back, suddenly raised his head to look at the sky, his eyebrows lifted. After a brief hesitation, he suddenly soared into the sky.

Feeling Chen Xuanhai's movement, Su Yuqing and Woo Qimo also flickered and rushed out toward the sky.

The three Sun Blaze cultivators had already developed a hypothesis, but to confirm whether this hypothesis was true, they had to see for themselves.

Even for such mighty figures as them, their expressions were filled with excitement and anticipation, for if the hypothesis were true, it would be a joyous event awaited by the Dwarf Race for countless years!

In the Void, Lu Ye's Mental Consciousness surged, utilizing the seven-color Divine Lotus within the Divine Sea to connect with the Soul Race ancestral land. As time passed, the vague connection grew increasingly stronger.

Until one moment, a portal suddenly opened in the void ahead.

Lu Ye maneuvered the core and rushed in through the portal.

After a whirlwind-like rotation, familiar scenery unfolded before his eyes once again.

The Soul Race ancestral land, arrived!

Simultaneously, at the eastern Mount Fangcun, Immortal Spirit Peak, Su Yuqing, who was cultivating with closed eyes, suddenly opened her eyes, revealing a puzzled expression.

Because just at that instant, she suddenly felt a strange anomaly, which she had never sensed before.

Not just her, on Misty Peak, Woo Qimo, who was watching the clouds roll by, also showed a look of suspicion and surprise simultaneously.

On Cloud Sea Peak, Chen Xuanhai stood with hands behind his back, suddenly raised his head to look at the sky, his eyebrows lifted. After a brief hesitation, he suddenly soared into the sky.

Feeling Chen Xuanhai's movement, Su Yuqing and Woo Qimo also flickered and rushed out toward the sky.

The three Sun Blaze cultivators had already developed a hypothesis, but to confirm whether this hypothesis was true, they had to see for themselves.

Even for such mighty figures as them, their expressions were filled with excitement and anticipation, for if the hypothesis were true, it would be a joyous event awaited by the Dwarf Race for countless years!



============================================================
Chapter 1812: Chapter 1812 1810: Life Origin
============================================================

The cultivators approaching from the front were not in perfect condition, looking like they had just been through a great battle, with numerous traces of disarray.

Upon spotting Lu Ye approaching head-on, the leading Moon Jade immediately came forward, cupping his fists from afar: "Lin Ran from Life Origin, greetings Fellow Daoist!"

Lin Ran had seen Lu Ye from afar. After all, a few days ago, when Lu Ye had steered the core onto that scorched battlefield, he was seated cross-legged on it without concealing his form, so many cultivators had seen his figure from afar.

For the Life Origin World, having one of the two Sun Blaze from the Insect Race removed, and the insect hive breached, undoubtedly helped immensely. Otherwise, the Life Origin World might already be in ruins, so even though he didn't know Lu Ye's background or identity, he showed a grateful expression upon seeing him, as it was indeed a lifesaving favor.

The cultivators following behind him also bowed in unison.

Lu Ye returned the salute: "Jade Conch, Lu Ye!"

He initially intended to investigate the situation of the battle over there, but upon seeing Lin Ran and the others, he understood there was no need. If the battle had not already ended, these people would not have been able to come here, and their demeanor clearly indicated they were looking for his whereabouts.

Life Origin should have won.

Though he had a guess in his heart, Lu Ye still asked.

As expected, Lin Ran informed him that the Insect Race had retreated.

The biggest reliance of the Insect Race was the two Sun Blaze and the insect hive. One Sun Blaze mysteriously disappeared, and the insect hive was shattered, instantly losing their advantage.

Many cultivators from the Life Origin World rose to resist, killing countless from the Insect Race.

The remaining Sun Blaze from the Insect Race, seeing the unfavorable situation, immediately retreated, probably also wary of Lu Ye's side, as the disappearance of his companion was too bizarre. Without finding out the whereabouts or even the life and death of his companion, he dared not linger outside the Life Origin World.

Though the Life Origin World won this battle and preserved the domain, the losses were significant. The Sun Blaze from their world was heavily injured and is currently recuperating within the domain.

"I was sent by Master Uncle Qin Jiang to investigate, Fellow Daoist Lu, that Sun Blaze from the Insect Race..." Lin Ran looked at Lu Ye. The Qin Jiang he mentioned was undoubtedly the Sun Blaze cultivator of the Life Origin World.

Lu Ye replied, "Fellow Daoist need not worry, that Sun Blaze from the Insect Race is already dead."

Lin Ran and the human race cultivators were overjoyed, hastening to ask, "May I ask which senior helped?"

It wasn't that he underestimated Lu Ye, but Lu Ye's Moon Jade mid-stage cultivation was evident, and the gap with Sun Blaze was too large, making it impossible for him to have such means.

Lu Ye also realized this issue, and after a brief ponder, replied, "My esteemed master personally took action and slew him." Not wanting to claim it as his kill, he just concocted a story.

Lin Ran showed an expression of understanding, looking behind Lu Ye and asked, "May I ask where your master is now..."

Lu Ye promptly replied, "My master fought with the enemy, got injured, and is recuperating, ordering me to check on the progress of your battle."

Lin Ran's expression tightened, and with concern, he asked, "Are the injuries severe?"

"Not too severe."

"If Fellow Daoist doesn't mind, may I invite your master to the Life Origin World to heal? Our world will offer the best healing resources, and additionally, Master Uncle Qin Jiang wants to express his thanks in person."

Lu Ye shook his head and said, "There's no need. My master is... rather reclusive and not accustomed to interacting with others. Since the battle in your domain has ended, my master and I will take our leave, Fellow Daoist, take care!"

Lu Ye cupped his fists, turning to leave.

Lin Ran hurriedly exclaimed, "Fellow Daoist, please wait! Such a great kindness is beyond repayment; no matter what, please allow us to do something, otherwise, we won't be able to explain to Master Uncle Qin Jiang when we return."

Lu Ye paused, turning to look at him, intending to refuse, but suddenly recalled something, and said, "If that's the case, would Fellow Daoist mind collecting some fire-type resources? My master has great use for them!" He had exhausted all the fire-type resources on him as well as the Talent Tree's fuel reserves, initially planning to replenish them later, but now there's an opportunity to get some for temporary use.

Moreover, although he consumed little in this battle, it actually consumed the essence of the Core World!

The power sealing the Sun Blaze from the Insect Race came from the Core World's essence, which was also why Lu Ye eventually used the Great Windmill Secret Technique, for sealing a Sun Blaze exhausted the Core World's essence significantly, and the earlier the opponent was dealt with, the sooner this consumption would cease.

Otherwise, Lu Ye could slowly wear down that Sun Blaze without taking risks.

Once a world's essence is exhausted, recovering it is very troublesome. At this moment, Lu Ye only sought some fire-type resources from the Life Origin World, a trifling matter compared to the consumption of the domain's essence.

Lin Ran's eyes brightened, quickly nodding, "Fellow Daoist, please wait a moment."

Saying this, he took out an audio talisman to send a message, giving some instructions.

He soon looked at Lu Ye again, "Within the domain, we will collect fire-type resources with full effort, and they will be delivered within half a day."

During the wait, Lin Ran chatted with Lu Ye, repeatedly proposing to visit the fictitious master to express thanks in person, all of which Lu Ye deftly deflected.

Lu Ye also thought of a problem: "Though the battle is won, if the Insect Race comes back, how will you respond?"

The Sun Blaze from the Insect Race wasn't dead but had escaped, and there's no guarantee they won't find another insect hive and lead it back to the Life Origin World side.

This could take a long time, but it's very likely to happen someday.

Lin Ran couldn't help but sigh: "There is really no good countermeasure, we can only strive for cultivation. Hopefully, by the time that day arrives, this domain will have enough power to protect itself."

Lu Ye remained silent. This time he was fortunate to be in the right place, lending a hand to the Life Origin World, saving them from peril, but next time they might not have such luck. Indeed, they must rely on their own efforts.

The Insect and Blood Races are the most notorious races in the stellar space. Comparatively, the harm from the Insect Race is somewhat greater than that from the Blood Race, due to the living methods of these two races.

The Blood Race owns several domains, all transformed from the remains of Blood Ancestors after their death, generally fixed locations. Even if the Blood Race does campaign outward, they only capture living beings to raise them, ensuring the supply of Blood Food.

However, the Insect Race is different. This race does not have a fixed place for cultivation; they typically base their existence on insect hives, drifting through stellar space. If they encounter any potential targets along the way, they would initiate a war.

Though, there are exceptions to everything. Sometimes, there are also Blood Race members within insect hives. Cooperation between the two races is not uncommon.

Half a day later, a cultivator hurriedly arrived from the direction of the Life Origin World, bringing several storage rings to Lin Ran.

Lin Ran briefly inspected them and then handed them over to Lu Ye.

"Fellow Daoist, can't you invite your Master to our Life Origin World for healing?" Lin Ran still wanted to make a final effort.

Lu Ye shook his head: "I appreciate your goodwill, Fellow Daoist. My master and I have no fixed place, wandering everywhere. As fellow humans, it is natural to lend a helping hand when our companions are in trouble. But going to your domain for healing is unnecessary now. My Master is already in a meditative trance, and it's not appropriate to disturb abruptly."

Lin Ran lamented deeply: "Your Master's righteousness is admirable! We at Life Origin will remember it deeply, and if we meet again someday, we'll certainly repay."

"Until we meet again." Lu Ye clasped his fists, picked up those rings, and swiftly departed.

Lin Ran and the others watched as he left.

Moments later, Lu Ye returned to the core location, sat atop it, and with a focused mind, maneuvered the core to continue the journey.

While traveling, he refined the fire-type resources obtained from the Life Origin World. Within days, he completely refined them.

Inspecting the Talent Tree, Lu Ye felt somewhat relieved. The lack of fuel in the Talent Tree made him uneasy, but now he could breathe a bit easier.

However, the fuel at hand was not sufficient. The treasure blood mixed within the Origin wasn't completely refined. This issue must be resolved later, but first, he needed to settle the core.

A storage ring appeared again in his hand. This was left by the deceased Insect Race Sun Blaze.

The legacy of a Sun Blaze was full of anticipation for Lu Ye, who devoted himself to deciphering the restriction lock on the storage ring.

After more than half a day, when the restriction lock on the ring was broken, Lu Ye's examination made his face turn dark!

Because the legacy within the ring was worlds apart from his expectations; there was hardly anything valuable inside, not even much spirit jade or spirit crystal!

Upon reflection, this wasn't surprising.

The survival mode of the Insect Race dictates that their warriors wouldn't have many resources on hand. The resources they acquire are mostly invested into the insect hives. Insect hives can convert all acquired resources into nourishment, with Insect Race's cultivation, healing, and growth happening within them.

This is somewhat similar to how he stores fuel within the Talent Tree, except the insect hives reserve nourishment made from resources acquired by the Insect Race.

Now, the massive accumulation of nourishment has also vanished with the destruction of the insect hives.

Lu Ye felt quite helpless.

Heading forward, the core finally reached its predetermined location.

In the Void, Lu Ye's Mental Consciousness surged, utilizing the seven-color Divine Lotus within the Divine Sea to connect with the Soul Race ancestral land. As time passed, the vague connection grew increasingly stronger.

Until one moment, a portal suddenly opened in the void ahead.

Lu Ye maneuvered the core and rushed in through the portal.

After a whirlwind-like rotation, familiar scenery unfolded before his eyes once again.

The Soul Race ancestral land, arrived!

Simultaneously, at the eastern Mount Fangcun, Immortal Spirit Peak, Su Yuqing, who was cultivating with closed eyes, suddenly opened her eyes, revealing a puzzled expression.

Because just at that instant, she suddenly felt a strange anomaly, which she had never sensed before.

Not just her, on Misty Peak, Woo Qimo, who was watching the clouds roll by, also showed a look of suspicion and surprise simultaneously.

On Cloud Sea Peak, Chen Xuanhai stood with hands behind his back, suddenly raised his head to look at the sky, his eyebrows lifted. After a brief hesitation, he suddenly soared into the sky.

Feeling Chen Xuanhai's movement, Su Yuqing and Woo Qimo also flickered and rushed out toward the sky.

The three Sun Blaze cultivators had already developed a hypothesis, but to confirm whether this hypothesis was true, they had to see for themselves.

Even for such mighty figures as them, their expressions were filled with excitement and anticipation, for if the hypothesis were true, it would be a joyous event awaited by the Dwarf Race for countless years!



============================================================
Chapter 1813: Chapter 1813 - 1811: Stopped!
============================================================

On the way rushing out to the sky, the three Sun Blaze from the Eastern Fangcun Mountain met at one place. They looked at each other and saw what each had in mind.

A moment later, the three flew out of Fangcun Mountain and entered the stellar space.

Turning back to look, Woo Qimo’s pupils shrank, exclaiming: "It stopped!"

Su Yuqing frowned, and Chen Xuanhai’s expression turned heavy.

The three of them had just noticed some anomalies in the main Fangcun Mountain. They initially guessed that some changes at the core triggered it, so they were full of anticipation, but when they came out and saw, it seemed not to be the case.

"What does this mean?" Woo Qimo pondered hard, unable to make sense of the sight before him as it differed from his expectations.

Since the Blood Ancestor broke open Fangcun Mountain, splitting it into three parts and losing the core, the three Fangcun Mountains have been performing what seemed like irregular, yet intricately hidden displacement, based on the core’s location.

This is precisely why the Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race could deduce the core’s hidden location and have persisted in their efforts to find the core over the years. They’ve even dispatched numerous carefully nurtured Foreign Clan Moon Jade to that marvel.

In the Sun Blaze’s vision, if anyone could bring the core out from that marvel, then the split Fangcun Mountains would immediately start moving towards the core and eventually integrate at one spot.

All these years, Fangcun Mountain suddenly exhibited anomalous activity, making them believe it had succeeded.

But what they see before them seems otherwise.

Because if someone truly brought the core out from the marvel, the main Fangcun Mountain wouldn’t have suddenly stopped at its original position. Instead, it should have turned direction to fly towards the core’s location.

This is precisely what Woo Qimo couldn’t comprehend.

Soon after, a chilling thought crossed his mind: "The two of you, could it be that the core... is destroyed?"

It is possible to manually control Fangcun Mountain to stop. Previously the Western Fangcun Mountain stayed over the All Phenomena Ocean for two months, but this duration wouldn’t be too long; otherwise, it would impact Fangcun Mountain’s subsequent displacement path.

Now, none of the three Sun Blaze are manually controlling the main Fangcun Mountain to stop, yet it suddenly halted here. This information inevitably leads to endless speculation.

A possible reason could be that the core was destroyed, hence the Eastern side stopped.

Chen Xuanhai shook his head and said: "Although Fangcun Mountain has split, if the core were destroyed, all three parts would be in turmoil; now the East is peaceful, so the core should be unharmed."

Su Yuqing nodded unambiguously, agreeing with Chen Xuanhai’s viewpoint.

"Then what is going on?" Woo Qimo scratched his head, never in his life having encountered such a bizarre event.

Su Yuqing’s eyes flashed, saying: "There’s another possibility!"

Chen Xuanhai turned to look at her.

"Based on our analysis, the reason the three Fangcun Mountain parts cannot integrate with the core is because of an isolation force within that marvel, obstructing their integration, and if that isolation force suddenly magnified significantly, completely severing the core’s connection with the main part..."

Then such a scenario might indeed occur, because the main part moves based on the core’s location. The core so thoroughly isolated, losing that foundation, the main Fangcun Mountain stopped dead in its tracks.

"Change in the marvel!" Chen Xuanhai furrowed his brow deeper, as, if true, it’s not good news for the Dwarf Race, since the core is within the marvel, and who knows if this change is good or bad for the core?

"Isn’t Lu Yiye there for three years now?" Woo Qimo suddenly looked at Su Yuqing, "Do you think this change has anything to do with him?"

No one could answer this because the Dwarf Race over here has no way to contact Lu Ye. When Zhang Kun of the Western region sent Lu Ye near the marvel, he then left.

Given the uncertainty about whether Lu Ye would gain anything from this journey, and not knowing how many years he’d linger in the marvel, Zhang Kun could hardly wait for him all along.

Su Yuqing was silent for a moment, then suddenly turned to look at Chen Xuanhai: "Senior Brother Chen, I want to go have a look." She ultimately felt uneasy, regretting talking to Lu Ye about the core originally, not expecting that Lu Ye would act quickly upon hearing it, and immediately searched for it afterward.

Chen Xuanhai could somewhat understand Su Yuqing’s feelings and didn’t dissuade her but said: "Junior Sister, if you truly wish to go there, it’s not urgent. Nobody knows why this sudden change happened, and subsequent developments are unpredictable. Better wait a while longer, and observe the situation; maybe some new discoveries can be made... if nothing changes, going later wouldn’t be too late."

Saying this made sense. Su Yuqing suppressed her inner unease and gently nodded.
