Chen Xuanhai raised his hand and said: "Let’s go back. There are changes here; likely, there are changes in the other two parts as well. Discuss with those old fellows before deciding."

The three Sun Blaze returned to the domain.

After another half day, within an illusionary hall, one illusory figure after another appeared—all Sun Blaze powerhouses of Fangcun Mountain’s psyche projection here.

Although the three parts have split, they still maintain exceedingly tight contact. At some cost, they can even allow transit among the parts.

Projecting Mental Consciousness here to discuss clan affairs in this manner is certainly not difficult. Compared to gathering physically in one location, this method costs significantly less.

The gathering of the three parts’ Sun Blaze happened just as Chen Xuanhai had anticipated. Not only did the Eastern Fangcun Mountain stop moving at that moment, but similar occurrences also happened in the Southern and Western parts.

However, no one knows the exact reason, and ultimately, it was summarized in one sentence—the core was completely isolated, which caused the anomaly of the three departments on Mount Fangcun!

When the three Sun Blaze convened for discussion, in the Soul Race ancestral land, Lu Ye rode the core to arrive at a five-color Lotus Land, where he saw figures moving around in the Lotus Land, many of whom seemed familiar.

These figures were the Xianyuan Guards of Xianyuan City from back then.

Lu Ye also saw a white big tiger, lying somewhere on the Lotus Land, fast asleep. Several figures gathered around it with solemn and devout expressions, unknown to what secret technique they were practicing.

A faint resonance of Soul Power emanated from the big tiger and those figures.

The sleeping big tiger seemed to sense something and suddenly opened its amber-colored tiger eyes, looking towards Lu Ye.

Immediately after, it got up quickly and dashed towards Lu Ye with playful excitement, leaping high and transforming into the size of a cat in mid-air.

Lu Ye smiled, caught it in his hand, and began to rub it. Amber squinted its eyes, letting out a contented purring sound.

After playing for a while, Lu Ye finally asked, "Where is Yiyi?"

Just as he finished asking, a portal appeared somewhere on the Lotus Land, and Yiyi’s little head popped out, evidently sensing something.

"Lu Ye!" Yiyi exclaimed joyfully, just like Amber did earlier, she rushed towards Lu Ye, directly colliding with him, wrapped her arms around his neck, and buried her head in his chest.

With one hand holding Amber, Lu Ye wrapped the other around her waist, spinning several times before slowly stopping.

They lingered for a long time; Yiyi didn’t want to let go.

Until the voice of Lih Shang rang out, "Fellow Daoist Lu!"

Lu Ye responded with a smile, "Fellow Daoist Lih Shang, long time no see!"

A moment later, at Yiyi’s residence, Lu Ye wandered around with hands behind his back, examining his surroundings. The Lotus Land is quite a peculiar place, appearing from the outside as an enormous blooming lotus flower, and it’s also the dwelling of the Soul Race.

The Lotus Lands in the Soul Race ancestral land are classified in tiers; the tier depends on the colors. The places where the Sun Blaze strong reside are the seven-color Lotus Lands, whereas the Moon Jade usually stays in the five-color ones.

Back when Lih Shang was just a Constellation, she was eligible to choose a five-color Lotus Land, and that was because she had rendered great service to the Soul Race by bringing back the Sacred Beast.

There is nowhere on the surface of the Lotus Land suitable for living, but as the Soul Race does not have physical bodies, they only need to develop the environment they require within the Lotus Land.

The place where Yiyi resides now is undoubtedly self-developed, and the interior setup is no different from the arrangement inside the Emerald Bamboo Peak Bamboo Pagoda of Righteous Blood Sect.

Yiyi sat beside, hugging the cat-sized Amber, tilted her head looking at him, her little legs swinging, her eyes full of happiness.

Lu Ye sat down next to her, patted her head, "Is cultivation hard for you?"

Yiyi shook her head, "Not hard at all, Amber accompanies me."

Lu Ye glimpsed at Amber, "It only knows how to sleep, how can it accompany you?"

Amber immediately let out a cry, indicating that sleeping itself is cultivation, and it is now much mightier than before!

"Alright, I know you’ve become stronger!" Lu Ye nodded Amber’s little head.

It must be said, throughout these years in the Soul Race, Amber and Yiyi have grown significantly. Under Lu Ye’s perception, both the spirit and the beast weren’t far from becoming Moon Jade.

This is undoubtedly related to the unique cultivation environment of the Soul Race ancestral land. In such a place, the Soul Race cultivators have an inherent advantage; even if not trying too hard, their cultivation can gradually increase.

"Earlier I saw several Soul Race cultivators surrounding Amber. What were they doing?" Lu Ye asked.

Yiyi immediately explained, "Amber recently accepted several attendants. Those Soul Race cultivators you saw are meticulously selected here, with the most outstanding aptitude. They established a commensal relationship with Amber, allowing them to cultivate and grow together, just like me."

Lu Ye finally understood, recalling the resonance waves felt earlier from those Soul Race cultivators and Amber, confirming Yiyi’s explanation.

"Did Amber consent willingly or was it requested by the Soul Race?" Lu Ye inquired.

Yiyi replied, "The Clan Leader personally came to speak, there wasn’t any demand. Amber agreed itself because the more attendants it has, the faster its strength grows, correspondingly, my strength can also grow alongside."

Lu Ye nodded.

Yiyi saw his concern, smiled, and said, "Don’t worry, the Soul Race holds Amber in high regard, and certainly wouldn’t force it to do anything it dislikes."

"That’s good, but keep in mind, if you ever feel unhappy here, tell me anytime, and I’ll take you away." Lu Ye seriously advised.

Back when Yiyi wanted to follow Lih Shang to the Soul Race ancestral land for cultivation, Lu Ye indeed felt a bit reluctant, but children grow up and having their own opinions is not a bad thing. Most importantly, Lu Ye understood he didn’t have much time to accompany Yiyi under his own circumstances.



============================================================
Chapter 1814: Chapter 1814 - 1812: Social Skills
============================================================

After staying for several days on Lih Shang’s Lotus Land, Lu Ye departed.

Yiyi and Amber watched him go, no longer feeling the sadness of the last farewell, as their mood had changed.

During the last farewell, Yiyi always felt that she might not see Lu Ye for a very long time, which naturally made her reluctant. But now she knew that Lu Ye could come and go to the Soul Race ancestral land, so there would be many opportunities to meet in the future.

Before parting, Yiyi gave Lu Ye thousands of soul jades, all meticulously refined by her during her cultivation time.

Lu Ye did not refuse, accepting them gladly. These soul jades are hard to find in the outside world because the environment suitable for their birth is rare, but here at the Soul Race ancestral land, they are easily acquired due to the abundance of pure Soul Power.

Typically, tribal members of the Soul Race wouldn’t refine soul jades because they can directly refine Soul Power for cultivation. Spending time and effort on refining soul jades would only be a waste of time.

These soul jades from Yiyi were undoubtedly specially prepared for Lu Ye, perhaps with a contribution from Lih Shang.

In front of the seven-color Lotus Land where the stellar space pond is located, Lu Ye had just arrived, riding the core, and from a distance, he saw Elder Xuyuan.

Elder Xuyuan had actually detected Lu Ye as soon as he entered the Soul Race ancestral land, but since Lu Ye first visited Lih Shang’s Lotus Land, Xuyuan did not interrupt but waited here all along.

"Elder!" Lu Ye jumped down from the core, greeting with respect.

Xuyuan nodded slightly, approached with interest, and scrutinized the core, appearing uncertain and curious. After a long while, Xuyuan finally asked, "Boy, is this a miniature world?"

Yet it seemed somewhat different from the miniature worlds he knew. To call it a miniature world seemed inaccurate because it is quite large; typically, so-called miniature worlds can be carried along, like the Small Flower World that Lu Ye possesses, which can be considered a miniature world.

Moreover, there were treasures when Ban Ci housed Ban Xia back then, also considered a miniature world.

But Xuyuan had never seen such a large miniature world, and its design was rather peculiar.

Facing Xuyuan, Lu Ye didn’t conceal the truth, candidly saying, "It’s not wrong to call it a miniature world, but it’s different from ordinary miniature worlds. It’s the core of Mount Fangcun."

Xuyuan suddenly whipped his head toward Lu Ye, shocked, "Mount Fangcun? The Dwarf Race’s Mount Fangcun?"

"Exactly!" Lu Ye nodded.

Xuyuan’s interest grew stronger as he surveyed the core nonstop, soon saying, "Back then, the Blood Ancestor intended to capture Mount Fangcun and led a strong force of the Blood Race to attack fiercely. A great battle ensued, resulting in mutual destruction. Mount Fangcun was shattered and divided into three parts with its core lost and whereabouts unknown. Where did you find it, boy?"

Lu Ye explained, "Actually, the Dwarf Race always knew the location of the core and worked hard over the years to retrieve it. But due to several reasons, they could not succeed, so I took on the task at the request of Sun Blaze from the Dwarf Race and eventually gained results."

"You have a good relationship with the Dwarf Race?" Xuyuan looked at him, stunned. Giving such an important task of searching for the core to an outsider indicates that their relationship is undoubtedly close.

"Quite good." Lu Ye touched his nose, hesitating to say his Dao companion relationship with Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race, which would be rather startling.

Xuyuan looked at him and chuckled, "You sure have a knack for networking."

Lu Ye could be considered half a member of the Soul Race, and now he was closely connected with the Dwarf Race as well. Yet both the Soul Race and Dwarf Race aren’t easy to engage with, especially the Soul Race; most people don’t even know where their ancestral land is, let alone find it.

Lu Ye pondered for a moment; he seemed to have good diplomatic ties with several races. Setting aside the Soul Race and Dwarf Race, he also had the merfolk of the All Phenomena Ocean, the most solid allies of Three Worlds Island, and now the Flower Race settled in the Nine Provinces...

"Treat others with sincerity, and naturally, they will treat me sincerely."

Xuyuan nodded, agreeing with his words.

"Elder, have you ever seen the Blood Ancestor?" Lu Ye asked.

Xuyuan shook his head, replying, "Never seen. The Blood Ancestor was active long ago, before my time, and you know our Soul Race’s circumstances; we generally don’t interact with the outside world much."

"Why did the Blood Ancestor target the Dwarf Race?"

Xuyuan waved his hand, saying, "You’re mistaken. The Blood Ancestor didn’t target the Dwarf Race; she wanted Mount Fangcun. The Dwarf Race was affected because they were born of Mount Fangcun. I’ve heard that during that era, the Insect Race also fell under her control. You should understand the Insect Race’s plundering style: the hives often drift about, seeking targets to invade. But hives are more fragile; if targeted by a powerful force, they can easily be destroyed. However, if the hives were to be placed inside Mount Fangcun?"

Lu Ye suddenly realized.

The Insect Race combined with Mount Fangcun would be a flawless partnership. Imagine the Insect Race commanding Mount Fangcun, such a stellar space supreme treasure, wandering through stellar space... If the Blood Ancestor truly seized Mount Fangcun back then, the harm the Insect Race could cause would be far greater than today.

Moreover, Lu Ye finally understood the fundamental reason for the good relationship between the Insect and Blood Races; it turns out both had served under the Blood Ancestor’s command in the past.

In this light, the war over Mount Fangcun likely involved not just the Blood Race, but the Insect Race too.

"How did the Blood Ancestor die?" Lu Ye asked again, curious. To nurture a race was indicative of her strength, and according to Lu Ye’s speculation, the Blood Ancestor’s prowess couldn’t be as simple as Sun Blaze. How could such a formidable being get defeated? And even dismembered.

Xuyuan shook his head: "I don’t know how the Blood Ancestor died, but kid, the world is not as simple as you see it. Some things can only be slowly uncovered when you have sufficiently strong power. For a cultivator, weakness is the greatest original sin."

After chatting with Xuyuan for a while, Lu Ye drove the core to the stellar space pond.

"Elder, can I pass through the passage with the core?" Lu Ye asked. He had always been traveling alone before, and although the core was not very large, it was a dozen or so feet long. He wasn’t sure if he could bring the core through the passage to return to the Jade Conch Galaxy.

If not, it would be a big trouble. At that time, he would have to choose to leave the core in the Soul Race ancestral land and then find a way to notify the Dwarf Race to take the core themselves.

"It’s not a big problem." Xuyuan said calmly, "You just need to wrap the core with power during transit."

Lu Ye understood and immediately began to locate the position of Jade Conch in the stellar space pond.

He had traveled to and from Jade Conch several times using the stellar space pond, so he was naturally skillful and quickly gained results.

"Then, Elder, I’m going." After saying a word to Xuyuan, Lu Ye wrapped the core with power and plunged into the stellar space pond.

The scene of an entire stellar space shrinking countless times and rushing toward him was shockingly spectacular no matter how many times he saw it. The stellar region belonging to Jade Conch in his field of vision continued to enlarge, enlarge, and enlarge again...

When Lu Ye regained his senses, he had arrived at Jade Conch.

After slightly discerning the direction, Lu Ye controlled the core and headed towards the Nine Provinces.

On the Eastern Mount Fangcun, due to previous incidents, the three big Sun Blazes did not engage in cultivation but constantly sensed the movements of the main part, anticipating some changes to occur.

Unfortunately, the main part of Mount Fangcun had been stationary somewhere in the stellar space and showed no signs of movement. Until this moment, it finally started to move.

What shocked Su Yuqing and the others was that the movement trajectory of Mount Fangcun suddenly changed significantly.

The three immediately gathered together and, after a simple discussion, concluded that the position of the core had shifted dramatically.

This is why the movement trajectory of the main Mount Fangcun changed.

First, the core was completely isolated by some mysterious power, causing the three Mount Fangcun to stop drifting. Then, within a few days, the core’s position changed dramatically. All these strange occurrences left people puzzled, and no one knew what happened.

Yet, despite this, the Sun Blazes of the Dwarf Race were extremely excited and hopeful.

Because if the core’s position changed significantly, it would likely mean the core had already escaped the Illusory Blood Devil’s Eye marvel.

This change is undoubtedly a good omen!

As for the current exact position of the core, it was unknown on the Mount Fangcun side. They had to observe for decades or even centuries according to the drifting trajectory of the three Mount Fangcun and then calculate comprehensively to determine the result.

This was not something that could be solved quickly, so the three Sun Blazes gathered again to discuss the significant matter of deducing the core’s position.

At this time, on the core, not only was Lu Ye present, but also Xiang Yin and sister, Yang Ling, and Hu Dequan were there.

Looking far ahead at the domain, Xiang Yin exclaimed with excitement, "Venerable Lord, is that your domain?"

"The domain where I was born, not my domain." Lu Ye replied.

Previously, Xiang Yin and the others had always been in the Core World. Now that they were nearing Nine Provinces, it would naturally not be appropriate to keep them inside.

Settling them wasn’t difficult. Xiang Yin and sister were his Blood Servants, and under Lu Ye’s command, they didn’t dare to disobey. For now, letting them stay in the Nine Provinces would suffice.

As for Yang Ling and Hu Dequan, they could also stay in the Nine Provinces, waiting for the three Mount Fangcun to merge, and on that day, they could be reunited with their Dao companions.

Moreover, all four of them were in the Moon Jade Late Stage and had considerable strength. Staying in the Nine Provinces would also enable them to protect it.

Many dangers in stellar space were sudden, like the previous invasion by the Filth Race, or encountering an insect hive invasion on the way...

The reason Nine Provinces had been safe for so many years was, one, due to Number Nine’s concealing ability, and two, the remoteness of Jade Conch.

But nothing is absolute, and some precautions are necessary.

Waiting for the local cultivator of Nine Provinces to grow takes too long. During this period, any unforeseen event could be unbearable for Nine Provinces.

Therefore, Lu Ye came up with the idea of using the Dwarf Race as a reliance. Now that he brought back the core of Mount Fangcun, given time, the fused Mount Fangcun would become the strongest backing for Nine Provinces, without fear of any external invasion.

In just a few days, they reached the outer regions of Nine Provinces.



============================================================
Chapter 1815: Chapter 1815 - 1813: Monumental Merit
============================================================

At the core, Lu Ye sighed.

In the past, by this time, Number Nine would have already contacted him, but this time upon returning, there was no message from Number Nine.

He didn’t think Number Nine had encountered any accident. If something had happened to Number Nine, the Nine Provinces would surely be in chaos.

Number Nine is probably indulged in the company of Little Flower Girl now...

But this is a good thing, at least Number Nine won’t be lonely anymore.

Soon, they were beside the Nine Provinces. As always, Lu Ye’s whereabouts were instantly detected by the Nine Provinces Constellation responsible for patrolling nearby. Upon seeing it was Lu Ye, they immediately lowered their guard and continued their patrol after greeting him.

Initially, when Lu Ye returned from the All Phenomena Ocean, the Constellations of the Nine Provinces were incredibly excited and expectant. However, as he left and returned more frequently, they all became accustomed to it.

For Constellations like them, cultivating and becoming stronger is always the primary task. Since the Nine Provinces don’t have their own Spirit Jade Vein, they can only delve deeper into the stellar space to search for spirit jade, refine a certain amount of it, and use it as nourishment for their growth.

The core stops, observes from afar, and is not unusual. In fact, if an uninformed cultivator were to encounter the core in stellar space, they wouldn’t give it a second glance because such things are so common in stellar space.

But this is the core of Mount Fangcun. The Dwarf Race of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun have been striving for countless years to recover this core, and today, the dust has settled.

Looking down at the core beneath his feet, Lu Ye’s mind stirred, and he gently stomped his foot.

The core trembled slightly, and a mystical force spread out, as if some restriction was being broken.

Indeed, it was a restriction being broken. Before Lu Ye took the core out of the marvel of the Illusory Blood Devil’s Eye, he had imposed a restriction using his status as the Origin Lord.

The function of this restriction is singular, which is to generate an isolating force similar to the marvel, preventing the three divisions of Mount Fangcun from merging with the core.

The reason for doing so was because of considering the numerous changes in the subsequent journey. Without placing a restriction, once Lu Ye took the core out of the marvel, the three divisions of Mount Fangcun would immediately merge toward the core.

This would undoubtedly be detrimental to the stability of Mount Fangcun.

Until this moment, returning to the vicinity of the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye lifted this restriction.

Although he couldn’t see the current state of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun, Lu Ye still had predictions, and what’s next is a long wait.

Currently, the three divisions of Mount Fangcun are very far from the core position, and merging is not a matter of a day or two.

Almost at the same time as Lu Ye lifted the restriction on Mount Fangcun, in a certain illusory grand hall, various Sun Blaze projections fluctuated. More than half of them vanished without a trace in that instant, while the remaining ones, though still maintained, were also distorted and transformed to varying degrees.

Such abnormal occurrences are undoubtedly caused by intense vibrations in the different divisions of Mount Fangcun. Their physical bodies are within each division, projecting their psyche here. The violent tremors of their home divisions impacted these projections.

A short while later, the disappearing figures reassembled.

A Sun Blaze from the Southern Region exclaimed, "Everyone, just now, our division of Mount Fangcun suddenly changed its moving direction again, swiftly heading straight for a certain position, and at an unprecedented speed!"

From the Eastern Region, Chen Xuanhai added, "The same in the Eastern Region!"

Both divisions of Sun Blaze looked towards the Western Region, where Zhang Kun spoke, "It’s the same in the Western Region!"

As he spoke, a group of Sun Blaze all felt a sense of excitement and anticipation through their respective psychic waves, for they realized that the critical moment to change the fragmentation of Mount Fangcun seemed to have arrived!

A few days ago, the moving trajectories of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun suddenly showed significant changes, leading to speculation that the core’s position had changed dramatically, which caused the change in the trajectories.

They gathered here to discuss how to deduce the current specific location of the core.

Who would have thought that before they could discuss a result, another change would occur.

And this time is clearly different from the last! Not only did the moving trajectories change directly, but the moving speed of Mount Fangcun also changed, as if the three divisions of Mount Fangcun were being pulled by some force...

This has never happened before, which inevitably led them to indulge in many reveries.

"Let’s deduce! Let’s see if the current moving directions of the divisions will converge at a point; if they do..." A Sun Blaze spoke with a solemn tone, but everyone understood what it would mean for the Dwarf Race if the moving trajectories of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun had a convergence point.

Concerning the future of the tribe, none of the Sun Blaze had objections and immediately started the busy task of deduction.

The three divisions of Mount Fangcun have so far wandered in different parts of stellar space. Their understanding of the entire stellar space is unmatched by any other race. They have almost complete star maps of each major star system. Based on the current positions and the moving directions of their divisions, they can simply deduce when their division will pass by which star system in the next several decades to a century!

There might be some margin of error, but it won’t be too large.

Sun Blaze projections constantly disappeared and reappeared. The group of Sun Blaze busied themselves for half a day, gradually deducing the moving routes of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun.

When the three routes were placed together, everyone concentrated on observing, and their gaze soon converged on an intersection point!

"Jade Conch Galaxy!" Su Yuqing’s eyes lit up, murmuring.

From the intelligence gathered so far, if the three divisions of Mount Fangcun do not change their direction, sooner or later they will pass through this Jade Conch Galaxy.

And Jade Conch... she was too familiar with this name.

"Is the core here now?" a Sun Blaze inquired.

"Does anyone know about this Jade Conch?" another Sun Blaze asked. In the vast stellar space with countless star systems, even they, as Sun Blaze, dared not claim familiarity with each one. They mostly knew about the more famous systems, and this Jade Conch seemed too inconspicuous to attract their attention.

Even Woo Qimo and Chen Xuanhai showed contemplative expressions. Although the Eastern Mount Fangcun indeed passed through Jade Conch, they never bothered to understand it, so naturally, they hadn’t heard of it.

Only Su Yuqing slowly spoke, "Jade Conch is the star system where Lu Ye was born!"

A group of Sun Blaze immediately turned their gazes, one speaking boldly, "Lu Ye is that little Dao companion of Junior Sister?"

Before the words were finished, another Sun Blaze beside him slapped apart his psyche projection...

Although it was no longer a secret that Su Yuqing in the East had found a young Dao companion, and Su Yuqing herself didn’t shy away from confirming it, no one brought it up in front of her. After all, they were all Sun Blaze, all cared about saving face. If she were a man, being an older person with a younger partner would be nothing, but Su Yuqing was a woman, and such matters were delicate to discuss and rather unpleasant to hear.

"Yes!" Su Yuqing’s expression remained unchanged, "The domain where he was born is called the Nine Heavens. The Nine Heavens World is within the Jade Conch Galaxy, moreover..."

"Moreover, what?"

"When he came from the All Phenomena Ocean to my East, I spoke with him about the core matter. He asked me if, after finding the core, it could be placed near the Nine Heavens, so that Mount Fangcun could merge there."

"This kid... cough, Junior Brother Lu intends to have Mount Fangcun shield the Nine Heavens?" a Sun Blaze perceived Lu Ye’s intention.

"That seems to be the idea. From what I know, the Nine Heavens only recently ascended to a large-scale domain, its foundation is still very weak," Su Yuqing replied.

The Sun Blaze fell silent.

After a long pause, Zhang Kun slapped his thigh, "Good kid, he really pulled it off!"

The situation was very clear. Lu Ye had found the core and brought it back to Jade Conch, which was why the three divisions of Mount Fangcun were being drawn towards Jade Conch under the core’s influence.

For Zhang Kun, who personally took Lu Ye there, this matter seemed almost unbelievable, as throughout history, the Dwarf Race had dispatched numerous foreign Moon Jade to search for the core, investing immense effort in nurturing many of them.

But so far, none had succeeded; they either disappeared without a trace or returned with nothing, having not even glimpsed the core.

After so many years and so much effort without any result, Lu Ye accomplished it in just a few years?

Just three years, yet he retrieved the core!

No matter how you look at it, this is a huge celebration for the Dwarf Race. The three divisions had been awaiting this moment for many years, each anticipation ending in disappointment. No one expected the surprise to come so suddenly, leaving even these Sun Blaze at a loss.

"Junior Sister’s choice in a husband is indeed exceptional!" a Sun Blaze couldn’t help but praise.

Regardless of any ’older person with a younger partner’ speculation, no matter Lu Ye’s potential, aptitude, or cultivation, just helping the Dwarf Race recover the core was a monumental feat.

Even if Lu Ye were a waste, the Dwarf Race here would have to take good care of him in the future.

A Sun Blaze from the Western Region chuckled, "Perhaps you all aren’t aware, but our Junior Brother Lu is also famous on the All Phenomena Ocean. He currently leads a group of cultivators occupying a Three Worlds Island there, a high-class Spirit Island, and even led his followers to conquer another high-class Spirit Island. In that battle, the enemy Moon Jade was completely wiped out, even when a Sun Blaze governor tried to intervene, he was badly humiliated by Lu Ye."

The audience of Sun Blaze, hearing this, couldn’t help but show expressions of surprise.

They all understood what it meant to occupy a high-class Spirit Island in a place like the All Phenomena Ocean. Generally, high-class Spirit Islands were the exclusive cravings of top forces, and without some skill and ability, one couldn’t occupy it, and even if one did, it wouldn’t last long.

Let alone forcefully conquering another high-class Spirit Island, which was countless times harder than merely holding onto one.

The Sun Blaze suddenly realized they might have underestimated this junior brother’s capabilities.

Otherwise, how else could he accomplish in three years what no one else did for so many? It undoubtedly showcased his enormous capabilities.

"Congratulations to Junior Sister for choosing an excellent husband, rendering great service to our race!"

"Once the three divisions merge, Junior Sister must introduce us properly to Junior Brother Lu."

...

A chorus of praise arose, Su Yuqing smiled gracefully, feeling a sense of honor, and the heavy worry held tight for three years finally eased entirely.



============================================================
Chapter 1816: Chapter 1816 - 1814: Busy Days (Happy Mid-Autumn Festival)
============================================================

Based on the current intelligence, it is deduced that the core, lost for years by the Dwarf Race, has been brought out by Lu Ye from the marvel and placed in the Jade Conch Galaxy. This is the reason for the significant change in the movement trajectory of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun, heading towards a convergence point.

However, this is ultimately just the inference of the Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race. Without witnessing it firsthand, no one can be certain of the facts.

With excitement, a Sun Blaze from the Southern Region spoke: "Who among us is closest to the Jade Conch? This matter is significant, and it is prudent to verify it in person."

All the Sun Blaze nodded in agreement with this suggestion.

Su Yuqing spoke: "Let our Eastern Region handle it. Over ten years ago, our Eastern Region passed through the Jade Conch Galaxy. Considering the distance, we are the closest, and if we hurry with all our might, I can return to the Jade Conch within three to five months."

Chen Xuanhai continued: "I will go with my junior sister."

Even for Sun Blaze, traveling at full speed is a massive strain and cannot be maintained for three to five months. However, if two people travel together, they can take turns exerting effort.

Chen Xuanhai undoubtedly also wishes to see with his own eyes whether Lu Ye has brought back the core. This is a matter of utmost importance to the Dwarf Race, which has been weighing on their minds for countless years.

"Then I entrust this matter to you two." The remaining Sun Blaze had no objections.

Once the decision was made, the numerous projections quickly dispersed. Moments later, two figures from the Eastern Region of Mount Fangcun shot up into the sky, transforming into a streak of light, rushing in the direction of the Jade Conch after leaving the domain.

The speed with which Sun Blaze travel is incredibly fast. Even the currently accelerated Mount Fangcun cannot compare. If it weren’t so, Su Yuqing wouldn’t have claimed to return to the Jade Conch within three to five months. After all, over ten years ago, the Eastern region of Mount Fangcun passed through Jade Conch, implying that with all their might, they can cover the distance that Mount Fangcun has drifted over more than ten years in three to five months.

On Misty Peak, Woo Qimo sighed with his hands behind his back. He also wished to visit Jade Conch to see the situation, but unfortunately, since Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing have left, he must stay behind to watch over the place...

In the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye returned after placing the Mount Fangcun core, without going to the Righteous Blood Sect, and directly went to the Grand Governor’s Hall in Tianzhou to have a face-to-face meeting with the current Nine Provinces Governor to give instructions.

Soon, a message was conveyed to all corners through the Nine Provinces Governor’s Palace.

Lu Ye placed something resembling a rockery near the Nine Provinces, and no cultivators are allowed to approach it casually. Additionally, four Moon Jade cultivators have arrived in this world. If encountered, do not panic.

The core has been placed under restriction by Lu Ye, so even if Nine Provinces cultivators approach, it’s not a big deal. They couldn’t break Lu Ye’s restriction to enter the Core World, but it’s always good to be cautious.

As for those four Moon Jade cultivators, they are, of course, Xiang Yin and her sister, along with Yang Ling and Hu Dequan.

Although Moon Jade has not yet emerged in the native Nine Provinces, they are not unfamiliar with Moon Jade, since there was one in the Flower World before. With the Flower World gaining great benefits by being attached to the Nine Provinces, Hua Qianying soon advanced to Moon Jade.

Also, the Clan Leader of the Wood Spirit Race, Mu He, and the Clan Leader of the Spore Race, Black Umbrella, are Moon Jade cultivators. They have all traveled in the Nine Provinces and have had interactions with many Nine Provinces cultivators.

Lu Ye eventually met Number Nine.

Little Flower Girl followed closely behind Number Nine, like Number Nine’s tail, her big eyes wide and bright, filled with innocence and wonder.

After casually chatting with Number Nine to confirm that there had been no incidents recently in the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye sent it off to play with Little Flower Girl.

Lu Ye then hurriedly rushed out of the Nine Provinces and returned to the location of the core.

Xiang Yin and others were still there, their four pairs of eyes looking in awe at the Blood Refinement World, towering near the Nine Provinces. From their viewpoint, the form of the Blood Refinement World was terrifyingly evident, as it clearly resembled a massive creature that had been decapitated with its limbs severed.

Seeing Lu Ye return, Xiang Yin turned to look: "Venerable Lord, what is the situation with that domain? My sister and I feel as though something there is calling out to us."

They had just discussed this with Yang Ling and Hu Dequan, who unfortunately did not have the same sensation, causing Xiang Yin some speculation.

Lu Ye glanced at the Blood Refinement World and explained: "That is the remains of the Blood Ancestor transformed, a place called the Blood Refinement World. Do not approach carelessly."

Ma Shangsi had a similar feeling when he first saw the Blood Refinement World, vaguely believing that his chance to break through to Sun Blaze lay upon it. He wanted to ask Lu Ye to let him visit, but Lu Ye had ruthlessly refused, leaving Ma Shangsi quite distressed.

Xiang Yin and her sister, being part of the Blood Race and possessed of saintliness, naturally feel similarly in the presence of the Blood Ancestor’s remains.

Lu Ye initially refused Ma Shangsi mainly due to the power disparity. Though both are Moon Jade, Lu Ye confidently believes he could handle Ma Shangsi, the Blood Servant, with his treasure blood, but no one knows what changes might occur if a Blood Servant’s cultivation advances to Sun Blaze.

Xiang Yin and her sister’s strength is not much less than Ma Shangsi’s, so clearly, Lu Ye wouldn’t allow them to enter the Blood Refinement World.

Even if they were to go, it wouldn’t be now.

"I’m going out for a while, I’ll be back in a few months. During the time I’m away, you two must guard the core well, and no one is allowed to approach it lightly!" Lu Ye instructed.

"Yes!" Xiang Yin accepted the order, Xuan Yu nodded.

Lu Ye then looked at Yang Ling and Hu Dequan: "You two can do as you please, the core has already been settled, but for the three parts of Mount Fangcun to merge, it will likely take some time."

Yang Ling chuckled: "We can wait!"

They endured all those years trapped in the Core World, now everything has settled, Mount Fangcun is surely on its way to merging, there’s no hurry at all.

The Nine Provinces are nice, the two of them can find a place to relax and unwind, treating it as some leisure after fulfilling their mission.

With arrangements made in the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye finally set off.

He needs to return to the All Phenomena Ocean to replenish the Talent Tree’s fuel. Though he previously obtained a batch of fire-type resources from the Life Origin World, the upcoming tasks will require a large amount of Talent Tree fuel, and those resources are far from sufficient.

The All Phenomena Ocean is the place for a massive fuel replenishment.

About ten days later, Lu Ye returned to the passage leading to the Soul Race ancestral land, transferred through the stellar space pond, and arrived at the Cangyue Galaxy.

Another ten days later, he reached the Insect Path connecting the Cangyue Galaxy to the Jade Conch Galaxy.

The Moon Jade stationed here was an old acquaintance, after all, Lu Ye had used this Insect Path several times, and as the Third Island Master of Three Worlds Island, he even led a glorious conquest to break through Baiyue Island. Lu Ye is not a nameless figure across the All Phenomena Ocean.

Suddenly seeing Lu Ye appear, the Moon Jade was undoubtedly surprised, because there was no record of Lu Ye coming from the All Phenomena Ocean, somehow he entered from this home galaxy.

However, this is no major issue, the routes in the stellar space are not singular, sometimes departing from one place and returning from another is possible.

After a short conversation with Lu Ye, he was quickly allowed through.

Over three years later, passing through the Insect Path, Lu Ye returned to the Jade Conch Galaxy.

Days later, at the bustling Three Worlds Island, at Lu Ye’s bamboo building, he was driving the Talent Tree’s powers to refine various fire-type resources, madly replenishing the fuel reserves.

Luan Xiao’e stood in front of him, holding a jade slip, chattering away.

Lu Ye couldn’t help but sigh: "Senior Sister, for all affairs on the island, you and Old Tang just take charge, no need to tell me so much."

Luan Xiao’e rebuked: "Three Worlds Island, this is the shared Spirit Island of the Three Worlds, the issue of accounts is the most serious matter. In these years you were away, our Three Worlds Island developed well, how much spirit jade we earned, how much we spent, you ought to know."

In the years Lu Ye was away, the development of Three Worlds Island indeed improved progressively.

When he left, Three Worlds Island was already experiencing vigorous growth, and later a batch of the Dwarf Race settled down, opening a talisman shop on Three Worlds Island, the only Dwarf Race talisman shop across the All Phenomena Ocean. Just the reputation alone is enticing enough, if one can secure a couple of purple talismans, they definitely serve as a trump card.

Nowadays, the liveliest place on the entire Three Worlds Island is not the Three Worlds Apothecary on this island, nor the Five Colors Merchants Guild branch, but the vicinity of the Dwarf Race talisman shop.

Every day, a large number of cultivators queue to purchase talismans from the Dwarf Race, yet still, the supply fails to meet the demand. The cultivators of the Dwarf Race residing on the Three Worlds Island are truly both blissful and distressed, blissful because earning spirit jade here is so easy, distressed because their lives are miserable, just making spirit talismans or on the journey to make them...

The spirit jade reserve of Three Worlds Island is now as high as over ten billion, and currently, looking out across the All Phenomena Ocean, the treatment of Three Worlds cultivators is unparalleled. With abundant cultivation resources, besides completing their own tasks, the Three Worlds cultivators are all diligently cultivating.

The Constellations over at the Nine Provinces have generally seen considerable growth, there are signs of several Constellation Late Stage cultivators from Qingli Dao World and Jade Conch intending to advance to Moon Jade, particularly from the Jade Conch World, where three Constellations have already advanced to Moon Jade, which is truly joyous. Although no matter how many Moon Jade there are, only five registered ones can participate in the Spirit Island contest, the increase in the number of Moon Jade here on this island is still a testament to the depth.

The Moon Jade level has always been an awkward point for the Nine Provinces; currently, besides Lu Ye, there are no other Moon Jade in the Nine Provinces. Hence, Luan Xiao’e would come here and chatter non-stop. The ability of Three Worlds Island to establish and its excellent cultivation environment for the Three Worlds cultivators now owes a lot to Lu Ye’s efforts in the past, so the account issues naturally need to be informed to Lu Ye.

Lu Ye blinked at Luan Xiao’e, his hands continuing to refine the resources: "I know now!"

Luan Xiao’e sighed: "I knew you’d have this attitude, pay more attention when you have time later."

Lu Ye nodded repeatedly: "Understood."

Luan Xiao’e reluctantly leaves, suddenly stopping, turning her head to Lu Ye: "When you go back to Jade Conch again, bring some resources back."

"Alright!" Lu Ye agreed.



============================================================
Chapter 1814: Chapter 1814 - 1812: Social Skills
============================================================

After staying for several days on Lih Shang’s Lotus Land, Lu Ye departed.

Yiyi and Amber watched him go, no longer feeling the sadness of the last farewell, as their mood had changed.

During the last farewell, Yiyi always felt that she might not see Lu Ye for a very long time, which naturally made her reluctant. But now she knew that Lu Ye could come and go to the Soul Race ancestral land, so there would be many opportunities to meet in the future.

Before parting, Yiyi gave Lu Ye thousands of soul jades, all meticulously refined by her during her cultivation time.

Lu Ye did not refuse, accepting them gladly. These soul jades are hard to find in the outside world because the environment suitable for their birth is rare, but here at the Soul Race ancestral land, they are easily acquired due to the abundance of pure Soul Power.

Typically, tribal members of the Soul Race wouldn’t refine soul jades because they can directly refine Soul Power for cultivation. Spending time and effort on refining soul jades would only be a waste of time.

These soul jades from Yiyi were undoubtedly specially prepared for Lu Ye, perhaps with a contribution from Lih Shang.

In front of the seven-color Lotus Land where the stellar space pond is located, Lu Ye had just arrived, riding the core, and from a distance, he saw Elder Xuyuan.

Elder Xuyuan had actually detected Lu Ye as soon as he entered the Soul Race ancestral land, but since Lu Ye first visited Lih Shang’s Lotus Land, Xuyuan did not interrupt but waited here all along.

"Elder!" Lu Ye jumped down from the core, greeting with respect.

Xuyuan nodded slightly, approached with interest, and scrutinized the core, appearing uncertain and curious. After a long while, Xuyuan finally asked, "Boy, is this a miniature world?"

Yet it seemed somewhat different from the miniature worlds he knew. To call it a miniature world seemed inaccurate because it is quite large; typically, so-called miniature worlds can be carried along, like the Small Flower World that Lu Ye possesses, which can be considered a miniature world.

Moreover, there were treasures when Ban Ci housed Ban Xia back then, also considered a miniature world.

But Xuyuan had never seen such a large miniature world, and its design was rather peculiar.

Facing Xuyuan, Lu Ye didn’t conceal the truth, candidly saying, "It’s not wrong to call it a miniature world, but it’s different from ordinary miniature worlds. It’s the core of Mount Fangcun."

Xuyuan suddenly whipped his head toward Lu Ye, shocked, "Mount Fangcun? The Dwarf Race’s Mount Fangcun?"

"Exactly!" Lu Ye nodded.

Xuyuan’s interest grew stronger as he surveyed the core nonstop, soon saying, "Back then, the Blood Ancestor intended to capture Mount Fangcun and led a strong force of the Blood Race to attack fiercely. A great battle ensued, resulting in mutual destruction. Mount Fangcun was shattered and divided into three parts with its core lost and whereabouts unknown. Where did you find it, boy?"

Lu Ye explained, "Actually, the Dwarf Race always knew the location of the core and worked hard over the years to retrieve it. But due to several reasons, they could not succeed, so I took on the task at the request of Sun Blaze from the Dwarf Race and eventually gained results."

"You have a good relationship with the Dwarf Race?" Xuyuan looked at him, stunned. Giving such an important task of searching for the core to an outsider indicates that their relationship is undoubtedly close.

"Quite good." Lu Ye touched his nose, hesitating to say his Dao companion relationship with Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race, which would be rather startling.

Xuyuan looked at him and chuckled, "You sure have a knack for networking."

Lu Ye could be considered half a member of the Soul Race, and now he was closely connected with the Dwarf Race as well. Yet both the Soul Race and Dwarf Race aren’t easy to engage with, especially the Soul Race; most people don’t even know where their ancestral land is, let alone find it.

Lu Ye pondered for a moment; he seemed to have good diplomatic ties with several races. Setting aside the Soul Race and Dwarf Race, he also had the merfolk of the All Phenomena Ocean, the most solid allies of Three Worlds Island, and now the Flower Race settled in the Nine Provinces...

"Treat others with sincerity, and naturally, they will treat me sincerely."

Xuyuan nodded, agreeing with his words.

"Elder, have you ever seen the Blood Ancestor?" Lu Ye asked.

Xuyuan shook his head, replying, "Never seen. The Blood Ancestor was active long ago, before my time, and you know our Soul Race’s circumstances; we generally don’t interact with the outside world much."

"Why did the Blood Ancestor target the Dwarf Race?"

Xuyuan waved his hand, saying, "You’re mistaken. The Blood Ancestor didn’t target the Dwarf Race; she wanted Mount Fangcun. The Dwarf Race was affected because they were born of Mount Fangcun. I’ve heard that during that era, the Insect Race also fell under her control. You should understand the Insect Race’s plundering style: the hives often drift about, seeking targets to invade. But hives are more fragile; if targeted by a powerful force, they can easily be destroyed. However, if the hives were to be placed inside Mount Fangcun?"

Lu Ye suddenly realized.

The Insect Race combined with Mount Fangcun would be a flawless partnership. Imagine the Insect Race commanding Mount Fangcun, such a stellar space supreme treasure, wandering through stellar space... If the Blood Ancestor truly seized Mount Fangcun back then, the harm the Insect Race could cause would be far greater than today.

Moreover, Lu Ye finally understood the fundamental reason for the good relationship between the Insect and Blood Races; it turns out both had served under the Blood Ancestor’s command in the past.

In this light, the war over Mount Fangcun likely involved not just the Blood Race, but the Insect Race too.

"How did the Blood Ancestor die?" Lu Ye asked again, curious. To nurture a race was indicative of her strength, and according to Lu Ye’s speculation, the Blood Ancestor’s prowess couldn’t be as simple as Sun Blaze. How could such a formidable being get defeated? And even dismembered.

Xuyuan shook his head: "I don’t know how the Blood Ancestor died, but kid, the world is not as simple as you see it. Some things can only be slowly uncovered when you have sufficiently strong power. For a cultivator, weakness is the greatest original sin."

After chatting with Xuyuan for a while, Lu Ye drove the core to the stellar space pond.

"Elder, can I pass through the passage with the core?" Lu Ye asked. He had always been traveling alone before, and although the core was not very large, it was a dozen or so feet long. He wasn’t sure if he could bring the core through the passage to return to the Jade Conch Galaxy.

If not, it would be a big trouble. At that time, he would have to choose to leave the core in the Soul Race ancestral land and then find a way to notify the Dwarf Race to take the core themselves.

"It’s not a big problem." Xuyuan said calmly, "You just need to wrap the core with power during transit."

Lu Ye understood and immediately began to locate the position of Jade Conch in the stellar space pond.

He had traveled to and from Jade Conch several times using the stellar space pond, so he was naturally skillful and quickly gained results.

"Then, Elder, I’m going." After saying a word to Xuyuan, Lu Ye wrapped the core with power and plunged into the stellar space pond.

The scene of an entire stellar space shrinking countless times and rushing toward him was shockingly spectacular no matter how many times he saw it. The stellar region belonging to Jade Conch in his field of vision continued to enlarge, enlarge, and enlarge again...

When Lu Ye regained his senses, he had arrived at Jade Conch.

After slightly discerning the direction, Lu Ye controlled the core and headed towards the Nine Provinces.

On the Eastern Mount Fangcun, due to previous incidents, the three big Sun Blazes did not engage in cultivation but constantly sensed the movements of the main part, anticipating some changes to occur.

Unfortunately, the main part of Mount Fangcun had been stationary somewhere in the stellar space and showed no signs of movement. Until this moment, it finally started to move.

What shocked Su Yuqing and the others was that the movement trajectory of Mount Fangcun suddenly changed significantly.

The three immediately gathered together and, after a simple discussion, concluded that the position of the core had shifted dramatically.

This is why the movement trajectory of the main Mount Fangcun changed.

First, the core was completely isolated by some mysterious power, causing the three Mount Fangcun to stop drifting. Then, within a few days, the core’s position changed dramatically. All these strange occurrences left people puzzled, and no one knew what happened.

Yet, despite this, the Sun Blazes of the Dwarf Race were extremely excited and hopeful.

Because if the core’s position changed significantly, it would likely mean the core had already escaped the Illusory Blood Devil’s Eye marvel.

This change is undoubtedly a good omen!

As for the current exact position of the core, it was unknown on the Mount Fangcun side. They had to observe for decades or even centuries according to the drifting trajectory of the three Mount Fangcun and then calculate comprehensively to determine the result.

This was not something that could be solved quickly, so the three Sun Blazes gathered again to discuss the significant matter of deducing the core’s position.

At this time, on the core, not only was Lu Ye present, but also Xiang Yin and sister, Yang Ling, and Hu Dequan were there.

Looking far ahead at the domain, Xiang Yin exclaimed with excitement, "Venerable Lord, is that your domain?"

"The domain where I was born, not my domain." Lu Ye replied.

Previously, Xiang Yin and the others had always been in the Core World. Now that they were nearing Nine Provinces, it would naturally not be appropriate to keep them inside.

Settling them wasn’t difficult. Xiang Yin and sister were his Blood Servants, and under Lu Ye’s command, they didn’t dare to disobey. For now, letting them stay in the Nine Provinces would suffice.

As for Yang Ling and Hu Dequan, they could also stay in the Nine Provinces, waiting for the three Mount Fangcun to merge, and on that day, they could be reunited with their Dao companions.

Moreover, all four of them were in the Moon Jade Late Stage and had considerable strength. Staying in the Nine Provinces would also enable them to protect it.

Many dangers in stellar space were sudden, like the previous invasion by the Filth Race, or encountering an insect hive invasion on the way...

The reason Nine Provinces had been safe for so many years was, one, due to Number Nine’s concealing ability, and two, the remoteness of Jade Conch.

But nothing is absolute, and some precautions are necessary.

Waiting for the local cultivator of Nine Provinces to grow takes too long. During this period, any unforeseen event could be unbearable for Nine Provinces.

Therefore, Lu Ye came up with the idea of using the Dwarf Race as a reliance. Now that he brought back the core of Mount Fangcun, given time, the fused Mount Fangcun would become the strongest backing for Nine Provinces, without fear of any external invasion.

In just a few days, they reached the outer regions of Nine Provinces.



============================================================
Chapter 1815: Chapter 1815 - 1813: Monumental Merit
============================================================

At the core, Lu Ye sighed.

In the past, by this time, Number Nine would have already contacted him, but this time upon returning, there was no message from Number Nine.

He didn’t think Number Nine had encountered any accident. If something had happened to Number Nine, the Nine Provinces would surely be in chaos.

Number Nine is probably indulged in the company of Little Flower Girl now...

But this is a good thing, at least Number Nine won’t be lonely anymore.

Soon, they were beside the Nine Provinces. As always, Lu Ye’s whereabouts were instantly detected by the Nine Provinces Constellation responsible for patrolling nearby. Upon seeing it was Lu Ye, they immediately lowered their guard and continued their patrol after greeting him.

Initially, when Lu Ye returned from the All Phenomena Ocean, the Constellations of the Nine Provinces were incredibly excited and expectant. However, as he left and returned more frequently, they all became accustomed to it.

For Constellations like them, cultivating and becoming stronger is always the primary task. Since the Nine Provinces don’t have their own Spirit Jade Vein, they can only delve deeper into the stellar space to search for spirit jade, refine a certain amount of it, and use it as nourishment for their growth.

The core stops, observes from afar, and is not unusual. In fact, if an uninformed cultivator were to encounter the core in stellar space, they wouldn’t give it a second glance because such things are so common in stellar space.

But this is the core of Mount Fangcun. The Dwarf Race of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun have been striving for countless years to recover this core, and today, the dust has settled.

Looking down at the core beneath his feet, Lu Ye’s mind stirred, and he gently stomped his foot.

The core trembled slightly, and a mystical force spread out, as if some restriction was being broken.

Indeed, it was a restriction being broken. Before Lu Ye took the core out of the marvel of the Illusory Blood Devil’s Eye, he had imposed a restriction using his status as the Origin Lord.

The function of this restriction is singular, which is to generate an isolating force similar to the marvel, preventing the three divisions of Mount Fangcun from merging with the core.

The reason for doing so was because of considering the numerous changes in the subsequent journey. Without placing a restriction, once Lu Ye took the core out of the marvel, the three divisions of Mount Fangcun would immediately merge toward the core.

This would undoubtedly be detrimental to the stability of Mount Fangcun.

Until this moment, returning to the vicinity of the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye lifted this restriction.

Although he couldn’t see the current state of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun, Lu Ye still had predictions, and what’s next is a long wait.

Currently, the three divisions of Mount Fangcun are very far from the core position, and merging is not a matter of a day or two.

Almost at the same time as Lu Ye lifted the restriction on Mount Fangcun, in a certain illusory grand hall, various Sun Blaze projections fluctuated. More than half of them vanished without a trace in that instant, while the remaining ones, though still maintained, were also distorted and transformed to varying degrees.

Such abnormal occurrences are undoubtedly caused by intense vibrations in the different divisions of Mount Fangcun. Their physical bodies are within each division, projecting their psyche here. The violent tremors of their home divisions impacted these projections.

A short while later, the disappearing figures reassembled.

A Sun Blaze from the Southern Region exclaimed, "Everyone, just now, our division of Mount Fangcun suddenly changed its moving direction again, swiftly heading straight for a certain position, and at an unprecedented speed!"

From the Eastern Region, Chen Xuanhai added, "The same in the Eastern Region!"

Both divisions of Sun Blaze looked towards the Western Region, where Zhang Kun spoke, "It’s the same in the Western Region!"

As he spoke, a group of Sun Blaze all felt a sense of excitement and anticipation through their respective psychic waves, for they realized that the critical moment to change the fragmentation of Mount Fangcun seemed to have arrived!

A few days ago, the moving trajectories of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun suddenly showed significant changes, leading to speculation that the core’s position had changed dramatically, which caused the change in the trajectories.

They gathered here to discuss how to deduce the current specific location of the core.

Who would have thought that before they could discuss a result, another change would occur.

And this time is clearly different from the last! Not only did the moving trajectories change directly, but the moving speed of Mount Fangcun also changed, as if the three divisions of Mount Fangcun were being pulled by some force...

This has never happened before, which inevitably led them to indulge in many reveries.

"Let’s deduce! Let’s see if the current moving directions of the divisions will converge at a point; if they do..." A Sun Blaze spoke with a solemn tone, but everyone understood what it would mean for the Dwarf Race if the moving trajectories of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun had a convergence point.

Concerning the future of the tribe, none of the Sun Blaze had objections and immediately started the busy task of deduction.

The three divisions of Mount Fangcun have so far wandered in different parts of stellar space. Their understanding of the entire stellar space is unmatched by any other race. They have almost complete star maps of each major star system. Based on the current positions and the moving directions of their divisions, they can simply deduce when their division will pass by which star system in the next several decades to a century!

There might be some margin of error, but it won’t be too large.

Sun Blaze projections constantly disappeared and reappeared. The group of Sun Blaze busied themselves for half a day, gradually deducing the moving routes of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun.

When the three routes were placed together, everyone concentrated on observing, and their gaze soon converged on an intersection point!

"Jade Conch Galaxy!" Su Yuqing’s eyes lit up, murmuring.

From the intelligence gathered so far, if the three divisions of Mount Fangcun do not change their direction, sooner or later they will pass through this Jade Conch Galaxy.

And Jade Conch... she was too familiar with this name.

"Is the core here now?" a Sun Blaze inquired.

"Does anyone know about this Jade Conch?" another Sun Blaze asked. In the vast stellar space with countless star systems, even they, as Sun Blaze, dared not claim familiarity with each one. They mostly knew about the more famous systems, and this Jade Conch seemed too inconspicuous to attract their attention.

Even Woo Qimo and Chen Xuanhai showed contemplative expressions. Although the Eastern Mount Fangcun indeed passed through Jade Conch, they never bothered to understand it, so naturally, they hadn’t heard of it.

Only Su Yuqing slowly spoke, "Jade Conch is the star system where Lu Ye was born!"

A group of Sun Blaze immediately turned their gazes, one speaking boldly, "Lu Ye is that little Dao companion of Junior Sister?"

Before the words were finished, another Sun Blaze beside him slapped apart his psyche projection...

Although it was no longer a secret that Su Yuqing in the East had found a young Dao companion, and Su Yuqing herself didn’t shy away from confirming it, no one brought it up in front of her. After all, they were all Sun Blaze, all cared about saving face. If she were a man, being an older person with a younger partner would be nothing, but Su Yuqing was a woman, and such matters were delicate to discuss and rather unpleasant to hear.

"Yes!" Su Yuqing’s expression remained unchanged, "The domain where he was born is called the Nine Heavens. The Nine Heavens World is within the Jade Conch Galaxy, moreover..."

"Moreover, what?"

"When he came from the All Phenomena Ocean to my East, I spoke with him about the core matter. He asked me if, after finding the core, it could be placed near the Nine Heavens, so that Mount Fangcun could merge there."

"This kid... cough, Junior Brother Lu intends to have Mount Fangcun shield the Nine Heavens?" a Sun Blaze perceived Lu Ye’s intention.

"That seems to be the idea. From what I know, the Nine Heavens only recently ascended to a large-scale domain, its foundation is still very weak," Su Yuqing replied.

The Sun Blaze fell silent.

After a long pause, Zhang Kun slapped his thigh, "Good kid, he really pulled it off!"

The situation was very clear. Lu Ye had found the core and brought it back to Jade Conch, which was why the three divisions of Mount Fangcun were being drawn towards Jade Conch under the core’s influence.

For Zhang Kun, who personally took Lu Ye there, this matter seemed almost unbelievable, as throughout history, the Dwarf Race had dispatched numerous foreign Moon Jade to search for the core, investing immense effort in nurturing many of them.

But so far, none had succeeded; they either disappeared without a trace or returned with nothing, having not even glimpsed the core.

After so many years and so much effort without any result, Lu Ye accomplished it in just a few years?

Just three years, yet he retrieved the core!

No matter how you look at it, this is a huge celebration for the Dwarf Race. The three divisions had been awaiting this moment for many years, each anticipation ending in disappointment. No one expected the surprise to come so suddenly, leaving even these Sun Blaze at a loss.

"Junior Sister’s choice in a husband is indeed exceptional!" a Sun Blaze couldn’t help but praise.

Regardless of any ’older person with a younger partner’ speculation, no matter Lu Ye’s potential, aptitude, or cultivation, just helping the Dwarf Race recover the core was a monumental feat.

Even if Lu Ye were a waste, the Dwarf Race here would have to take good care of him in the future.

A Sun Blaze from the Western Region chuckled, "Perhaps you all aren’t aware, but our Junior Brother Lu is also famous on the All Phenomena Ocean. He currently leads a group of cultivators occupying a Three Worlds Island there, a high-class Spirit Island, and even led his followers to conquer another high-class Spirit Island. In that battle, the enemy Moon Jade was completely wiped out, even when a Sun Blaze governor tried to intervene, he was badly humiliated by Lu Ye."

The audience of Sun Blaze, hearing this, couldn’t help but show expressions of surprise.

They all understood what it meant to occupy a high-class Spirit Island in a place like the All Phenomena Ocean. Generally, high-class Spirit Islands were the exclusive cravings of top forces, and without some skill and ability, one couldn’t occupy it, and even if one did, it wouldn’t last long.

Let alone forcefully conquering another high-class Spirit Island, which was countless times harder than merely holding onto one.

The Sun Blaze suddenly realized they might have underestimated this junior brother’s capabilities.

Otherwise, how else could he accomplish in three years what no one else did for so many? It undoubtedly showcased his enormous capabilities.

"Congratulations to Junior Sister for choosing an excellent husband, rendering great service to our race!"

"Once the three divisions merge, Junior Sister must introduce us properly to Junior Brother Lu."

...

A chorus of praise arose, Su Yuqing smiled gracefully, feeling a sense of honor, and the heavy worry held tight for three years finally eased entirely.



============================================================
Chapter 1816: Chapter 1816 - 1814: Busy Days (Happy Mid-Autumn Festival)
============================================================

Based on the current intelligence, it is deduced that the core, lost for years by the Dwarf Race, has been brought out by Lu Ye from the marvel and placed in the Jade Conch Galaxy. This is the reason for the significant change in the movement trajectory of the three divisions of Mount Fangcun, heading towards a convergence point.

However, this is ultimately just the inference of the Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race. Without witnessing it firsthand, no one can be certain of the facts.

With excitement, a Sun Blaze from the Southern Region spoke: "Who among us is closest to the Jade Conch? This matter is significant, and it is prudent to verify it in person."

All the Sun Blaze nodded in agreement with this suggestion.

Su Yuqing spoke: "Let our Eastern Region handle it. Over ten years ago, our Eastern Region passed through the Jade Conch Galaxy. Considering the distance, we are the closest, and if we hurry with all our might, I can return to the Jade Conch within three to five months."

Chen Xuanhai continued: "I will go with my junior sister."

Even for Sun Blaze, traveling at full speed is a massive strain and cannot be maintained for three to five months. However, if two people travel together, they can take turns exerting effort.

Chen Xuanhai undoubtedly also wishes to see with his own eyes whether Lu Ye has brought back the core. This is a matter of utmost importance to the Dwarf Race, which has been weighing on their minds for countless years.

"Then I entrust this matter to you two." The remaining Sun Blaze had no objections.

Once the decision was made, the numerous projections quickly dispersed. Moments later, two figures from the Eastern Region of Mount Fangcun shot up into the sky, transforming into a streak of light, rushing in the direction of the Jade Conch after leaving the domain.

The speed with which Sun Blaze travel is incredibly fast. Even the currently accelerated Mount Fangcun cannot compare. If it weren’t so, Su Yuqing wouldn’t have claimed to return to the Jade Conch within three to five months. After all, over ten years ago, the Eastern region of Mount Fangcun passed through Jade Conch, implying that with all their might, they can cover the distance that Mount Fangcun has drifted over more than ten years in three to five months.

On Misty Peak, Woo Qimo sighed with his hands behind his back. He also wished to visit Jade Conch to see the situation, but unfortunately, since Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing have left, he must stay behind to watch over the place...

In the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye returned after placing the Mount Fangcun core, without going to the Righteous Blood Sect, and directly went to the Grand Governor’s Hall in Tianzhou to have a face-to-face meeting with the current Nine Provinces Governor to give instructions.

Soon, a message was conveyed to all corners through the Nine Provinces Governor’s Palace.

Lu Ye placed something resembling a rockery near the Nine Provinces, and no cultivators are allowed to approach it casually. Additionally, four Moon Jade cultivators have arrived in this world. If encountered, do not panic.

The core has been placed under restriction by Lu Ye, so even if Nine Provinces cultivators approach, it’s not a big deal. They couldn’t break Lu Ye’s restriction to enter the Core World, but it’s always good to be cautious.

As for those four Moon Jade cultivators, they are, of course, Xiang Yin and her sister, along with Yang Ling and Hu Dequan.

Although Moon Jade has not yet emerged in the native Nine Provinces, they are not unfamiliar with Moon Jade, since there was one in the Flower World before. With the Flower World gaining great benefits by being attached to the Nine Provinces, Hua Qianying soon advanced to Moon Jade.

Also, the Clan Leader of the Wood Spirit Race, Mu He, and the Clan Leader of the Spore Race, Black Umbrella, are Moon Jade cultivators. They have all traveled in the Nine Provinces and have had interactions with many Nine Provinces cultivators.

Lu Ye eventually met Number Nine.

Little Flower Girl followed closely behind Number Nine, like Number Nine’s tail, her big eyes wide and bright, filled with innocence and wonder.

After casually chatting with Number Nine to confirm that there had been no incidents recently in the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye sent it off to play with Little Flower Girl.

Lu Ye then hurriedly rushed out of the Nine Provinces and returned to the location of the core.

Xiang Yin and others were still there, their four pairs of eyes looking in awe at the Blood Refinement World, towering near the Nine Provinces. From their viewpoint, the form of the Blood Refinement World was terrifyingly evident, as it clearly resembled a massive creature that had been decapitated with its limbs severed.

Seeing Lu Ye return, Xiang Yin turned to look: "Venerable Lord, what is the situation with that domain? My sister and I feel as though something there is calling out to us."

They had just discussed this with Yang Ling and Hu Dequan, who unfortunately did not have the same sensation, causing Xiang Yin some speculation.

Lu Ye glanced at the Blood Refinement World and explained: "That is the remains of the Blood Ancestor transformed, a place called the Blood Refinement World. Do not approach carelessly."

Ma Shangsi had a similar feeling when he first saw the Blood Refinement World, vaguely believing that his chance to break through to Sun Blaze lay upon it. He wanted to ask Lu Ye to let him visit, but Lu Ye had ruthlessly refused, leaving Ma Shangsi quite distressed.

Xiang Yin and her sister, being part of the Blood Race and possessed of saintliness, naturally feel similarly in the presence of the Blood Ancestor’s remains.

Lu Ye initially refused Ma Shangsi mainly due to the power disparity. Though both are Moon Jade, Lu Ye confidently believes he could handle Ma Shangsi, the Blood Servant, with his treasure blood, but no one knows what changes might occur if a Blood Servant’s cultivation advances to Sun Blaze.

Xiang Yin and her sister’s strength is not much less than Ma Shangsi’s, so clearly, Lu Ye wouldn’t allow them to enter the Blood Refinement World.

Even if they were to go, it wouldn’t be now.

"I’m going out for a while, I’ll be back in a few months. During the time I’m away, you two must guard the core well, and no one is allowed to approach it lightly!" Lu Ye instructed.

"Yes!" Xiang Yin accepted the order, Xuan Yu nodded.

Lu Ye then looked at Yang Ling and Hu Dequan: "You two can do as you please, the core has already been settled, but for the three parts of Mount Fangcun to merge, it will likely take some time."

Yang Ling chuckled: "We can wait!"

They endured all those years trapped in the Core World, now everything has settled, Mount Fangcun is surely on its way to merging, there’s no hurry at all.

The Nine Provinces are nice, the two of them can find a place to relax and unwind, treating it as some leisure after fulfilling their mission.

With arrangements made in the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye finally set off.

He needs to return to the All Phenomena Ocean to replenish the Talent Tree’s fuel. Though he previously obtained a batch of fire-type resources from the Life Origin World, the upcoming tasks will require a large amount of Talent Tree fuel, and those resources are far from sufficient.

The All Phenomena Ocean is the place for a massive fuel replenishment.

About ten days later, Lu Ye returned to the passage leading to the Soul Race ancestral land, transferred through the stellar space pond, and arrived at the Cangyue Galaxy.

Another ten days later, he reached the Insect Path connecting the Cangyue Galaxy to the Jade Conch Galaxy.

The Moon Jade stationed here was an old acquaintance, after all, Lu Ye had used this Insect Path several times, and as the Third Island Master of Three Worlds Island, he even led a glorious conquest to break through Baiyue Island. Lu Ye is not a nameless figure across the All Phenomena Ocean.

Suddenly seeing Lu Ye appear, the Moon Jade was undoubtedly surprised, because there was no record of Lu Ye coming from the All Phenomena Ocean, somehow he entered from this home galaxy.

However, this is no major issue, the routes in the stellar space are not singular, sometimes departing from one place and returning from another is possible.

After a short conversation with Lu Ye, he was quickly allowed through.

Over three years later, passing through the Insect Path, Lu Ye returned to the Jade Conch Galaxy.

Days later, at the bustling Three Worlds Island, at Lu Ye’s bamboo building, he was driving the Talent Tree’s powers to refine various fire-type resources, madly replenishing the fuel reserves.

Luan Xiao’e stood in front of him, holding a jade slip, chattering away.

Lu Ye couldn’t help but sigh: "Senior Sister, for all affairs on the island, you and Old Tang just take charge, no need to tell me so much."

Luan Xiao’e rebuked: "Three Worlds Island, this is the shared Spirit Island of the Three Worlds, the issue of accounts is the most serious matter. In these years you were away, our Three Worlds Island developed well, how much spirit jade we earned, how much we spent, you ought to know."

In the years Lu Ye was away, the development of Three Worlds Island indeed improved progressively.

When he left, Three Worlds Island was already experiencing vigorous growth, and later a batch of the Dwarf Race settled down, opening a talisman shop on Three Worlds Island, the only Dwarf Race talisman shop across the All Phenomena Ocean. Just the reputation alone is enticing enough, if one can secure a couple of purple talismans, they definitely serve as a trump card.

Nowadays, the liveliest place on the entire Three Worlds Island is not the Three Worlds Apothecary on this island, nor the Five Colors Merchants Guild branch, but the vicinity of the Dwarf Race talisman shop.

Every day, a large number of cultivators queue to purchase talismans from the Dwarf Race, yet still, the supply fails to meet the demand. The cultivators of the Dwarf Race residing on the Three Worlds Island are truly both blissful and distressed, blissful because earning spirit jade here is so easy, distressed because their lives are miserable, just making spirit talismans or on the journey to make them...

The spirit jade reserve of Three Worlds Island is now as high as over ten billion, and currently, looking out across the All Phenomena Ocean, the treatment of Three Worlds cultivators is unparalleled. With abundant cultivation resources, besides completing their own tasks, the Three Worlds cultivators are all diligently cultivating.

The Constellations over at the Nine Provinces have generally seen considerable growth, there are signs of several Constellation Late Stage cultivators from Qingli Dao World and Jade Conch intending to advance to Moon Jade, particularly from the Jade Conch World, where three Constellations have already advanced to Moon Jade, which is truly joyous. Although no matter how many Moon Jade there are, only five registered ones can participate in the Spirit Island contest, the increase in the number of Moon Jade here on this island is still a testament to the depth.

The Moon Jade level has always been an awkward point for the Nine Provinces; currently, besides Lu Ye, there are no other Moon Jade in the Nine Provinces. Hence, Luan Xiao’e would come here and chatter non-stop. The ability of Three Worlds Island to establish and its excellent cultivation environment for the Three Worlds cultivators now owes a lot to Lu Ye’s efforts in the past, so the account issues naturally need to be informed to Lu Ye.

Lu Ye blinked at Luan Xiao’e, his hands continuing to refine the resources: "I know now!"

Luan Xiao’e sighed: "I knew you’d have this attitude, pay more attention when you have time later."

Lu Ye nodded repeatedly: "Understood."

Luan Xiao’e reluctantly leaves, suddenly stopping, turning her head to Lu Ye: "When you go back to Jade Conch again, bring some resources back."

"Alright!" Lu Ye agreed.
