Chapter 1817: Chapter 1817 1815: Your People?
============================================================

Lu Ye didn't stay long on Three Worlds Island, only for half a month, but the spirit jade reserve on Three Worlds Island cost nearly two hundred million.

This is also why he doesn't worry much about accounting issues, because whenever he has a need, the warehouse on Three Worlds Island will open to him without limit, and neither Luan Xiao'e nor Tang Jun will say anything about it.

There was enough replenishment for the Talent Tree's fuel reserve, and Lu Ye even left a batch of fire-type resources as a backup.

During this period, he also took time to visit Hua Ci in the merfolk territory. Unfortunately, after several years, the amber sealing Hua Ci remained unchanged, with no significant transformation.

The only thing that delighted Lu Ye was that he could sense Hua Ci's strength had greatly improved.

This is not hard to understand because, in Lu Ye's perception, the amber that sealed Hua Ci had been continuously absorbing the sea water of All Phenomena Ocean, seemingly possessing a refining capability. Even though this refining efficiency didn't match that of the Talent Tree, it was much more terrifying than the efficiency of a cultivator's normal cultivation.

Undoubtedly, part of the energy produced after refining the sea water of All Phenomena Ocean was used by Hua Ci, and naturally, her strength could improve.

Compared to Hua Ci's improvement, the enhancement of the Pixiu she held seemed even more terrifying...

Lu Ye was eagerly anticipating the state Hua Ci would be in after being unsealed.

Half a month after returning to All Phenomena Ocean, Lu Ye set off on the journey back to the Nine Provinces.

This journey was already very familiar to him.

In a swift twenty days, he returned to the Nine Provinces once again.

Xiang Yin and sister diligently guarded near the core, but Yang Ling and Hu Dequan were nowhere to be seen. According to Xiang Yin, they had already entered the Nine Provinces, but what they were doing there was unknown.

A short while later, in the Nine Provinces Governor's Palace, Lu Ye placed a large pile of storage rings on the table in front of him, jingling for quite a while.

The current Nine Provinces Governor, originally the Sect Master of a certain sect in Leizhou, widened his eyes in astonishment, "Brother Lu, what's going on here?" As he spoke, he picked up a storage ring and probed inside with his Mental Consciousness, almost blinded by the sight.

The ring was filled with spirit jade.

"This..." The Sect Master was shocked.

He picked up another storage ring and exclaimed again, "Ah, this..." Inside was also a large amount of spirit jade.

"Stop fussing." Lu Ye interrupted him, "These are resources brought back from Three Worlds Island. Get some people over to count them, then divide them into three parts. Our Nine Provinces will keep one part, and the other two will be sent to Qingli Dao World and Jade Conch World."

The Sect Master could hardly believe it, "Has our Three Worlds Island developed this well?"

Though the Nine Provinces had heard of the matters regarding All Phenomena Ocean for over a decade, and the first batch of cultivators had gone there some years ago, the local cultivators who stayed behind hadn't really obtained any tangible benefits from All Phenomena Ocean. This was the first time.

So many benefits!

Lu Ye smiled and patted him on the shoulder, "It will get even better in the future!"

He also warned, "Find reliable people to handle this, and don't embezzle anything privately. If I find out in the future, there will be no leniency."

The Sect Master immediately nodded, "Rest assured, I will personally oversee it."

Lu Ye swiftly departed and soon arrived at the core area, waving his hand, "Stand down, no need to keep watch here."

Xiang Yin and sister took the order and headed straight for the Nine Provinces.

Lu Ye stood in front of the core, pondered for a moment, and eventually flashed and entered the core world.

In the Origin space, Lu Ye sat cross-legged before the Origin that resembled a small sun.

At the last moment of the Black Abyss confrontation, the Origin, under Veteran Fang's control, rushed into Lu Ye's Divine Sea, and Lu Ye spent three years barely refining it.

Within the Origin, the consciousness of Veteran Fang and the consciousness of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood were thoroughly refined.

It could be said that the present Origin was very pure, with no residual saintliness power. Thus, Lu Ye didn't need to busy himself further.

But the problem is, the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood had eroded Mount Fangcun's core for so many years, and the erosion wasn't just limited to the Origin.

The Origin was the key focus of the treasure blood's erosion because if it could erode the Origin away, the treasure blood's consciousness could control the core world.

Yet throughout the core world, besides the Origin being eroded, the entire domain still retained traces of the treasure blood's power. Not to mention, even now, from time to time, there would be a rain of blood in the core world, though not as frequent as before.

Lu Ye also personally investigated the spirit jade vein in the core world, which was likewise contaminated with saintliness power.

If these remnants of saintliness power in the core world are not thoroughly cleared, no one can predict what changes might occur once the three sections of Mount Fangcun fully integrate with the core, or whether there will be any saintliness power infecting the Dwarf Race cultivators.

If that happens, all the Dwarf Race would turn into the first generation Blood Race, which would undoubtedly be a tragedy and an unacceptable event for the Dwarf Race.

So what Lu Ye needs to do now is to completely purify the entire Core World before the three parts of Mount Fangcun merge over.

Under normal circumstances, he couldn't achieve this. Let alone him being just a Moon Jade, even a Sun Blaze coming here would find this task as difficult as climbing to the sky.

But after all, he has refined the core origin. With the help of Origin Power, he can clearly perceive every corner of the Core World, which makes the impossible possible!

Simply put, with the help of the core origin, he can extend the power of the Talent Tree to any part of the Core World, thereby refining the saintliness power lingering in this world cleanly.

This is not something that can be accomplished in a day or two. Lu Ye is mentally prepared for this, and he has prepared enough Talent Tree fuel, so there is no need to worry about a shortage of fuel.

Sinking his mind, relying on the core origin, Lu Ye radiated the power of the Talent Tree in all directions, gradually eroding the saintliness power lingering within the domain.

Time flowed by, with no knowledge of the changes in the sun and moon.

One day, Lu Ye suddenly sensed a violent tremor coming from the Core World, causing him to frown.

Before entering the Origin Space, he had already sealed the Core World, fearing someone might intrude. It wasn't that they would disturb him, but anyone entering might get tainted by the saintliness left by the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood.

He had already informed the Nine Provinces Governor's Hall, so no Nine Provinces cultivator should disregard his warning, and Xiang Yin and her sister certainly wouldn't defy him.

In confusion, Lu Ye extended his Mental Consciousness to investigate, wanting to see who was triggering the seal of the Core World.

He was soon surprised because Xiang Yin, her sister, Yang Ling, and Hu Dequan were all present beside the core, along with two other familiar figures.

At this moment, Xiang Yin and her sister were trembling because they could feel a powerful Mental Consciousness enveloping them, full of hostility, giving them the feeling they might die here at any moment.

The source of the Mental Consciousness was a cultivator in a blue robe, whose powerful aura revealed his identity as a Sun Blaze. Beside him, a graceful and poised woman stood quietly, speaking softly with Yang Ling and Hu Dequan.

Xiang Yin and her sister quickly realized the origins of these two Sun Blaze cultivators—they were from the Dwarf Race!

Suddenly, ripples appeared above the core, and Lu Ye's figure emerged.

Xiang Yin and her sister immediately sent hopeful glances towards him.

With a swift glance, Lu Ye understood what had happened. The Dwarf Race and the Blood Race are old enemies. Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing had come here to investigate the core, and Xiang Yin and her sister, unaware of the situation, tried to prevent them, thereby exposing their identity as the first generation of the Blood Race, and were subsequently subdued on the spot by Chen Xuanhai.

"Senior Brother Chen, Senior Sister Su!" Lu Ye stepped forward to greet them.

Su Yuqing, who was speaking with Yang Ling and Hu Dequan, turned her head towards him, smiling brightly, which stunned Yang Ling and Hu Dequan, as this Sun Blaze had been rather serious until now.

Hearing Lu Ye's address for the two Sun Blaze cultivators...the two couldn't help but recall the scene of meeting Lu Ye for the first time.

This person...is indeed a Master Uncle, though we were calling each other brothers before. In the future, our seniority might just drop a level.

Chen Xuanhai also glanced at Lu Ye, nodding slightly, and praised, "Well done!"

Throughout this hasty journey, both he and Su Yuqing had been somewhat uneasy, as no one could be sure if things were as they presumed before seeing the core with their own eyes.

It wasn't until they reached here, seeing the core placed right there!

Even though they had never seen the core, the deep-seated sensation within them couldn't be fake. This thing resembling an artificial hill was undoubtedly the core that the Dwarf Race lost countless years ago.

Think about it, Lu Ye is indeed a benefactor to the Dwarf Race, especially to the eastern part. He helped them win the Black Abyss Martial Arts Meet back then, and now he has helped them retrieve an essential item.

A mere compliment can't express the gratitude of the Dwarf Race. Fortunately, Junior Sister Su had the foresight to become his Dao companion early on, making Lu Ye half a member of the Dwarf Race, so contributing to the clan is only right.

"Senior Brother, you overpraise." Lu Ye said modestly, looking at Xiang Yin and her sister struggling, and said, "Senior Brother, please release them. They are my people."

Su Yuqing smiled gently, narrowing her eyes slightly, "Your people?"

Lu Ye suddenly felt a chill down his spine and hurriedly explained, "They are my subordinates. During the struggle for the core, they also contributed significantly."

"Oh?" Chen Xuanhai raised an eyebrow, not understanding what was going on, but he still released the suppression on Xiang Yin and her sister.

The two sisters staggered slightly, feeling as if they had narrowly escaped death.

Su Yuqing asked, "Did you just say a struggle for the core? With whom?"

Lu Ye sighed, "It's a long story; should we find a place to talk slowly?"

"Alright." Su Yuqing nodded. She was also curious about how Lu Ye managed to bring the core out of the marvel.

"If the two Master Uncles don't mind, you can come with me and Brother Hu. We have found a place to stay in this domain. It's not big, but it's quiet." Yang Ling suggested.

"Let's go." Chen Xuanhai, with hands behind his back, gestured for Yang Ling to lead the way.



============================================================
Chapter 1818: Chapter 1818 1816: I Didn't Tell You to Refine It
============================================================

On a towering spirit mountaintop in Dingzhou, as far as the eye could see, a sea of clouds surged and shifted, resembling a fairyland.

Lu Ye's voice continually rang out, occasionally supplemented by Yang Ling and Hu Dequan.

Gradually, everything that had happened in the Core World was completely revealed before Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing.

When they learned that the Red Talisman Society had been hiding in the Core World for years, facing enemies many times more powerful, and with Sun Blaze sitting among them, yet they had not submitted, both Sun Blaze nodded slightly.

The foreign cultivators they had chosen back then had been selected after a long period of observation and training. Looking back now, most of these dispatched cultivators were trustworthy.

Upon learning that the treasure blood of the Blood Ancestor in the Core World had developed spiritual intelligence, Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing couldn't help but change their expressions.

They also didn't know that a drop of the treasure blood of the Blood Ancestor had remained in the Core World, and that the blood had actually nurtured spiritual intelligence, aiming to stain the core origin.

However, they finally understood why Moon Jade of the Dwarf Race found nothing whenever she went searching. According to Lu Ye's speculation, it was because the core origin protected the Dwarf Race cultivators, preventing them from entering the Core World. Whenever a Dwarf Race cultivator entered the marvel, the Core World would avoid them.

The foreign cultivators they sent did not receive this kind of treatment. Some encountered the core and wandered in, while others returned empty-handed.

Through the gentle narration, the whole process of the final battle in the origin space was made known to the two Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race.

After Lu Ye finished speaking, both Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai's expressions turned peculiar.

Chen Xuanhai looked at him with surprise and doubt: "So, at the final moment of that battle, the core consciousness used itself as a cage to imprison the treasure blood consciousness, and then you refined them all?"

"Yes!"

Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing exchanged a glance, seeing what was on each other's mind, and then Chen Xuanhai cautiously asked, "After refining the origin, what changes have you noticed?"

Lu Ye said, "Not much change in myself, but I can easily control the Core World with the origin, and I can also mobilize the Core World's essence. On the way back, I encountered an insect hive, and with this method, I sealed an Insect Race Sun Blaze in the Core World and destroyed it."

Despite having anticipated it, Chen Xuanhai couldn't help but feel amused when Lu Ye said this. As for the Insect Race Sun Blaze being killed, though significant, it was not much compared to the current situation.

Seeing Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing's expressions turning somewhat odd, Lu Ye suspiciously asked, "What's wrong? Is there something inappropriate?"

Chen Xuanhai opened his mouth as if finding it difficult to speak, and finally, he waved his hand, "Junior Sister, you tell him."

Su Yuqing nodded, looked at Lu Ye with gentle eyes, and said, "Lu Ye, during your travels in the stellar space, have you heard of the title World Lord?"

"Yes!" Lu Ye nodded.

In the Indeterminate World of the four galaxies, Jyang Shang was a World Lord, and in the Jade Conch World, there was also a World Lord called Qiu Wu.

Su Yuqing continued, "There are actually two types of World Lords: True World Masters and False World Lords."

Lu Ye was puzzled, "There's such a distinction? How can one tell the difference?"

Su Yuqing explained, "The biggest difference between true and false World Lords is whether they have refined the origin of a world! Those who have not refined a world's origin, called World Lords, are merely respected by the local cultivators. They might be the strongest or the most esteemed in the world, but either way, they do not have many advantages in their world. True World Masters, on the other hand, having refined the origin of the world, can mobilize the essence of their world at will, as you did when suppressing the Insect Race Sun Blaze. At a thought, they can even change the world drastically or break it apart. Such a World Lord is truly the master of that world."

As Su Yuqing spoke, she looked at Lu Ye with a complex expression in her eyes.

Chen Xuanhai also watched him with a similar expression, unable to help but curse internally.

Sending Lu Ye to the Demon Eye Marvel was meant for him to explore information about the core. The Dwarf Race hadn't held much hope since generations of Dwarves had tried for ages without success. As long as Lu Ye could uncover some intelligence about the core, it would be a tremendous gain.

No one expected that in just a few years, only at the Moon Jade Mid-Stage, Lu Ye would actually bring the core out of the marvel. Not only that, but he also refined the core origin and became the core's master!

The core's return is a good thing, but having a master for the core is not, especially since the master is not of Dwarf Race descent!

It's imaginable that when the three parts of Mount Fangcun merge, Lu Ye, as the master of the core, would naturally become the master of the entire Mount Fangcun!

This was what the Blood Ancestor coveted back in the day, but never achieved.

They asked you to find the core, not to refine it!

With two Sun Blaze eyes fixed on him, Lu Ye blinked, realizing something, and turned to Chen Xuanhai, declaring righteously, "Rest assured, Senior Brother, though I am of the human race, since I am Dao companions with Yuqing, my heart is surely aligned with our Dwarf Race. I will never do anything to betray the Dwarf Race. My loyalty is as clear as the heavens and earth, the sun and moon bear witness!" He spoke while reaching out to hold Su Yuqing's hand, grasping it firmly.

Su Yuqing immediately blushed deeply, struggled hard for a moment, but couldn't free herself...

Yang Ling and Hu Dequan were shocked, hurriedly looking up at the sky or down at their feet...

Xiang Yin and sister also averted their gaze in time.

Chen Xuanhai felt a headache coming on... Just a moment ago, when they first met, Lu Ye addressed Su Yuqing as Senior Sister. Now that he's aware of the importance, he calls her Yuqing. This person is too realistic.

Taking a few deep breaths, Chen Xuanhai finally managed to steady his somewhat chaotic breathing. After pondering for a while, he said, "This matter is of great importance, it must be immediately reported to the others."

He also knew that Lu Ye's refining of the core origin was not intentional, because according to Lu Ye's previous accounts, it was the Origin Consciousness guiding him. Otherwise, how could Lu Ye, a Moon Jade Mid-Stage, possibly refine the core?

When Mount Fangcun was intact in the past, it wasn't that no Insect Race Sun Blaze from the Dwarf Race tried refining the origin, but none succeeded.

Mount Fangcun... that is a stellar space supreme treasure! How could it be casually refined by someone?

Lu Ye's refining was a huge coincidence, the erosion of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, the weakening of the Origin Consciousness, and the choice at the critical moment of life and death, all these created the reality of a Moon Jade Mid-Stage achieving the status of the core master.

Looking throughout history, such an event has never happened before.

But no matter what, this monumental event still needs to be immediately reported to the Sun Blaze of the other two divisions, and at this moment, surely everyone is waiting for their news.

With a flushed face, Su Yuqing nodded slightly, then turned to Lu Ye and said, "Go to the core."

Lu Ye felt a pinch in the palm of his hand and immediately nodded, "Then let's go."

The group then hurried towards the core area again.

Halfway there, Su Yuqing transmitted an audio message: "Don't worry, since you've refined the origin, you are the rightful Origin Lord. When Mount Fangcun merges in the future, you will also be the master of the entire Mount Fangcun. The Dwarf Race will not be hostile towards you, but this matter is of great significance, and they need some time to accept it."

Lu Ye nodded, "I'm not worried."

He actually hadn't realized these issues before, but after hearing Su Yuqing's explanation, he understood how significant his refining of the origin was to the Dwarf Race.

From another perspective, if a foreign clan cultivator suddenly refined the origin of the Nine Provinces and became the master of the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye and other cultivators would certainly find it hard to remain calm, even if that foreign clan cultivator made great contributions to the Nine Provinces.

In a short while, they reached a spacious area in the Core World.

Lu Ye stood quietly to the side, waiting. Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai were busy setting up a complex big array.

Lu Ye knew that cultivators of each division in Mount Fangcun could travel back and forth at some cost. Previously, he had traveled from the Western Region to the Eastern Region.

But such travel not only required resources but also certain special methods, and only the Dwarf Race could utilize these methods within Mount Fangcun.

No one else could use them.

The formation being set up in front of them was undoubtedly something like a bridge.

After being busy for several days, the two Sun Blaze finally completed their work. Su Yuqing looked up towards Lu Ye, "You just wait outside."

Lu Ye nodded.

The next moment, the two Sun Blaze's Mental Consciousness surged, and as the powerful Soul Power fluctuated and spread, Lu Ye immediately felt immense pressure and couldn't help but step back.

The array runes of the setup big array shimmered and gradually transformed into light, enveloping the figures of the two Sun Blaze.

In a phantom hall, the blurred figures of Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing began to appear, and only after they completely solidified did they transmit a message through special means.

Soon, one after another, illusory figures similar to theirs appeared in the hall.

Months later, the Sun Blaze from the three divisions gathered again.

Someone urgently asked, "Have you arrived? What is the situation now?"

Before Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing could answer, someone responded, "Since Senior Brother Chen and Junior Sister Su can project here, they must already be at the core. Our Junior Brother Lu is truly amazing, he actually managed to bring out the core, hahaha!"

Upon these words, the emotions of the many Sun Blaze reached a high. Just as the person said, since Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing could project themselves here, they must have entered the Core World; otherwise, such a feat would not be possible.

Moreover, considering the timing, they indeed should have reached the Jade Conch by now.

For a moment, the atmosphere was warm, and the Sun Blaze from each division were in good spirits.

"Senior Brother Chen, go ahead?" said the first Sun Blaze to speak.

Chen Xuanhai nodded and began to recount the information he had learned from Lu Ye. Many Sun Blaze listened attentively.

When they heard that Lu Ye had actually refined the core and now became the Origin Lord, the group of Sun Blaze was instantly dumbfounded.



============================================================
Chapter 1817: Chapter 1817 1815: Your People?
============================================================

Lu Ye didn't stay long on Three Worlds Island, only for half a month, but the spirit jade reserve on Three Worlds Island cost nearly two hundred million.

This is also why he doesn't worry much about accounting issues, because whenever he has a need, the warehouse on Three Worlds Island will open to him without limit, and neither Luan Xiao'e nor Tang Jun will say anything about it.

There was enough replenishment for the Talent Tree's fuel reserve, and Lu Ye even left a batch of fire-type resources as a backup.

During this period, he also took time to visit Hua Ci in the merfolk territory. Unfortunately, after several years, the amber sealing Hua Ci remained unchanged, with no significant transformation.

The only thing that delighted Lu Ye was that he could sense Hua Ci's strength had greatly improved.

This is not hard to understand because, in Lu Ye's perception, the amber that sealed Hua Ci had been continuously absorbing the sea water of All Phenomena Ocean, seemingly possessing a refining capability. Even though this refining efficiency didn't match that of the Talent Tree, it was much more terrifying than the efficiency of a cultivator's normal cultivation.

Undoubtedly, part of the energy produced after refining the sea water of All Phenomena Ocean was used by Hua Ci, and naturally, her strength could improve.

Compared to Hua Ci's improvement, the enhancement of the Pixiu she held seemed even more terrifying...

Lu Ye was eagerly anticipating the state Hua Ci would be in after being unsealed.

Half a month after returning to All Phenomena Ocean, Lu Ye set off on the journey back to the Nine Provinces.

This journey was already very familiar to him.

In a swift twenty days, he returned to the Nine Provinces once again.

Xiang Yin and sister diligently guarded near the core, but Yang Ling and Hu Dequan were nowhere to be seen. According to Xiang Yin, they had already entered the Nine Provinces, but what they were doing there was unknown.

A short while later, in the Nine Provinces Governor's Palace, Lu Ye placed a large pile of storage rings on the table in front of him, jingling for quite a while.

The current Nine Provinces Governor, originally the Sect Master of a certain sect in Leizhou, widened his eyes in astonishment, "Brother Lu, what's going on here?" As he spoke, he picked up a storage ring and probed inside with his Mental Consciousness, almost blinded by the sight.

The ring was filled with spirit jade.

"This..." The Sect Master was shocked.

He picked up another storage ring and exclaimed again, "Ah, this..." Inside was also a large amount of spirit jade.

"Stop fussing." Lu Ye interrupted him, "These are resources brought back from Three Worlds Island. Get some people over to count them, then divide them into three parts. Our Nine Provinces will keep one part, and the other two will be sent to Qingli Dao World and Jade Conch World."

The Sect Master could hardly believe it, "Has our Three Worlds Island developed this well?"

Though the Nine Provinces had heard of the matters regarding All Phenomena Ocean for over a decade, and the first batch of cultivators had gone there some years ago, the local cultivators who stayed behind hadn't really obtained any tangible benefits from All Phenomena Ocean. This was the first time.

So many benefits!

Lu Ye smiled and patted him on the shoulder, "It will get even better in the future!"

He also warned, "Find reliable people to handle this, and don't embezzle anything privately. If I find out in the future, there will be no leniency."

The Sect Master immediately nodded, "Rest assured, I will personally oversee it."

Lu Ye swiftly departed and soon arrived at the core area, waving his hand, "Stand down, no need to keep watch here."

Xiang Yin and sister took the order and headed straight for the Nine Provinces.

Lu Ye stood in front of the core, pondered for a moment, and eventually flashed and entered the core world.

In the Origin space, Lu Ye sat cross-legged before the Origin that resembled a small sun.

At the last moment of the Black Abyss confrontation, the Origin, under Veteran Fang's control, rushed into Lu Ye's Divine Sea, and Lu Ye spent three years barely refining it.

Within the Origin, the consciousness of Veteran Fang and the consciousness of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood were thoroughly refined.

It could be said that the present Origin was very pure, with no residual saintliness power. Thus, Lu Ye didn't need to busy himself further.

But the problem is, the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood had eroded Mount Fangcun's core for so many years, and the erosion wasn't just limited to the Origin.

The Origin was the key focus of the treasure blood's erosion because if it could erode the Origin away, the treasure blood's consciousness could control the core world.

Yet throughout the core world, besides the Origin being eroded, the entire domain still retained traces of the treasure blood's power. Not to mention, even now, from time to time, there would be a rain of blood in the core world, though not as frequent as before.

Lu Ye also personally investigated the spirit jade vein in the core world, which was likewise contaminated with saintliness power.

If these remnants of saintliness power in the core world are not thoroughly cleared, no one can predict what changes might occur once the three sections of Mount Fangcun fully integrate with the core, or whether there will be any saintliness power infecting the Dwarf Race cultivators.

If that happens, all the Dwarf Race would turn into the first generation Blood Race, which would undoubtedly be a tragedy and an unacceptable event for the Dwarf Race.

So what Lu Ye needs to do now is to completely purify the entire Core World before the three parts of Mount Fangcun merge over.

Under normal circumstances, he couldn't achieve this. Let alone him being just a Moon Jade, even a Sun Blaze coming here would find this task as difficult as climbing to the sky.

But after all, he has refined the core origin. With the help of Origin Power, he can clearly perceive every corner of the Core World, which makes the impossible possible!

Simply put, with the help of the core origin, he can extend the power of the Talent Tree to any part of the Core World, thereby refining the saintliness power lingering in this world cleanly.

This is not something that can be accomplished in a day or two. Lu Ye is mentally prepared for this, and he has prepared enough Talent Tree fuel, so there is no need to worry about a shortage of fuel.

Sinking his mind, relying on the core origin, Lu Ye radiated the power of the Talent Tree in all directions, gradually eroding the saintliness power lingering within the domain.

Time flowed by, with no knowledge of the changes in the sun and moon.

One day, Lu Ye suddenly sensed a violent tremor coming from the Core World, causing him to frown.

Before entering the Origin Space, he had already sealed the Core World, fearing someone might intrude. It wasn't that they would disturb him, but anyone entering might get tainted by the saintliness left by the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood.

He had already informed the Nine Provinces Governor's Hall, so no Nine Provinces cultivator should disregard his warning, and Xiang Yin and her sister certainly wouldn't defy him.

In confusion, Lu Ye extended his Mental Consciousness to investigate, wanting to see who was triggering the seal of the Core World.

He was soon surprised because Xiang Yin, her sister, Yang Ling, and Hu Dequan were all present beside the core, along with two other familiar figures.

At this moment, Xiang Yin and her sister were trembling because they could feel a powerful Mental Consciousness enveloping them, full of hostility, giving them the feeling they might die here at any moment.

The source of the Mental Consciousness was a cultivator in a blue robe, whose powerful aura revealed his identity as a Sun Blaze. Beside him, a graceful and poised woman stood quietly, speaking softly with Yang Ling and Hu Dequan.

Xiang Yin and her sister quickly realized the origins of these two Sun Blaze cultivators—they were from the Dwarf Race!

Xiang Yin and her sister immediately sent hopeful glances towards him.

This person...is indeed a Master Uncle, though we were calling each other brothers before. In the future, our seniority might just drop a level.

It wasn't until they reached here, seeing the core placed right there!

Even though they had never seen the core, the deep-seated sensation within them couldn't be fake. This thing resembling an artificial hill was undoubtedly the core that the Dwarf Race lost countless years ago.

Think about it, Lu Ye is indeed a benefactor to the Dwarf Race, especially to the eastern part. He helped them win the Black Abyss Martial Arts Meet back then, and now he has helped them retrieve an essential item.

A mere compliment can't express the gratitude of the Dwarf Race. Fortunately, Junior Sister Su had the foresight to become his Dao companion early on, making Lu Ye half a member of the Dwarf Race, so contributing to the clan is only right.

"Senior Brother, you overpraise." Lu Ye said modestly, looking at Xiang Yin and her sister struggling, and said, "Senior Brother, please release them. They are my people."

Su Yuqing smiled gently, narrowing her eyes slightly, "Your people?"

Lu Ye suddenly felt a chill down his spine and hurriedly explained, "They are my subordinates. During the struggle for the core, they also contributed significantly."

"Oh?" Chen Xuanhai raised an eyebrow, not understanding what was going on, but he still released the suppression on Xiang Yin and her sister.

The two sisters staggered slightly, feeling as if they had narrowly escaped death.

Su Yuqing asked, "Did you just say a struggle for the core? With whom?"

Lu Ye sighed, "It's a long story; should we find a place to talk slowly?"

"Alright." Su Yuqing nodded. She was also curious about how Lu Ye managed to bring the core out of the marvel.

"If the two Master Uncles don't mind, you can come with me and Brother Hu. We have found a place to stay in this domain. It's not big, but it's quiet." Yang Ling suggested.

"Let's go." Chen Xuanhai, with hands behind his back, gestured for Yang Ling to lead the way.

When Mount Fangcun was intact in the past, it wasn't that no Insect Race Sun Blaze from the Dwarf Race tried refining the origin, but none succeeded.

Mount Fangcun... that is a stellar space supreme treasure! How could it be casually refined by someone?

Lu Ye's refining was a huge coincidence, the erosion of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, the weakening of the Origin Consciousness, and the choice at the critical moment of life and death, all these created the reality of a Moon Jade Mid-Stage achieving the status of the core master.

Looking throughout history, such an event has never happened before.

But no matter what, this monumental event still needs to be immediately reported to the Sun Blaze of the other two divisions, and at this moment, surely everyone is waiting for their news.

With a flushed face, Su Yuqing nodded slightly, then turned to Lu Ye and said, "Go to the core."

Lu Ye felt a pinch in the palm of his hand and immediately nodded, "Then let's go."

The group then hurried towards the core area again.

Halfway there, Su Yuqing transmitted an audio message: "Don't worry, since you've refined the origin, you are the rightful Origin Lord. When Mount Fangcun merges in the future, you will also be the master of the entire Mount Fangcun. The Dwarf Race will not be hostile towards you, but this matter is of great significance, and they need some time to accept it."

Lu Ye nodded, "I'm not worried."

He actually hadn't realized these issues before, but after hearing Su Yuqing's explanation, he understood how significant his refining of the origin was to the Dwarf Race.

From another perspective, if a foreign clan cultivator suddenly refined the origin of the Nine Provinces and became the master of the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye and other cultivators would certainly find it hard to remain calm, even if that foreign clan cultivator made great contributions to the Nine Provinces.

In a short while, they reached a spacious area in the Core World.

Lu Ye stood quietly to the side, waiting. Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai were busy setting up a complex big array.

Lu Ye knew that cultivators of each division in Mount Fangcun could travel back and forth at some cost. Previously, he had traveled from the Western Region to the Eastern Region.

But such travel not only required resources but also certain special methods, and only the Dwarf Race could utilize these methods within Mount Fangcun.

No one else could use them.

The formation being set up in front of them was undoubtedly something like a bridge.

After being busy for several days, the two Sun Blaze finally completed their work. Su Yuqing looked up towards Lu Ye, "You just wait outside."

Lu Ye nodded.

The next moment, the two Sun Blaze's Mental Consciousness surged, and as the powerful Soul Power fluctuated and spread, Lu Ye immediately felt immense pressure and couldn't help but step back.

The array runes of the setup big array shimmered and gradually transformed into light, enveloping the figures of the two Sun Blaze.

In a phantom hall, the blurred figures of Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing began to appear, and only after they completely solidified did they transmit a message through special means.

Soon, one after another, illusory figures similar to theirs appeared in the hall.

Months later, the Sun Blaze from the three divisions gathered again.

Someone urgently asked, "Have you arrived? What is the situation now?"

Before Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing could answer, someone responded, "Since Senior Brother Chen and Junior Sister Su can project here, they must already be at the core. Our Junior Brother Lu is truly amazing, he actually managed to bring out the core, hahaha!"

Upon these words, the emotions of the many Sun Blaze reached a high. Just as the person said, since Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing could project themselves here, they must have entered the Core World; otherwise, such a feat would not be possible.

Moreover, considering the timing, they indeed should have reached the Jade Conch by now.

For a moment, the atmosphere was warm, and the Sun Blaze from each division were in good spirits.

"Senior Brother Chen, go ahead?" said the first Sun Blaze to speak.

Chen Xuanhai nodded and began to recount the information he had learned from Lu Ye. Many Sun Blaze listened attentively.

When they heard that Lu Ye had actually refined the core and now became the Origin Lord, the group of Sun Blaze was instantly dumbfounded.



============================================================
Chapter 1818: Chapter 1818 1816: I Didn't Tell You to Refine It
============================================================

On a towering spirit mountaintop in Dingzhou, as far as the eye could see, a sea of clouds surged and shifted, resembling a fairyland.

Lu Ye's voice continually rang out, occasionally supplemented by Yang Ling and Hu Dequan.

Gradually, everything that had happened in the Core World was completely revealed before Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing.

When they learned that the Red Talisman Society had been hiding in the Core World for years, facing enemies many times more powerful, and with Sun Blaze sitting among them, yet they had not submitted, both Sun Blaze nodded slightly.

The foreign cultivators they had chosen back then had been selected after a long period of observation and training. Looking back now, most of these dispatched cultivators were trustworthy.

Upon learning that the treasure blood of the Blood Ancestor in the Core World had developed spiritual intelligence, Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing couldn't help but change their expressions.

They also didn't know that a drop of the treasure blood of the Blood Ancestor had remained in the Core World, and that the blood had actually nurtured spiritual intelligence, aiming to stain the core origin.

However, they finally understood why Moon Jade of the Dwarf Race found nothing whenever she went searching. According to Lu Ye's speculation, it was because the core origin protected the Dwarf Race cultivators, preventing them from entering the Core World. Whenever a Dwarf Race cultivator entered the marvel, the Core World would avoid them.

The foreign cultivators they sent did not receive this kind of treatment. Some encountered the core and wandered in, while others returned empty-handed.

Through the gentle narration, the whole process of the final battle in the origin space was made known to the two Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race.

After Lu Ye finished speaking, both Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai's expressions turned peculiar.

Chen Xuanhai looked at him with surprise and doubt: "So, at the final moment of that battle, the core consciousness used itself as a cage to imprison the treasure blood consciousness, and then you refined them all?"

"Yes!"

Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing exchanged a glance, seeing what was on each other's mind, and then Chen Xuanhai cautiously asked, "After refining the origin, what changes have you noticed?"

Lu Ye said, "Not much change in myself, but I can easily control the Core World with the origin, and I can also mobilize the Core World's essence. On the way back, I encountered an insect hive, and with this method, I sealed an Insect Race Sun Blaze in the Core World and destroyed it."

Despite having anticipated it, Chen Xuanhai couldn't help but feel amused when Lu Ye said this. As for the Insect Race Sun Blaze being killed, though significant, it was not much compared to the current situation.

Seeing Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing's expressions turning somewhat odd, Lu Ye suspiciously asked, "What's wrong? Is there something inappropriate?"

Chen Xuanhai opened his mouth as if finding it difficult to speak, and finally, he waved his hand, "Junior Sister, you tell him."

Su Yuqing nodded, looked at Lu Ye with gentle eyes, and said, "Lu Ye, during your travels in the stellar space, have you heard of the title World Lord?"

"Yes!" Lu Ye nodded.

In the Indeterminate World of the four galaxies, Jyang Shang was a World Lord, and in the Jade Conch World, there was also a World Lord called Qiu Wu.

Su Yuqing continued, "There are actually two types of World Lords: True World Masters and False World Lords."

Lu Ye was puzzled, "There's such a distinction? How can one tell the difference?"

Su Yuqing explained, "The biggest difference between true and false World Lords is whether they have refined the origin of a world! Those who have not refined a world's origin, called World Lords, are merely respected by the local cultivators. They might be the strongest or the most esteemed in the world, but either way, they do not have many advantages in their world. True World Masters, on the other hand, having refined the origin of the world, can mobilize the essence of their world at will, as you did when suppressing the Insect Race Sun Blaze. At a thought, they can even change the world drastically or break it apart. Such a World Lord is truly the master of that world."

As Su Yuqing spoke, she looked at Lu Ye with a complex expression in her eyes.

Chen Xuanhai also watched him with a similar expression, unable to help but curse internally.

Sending Lu Ye to the Demon Eye Marvel was meant for him to explore information about the core. The Dwarf Race hadn't held much hope since generations of Dwarves had tried for ages without success. As long as Lu Ye could uncover some intelligence about the core, it would be a tremendous gain.

No one expected that in just a few years, only at the Moon Jade Mid-Stage, Lu Ye would actually bring the core out of the marvel. Not only that, but he also refined the core origin and became the core's master!

The core's return is a good thing, but having a master for the core is not, especially since the master is not of Dwarf Race descent!

It's imaginable that when the three parts of Mount Fangcun merge, Lu Ye, as the master of the core, would naturally become the master of the entire Mount Fangcun!

This was what the Blood Ancestor coveted back in the day, but never achieved.

They asked you to find the core, not to refine it!

With two Sun Blaze eyes fixed on him, Lu Ye blinked, realizing something, and turned to Chen Xuanhai, declaring righteously, "Rest assured, Senior Brother, though I am of the human race, since I am Dao companions with Yuqing, my heart is surely aligned with our Dwarf Race. I will never do anything to betray the Dwarf Race. My loyalty is as clear as the heavens and earth, the sun and moon bear witness!" He spoke while reaching out to hold Su Yuqing's hand, grasping it firmly.

Su Yuqing immediately blushed deeply, struggled hard for a moment, but couldn't free herself...

Yang Ling and Hu Dequan were shocked, hurriedly looking up at the sky or down at their feet...

Xiang Yin and sister also averted their gaze in time.

Chen Xuanhai felt a headache coming on... Just a moment ago, when they first met, Lu Ye addressed Su Yuqing as Senior Sister. Now that he's aware of the importance, he calls her Yuqing. This person is too realistic.

Taking a few deep breaths, Chen Xuanhai finally managed to steady his somewhat chaotic breathing. After pondering for a while, he said, "This matter is of great importance, it must be immediately reported to the others."

He also knew that Lu Ye's refining of the core origin was not intentional, because according to Lu Ye's previous accounts, it was the Origin Consciousness guiding him. Otherwise, how could Lu Ye, a Moon Jade Mid-Stage, possibly refine the core?

When Mount Fangcun was intact in the past, it wasn't that no Insect Race Sun Blaze from the Dwarf Race tried refining the origin, but none succeeded.

Mount Fangcun... that is a stellar space supreme treasure! How could it be casually refined by someone?

Lu Ye's refining was a huge coincidence, the erosion of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, the weakening of the Origin Consciousness, and the choice at the critical moment of life and death, all these created the reality of a Moon Jade Mid-Stage achieving the status of the core master.

Looking throughout history, such an event has never happened before.

But no matter what, this monumental event still needs to be immediately reported to the Sun Blaze of the other two divisions, and at this moment, surely everyone is waiting for their news.

With a flushed face, Su Yuqing nodded slightly, then turned to Lu Ye and said, "Go to the core."

Lu Ye felt a pinch in the palm of his hand and immediately nodded, "Then let's go."

The group then hurried towards the core area again.

Halfway there, Su Yuqing transmitted an audio message: "Don't worry, since you've refined the origin, you are the rightful Origin Lord. When Mount Fangcun merges in the future, you will also be the master of the entire Mount Fangcun. The Dwarf Race will not be hostile towards you, but this matter is of great significance, and they need some time to accept it."

Lu Ye nodded, "I'm not worried."

He actually hadn't realized these issues before, but after hearing Su Yuqing's explanation, he understood how significant his refining of the origin was to the Dwarf Race.

From another perspective, if a foreign clan cultivator suddenly refined the origin of the Nine Provinces and became the master of the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye and other cultivators would certainly find it hard to remain calm, even if that foreign clan cultivator made great contributions to the Nine Provinces.

In a short while, they reached a spacious area in the Core World.

Lu Ye stood quietly to the side, waiting. Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai were busy setting up a complex big array.

Lu Ye knew that cultivators of each division in Mount Fangcun could travel back and forth at some cost. Previously, he had traveled from the Western Region to the Eastern Region.

But such travel not only required resources but also certain special methods, and only the Dwarf Race could utilize these methods within Mount Fangcun.

No one else could use them.

The formation being set up in front of them was undoubtedly something like a bridge.

After being busy for several days, the two Sun Blaze finally completed their work. Su Yuqing looked up towards Lu Ye, "You just wait outside."

Lu Ye nodded.

The next moment, the two Sun Blaze's Mental Consciousness surged, and as the powerful Soul Power fluctuated and spread, Lu Ye immediately felt immense pressure and couldn't help but step back.

The array runes of the setup big array shimmered and gradually transformed into light, enveloping the figures of the two Sun Blaze.

In a phantom hall, the blurred figures of Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing began to appear, and only after they completely solidified did they transmit a message through special means.

Soon, one after another, illusory figures similar to theirs appeared in the hall.

Months later, the Sun Blaze from the three divisions gathered again.

Someone urgently asked, "Have you arrived? What is the situation now?"

Before Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing could answer, someone responded, "Since Senior Brother Chen and Junior Sister Su can project here, they must already be at the core. Our Junior Brother Lu is truly amazing, he actually managed to bring out the core, hahaha!"

Upon these words, the emotions of the many Sun Blaze reached a high. Just as the person said, since Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing could project themselves here, they must have entered the Core World; otherwise, such a feat would not be possible.

Moreover, considering the timing, they indeed should have reached the Jade Conch by now.

For a moment, the atmosphere was warm, and the Sun Blaze from each division were in good spirits.

"Senior Brother Chen, go ahead?" said the first Sun Blaze to speak.

Chen Xuanhai nodded and began to recount the information he had learned from Lu Ye. Many Sun Blaze listened attentively.

When they heard that Lu Ye had actually refined the core and now became the Origin Lord, the group of Sun Blaze was instantly dumbfounded.

Mount Fangcun... that is a stellar space supreme treasure! How could it be casually refined by someone?

Lu Ye's refining was a huge coincidence, the erosion of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, the weakening of the Origin Consciousness, and the choice at the critical moment of life and death, all these created the reality of a Moon Jade Mid-Stage achieving the status of the core master.

Looking throughout history, such an event has never happened before.

But no matter what, this monumental event still needs to be immediately reported to the Sun Blaze of the other two divisions, and at this moment, surely everyone is waiting for their news.

With a flushed face, Su Yuqing nodded slightly, then turned to Lu Ye and said, "Go to the core."

Lu Ye felt a pinch in the palm of his hand and immediately nodded, "Then let's go."

The group then hurried towards the core area again.

Halfway there, Su Yuqing transmitted an audio message: "Don't worry, since you've refined the origin, you are the rightful Origin Lord. When Mount Fangcun merges in the future, you will also be the master of the entire Mount Fangcun. The Dwarf Race will not be hostile towards you, but this matter is of great significance, and they need some time to accept it."

Lu Ye nodded, "I'm not worried."

He actually hadn't realized these issues before, but after hearing Su Yuqing's explanation, he understood how significant his refining of the origin was to the Dwarf Race.

From another perspective, if a foreign clan cultivator suddenly refined the origin of the Nine Provinces and became the master of the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye and other cultivators would certainly find it hard to remain calm, even if that foreign clan cultivator made great contributions to the Nine Provinces.

In a short while, they reached a spacious area in the Core World.

Lu Ye stood quietly to the side, waiting. Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai were busy setting up a complex big array.

Lu Ye knew that cultivators of each division in Mount Fangcun could travel back and forth at some cost. Previously, he had traveled from the Western Region to the Eastern Region.

But such travel not only required resources but also certain special methods, and only the Dwarf Race could utilize these methods within Mount Fangcun.

No one else could use them.

The formation being set up in front of them was undoubtedly something like a bridge.

After being busy for several days, the two Sun Blaze finally completed their work. Su Yuqing looked up towards Lu Ye, "You just wait outside."

Lu Ye nodded.

The next moment, the two Sun Blaze's Mental Consciousness surged, and as the powerful Soul Power fluctuated and spread, Lu Ye immediately felt immense pressure and couldn't help but step back.

The array runes of the setup big array shimmered and gradually transformed into light, enveloping the figures of the two Sun Blaze.

In a phantom hall, the blurred figures of Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing began to appear, and only after they completely solidified did they transmit a message through special means.

Soon, one after another, illusory figures similar to theirs appeared in the hall.

Months later, the Sun Blaze from the three divisions gathered again.

Someone urgently asked, "Have you arrived? What is the situation now?"

Before Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing could answer, someone responded, "Since Senior Brother Chen and Junior Sister Su can project here, they must already be at the core. Our Junior Brother Lu is truly amazing, he actually managed to bring out the core, hahaha!"

Upon these words, the emotions of the many Sun Blaze reached a high. Just as the person said, since Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing could project themselves here, they must have entered the Core World; otherwise, such a feat would not be possible.

Moreover, considering the timing, they indeed should have reached the Jade Conch by now.

For a moment, the atmosphere was warm, and the Sun Blaze from each division were in good spirits.

"Senior Brother Chen, go ahead?" said the first Sun Blaze to speak.

Chen Xuanhai nodded and began to recount the information he had learned from Lu Ye. Many Sun Blaze listened attentively.

When they heard that Lu Ye had actually refined the core and now became the Origin Lord, the group of Sun Blaze was instantly dumbfounded.



============================================================
Chapter 1818: Chapter 1818 1816: I Didn't Tell You to Refine It
============================================================

On a towering spirit mountaintop in Dingzhou, as far as the eye could see, a sea of clouds surged and shifted, resembling a fairyland.

Lu Ye's voice continually rang out, occasionally supplemented by Yang Ling and Hu Dequan.

Gradually, everything that had happened in the Core World was completely revealed before Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing.

When they learned that the Red Talisman Society had been hiding in the Core World for years, facing enemies many times more powerful, and with Sun Blaze sitting among them, yet they had not submitted, both Sun Blaze nodded slightly.

The foreign cultivators they had chosen back then had been selected after a long period of observation and training. Looking back now, most of these dispatched cultivators were trustworthy.

Upon learning that the treasure blood of the Blood Ancestor in the Core World had developed spiritual intelligence, Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing couldn't help but change their expressions.

They also didn't know that a drop of the treasure blood of the Blood Ancestor had remained in the Core World, and that the blood had actually nurtured spiritual intelligence, aiming to stain the core origin.

However, they finally understood why Moon Jade of the Dwarf Race found nothing whenever she went searching. According to Lu Ye's speculation, it was because the core origin protected the Dwarf Race cultivators, preventing them from entering the Core World. Whenever a Dwarf Race cultivator entered the marvel, the Core World would avoid them.

The foreign cultivators they sent did not receive this kind of treatment. Some encountered the core and wandered in, while others returned empty-handed.

Through the gentle narration, the whole process of the final battle in the origin space was made known to the two Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race.

After Lu Ye finished speaking, both Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai's expressions turned peculiar.

Chen Xuanhai looked at him with surprise and doubt: "So, at the final moment of that battle, the core consciousness used itself as a cage to imprison the treasure blood consciousness, and then you refined them all?"

"Yes!"

Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing exchanged a glance, seeing what was on each other's mind, and then Chen Xuanhai cautiously asked, "After refining the origin, what changes have you noticed?"

Lu Ye said, "Not much change in myself, but I can easily control the Core World with the origin, and I can also mobilize the Core World's essence. On the way back, I encountered an insect hive, and with this method, I sealed an Insect Race Sun Blaze in the Core World and destroyed it."

Despite having anticipated it, Chen Xuanhai couldn't help but feel amused when Lu Ye said this. As for the Insect Race Sun Blaze being killed, though significant, it was not much compared to the current situation.

Seeing Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing's expressions turning somewhat odd, Lu Ye suspiciously asked, "What's wrong? Is there something inappropriate?"

Chen Xuanhai opened his mouth as if finding it difficult to speak, and finally, he waved his hand, "Junior Sister, you tell him."

Su Yuqing nodded, looked at Lu Ye with gentle eyes, and said, "Lu Ye, during your travels in the stellar space, have you heard of the title World Lord?"

"Yes!" Lu Ye nodded.

In the Indeterminate World of the four galaxies, Jyang Shang was a World Lord, and in the Jade Conch World, there was also a World Lord called Qiu Wu.

Su Yuqing continued, "There are actually two types of World Lords: True World Masters and False World Lords."

Lu Ye was puzzled, "There's such a distinction? How can one tell the difference?"

Su Yuqing explained, "The biggest difference between true and false World Lords is whether they have refined the origin of a world! Those who have not refined a world's origin, called World Lords, are merely respected by the local cultivators. They might be the strongest or the most esteemed in the world, but either way, they do not have many advantages in their world. True World Masters, on the other hand, having refined the origin of the world, can mobilize the essence of their world at will, as you did when suppressing the Insect Race Sun Blaze. At a thought, they can even change the world drastically or break it apart. Such a World Lord is truly the master of that world."

As Su Yuqing spoke, she looked at Lu Ye with a complex expression in her eyes.

Chen Xuanhai also watched him with a similar expression, unable to help but curse internally.

Sending Lu Ye to the Demon Eye Marvel was meant for him to explore information about the core. The Dwarf Race hadn't held much hope since generations of Dwarves had tried for ages without success. As long as Lu Ye could uncover some intelligence about the core, it would be a tremendous gain.

No one expected that in just a few years, only at the Moon Jade Mid-Stage, Lu Ye would actually bring the core out of the marvel. Not only that, but he also refined the core origin and became the core's master!

The core's return is a good thing, but having a master for the core is not, especially since the master is not of Dwarf Race descent!

It's imaginable that when the three parts of Mount Fangcun merge, Lu Ye, as the master of the core, would naturally become the master of the entire Mount Fangcun!

This was what the Blood Ancestor coveted back in the day, but never achieved.

They asked you to find the core, not to refine it!

With two Sun Blaze eyes fixed on him, Lu Ye blinked, realizing something, and turned to Chen Xuanhai, declaring righteously, "Rest assured, Senior Brother, though I am of the human race, since I am Dao companions with Yuqing, my heart is surely aligned with our Dwarf Race. I will never do anything to betray the Dwarf Race. My loyalty is as clear as the heavens and earth, the sun and moon bear witness!" He spoke while reaching out to hold Su Yuqing's hand, grasping it firmly.

Su Yuqing immediately blushed deeply, struggled hard for a moment, but couldn't free herself...

Yang Ling and Hu Dequan were shocked, hurriedly looking up at the sky or down at their feet...

Xiang Yin and sister also averted their gaze in time.

Chen Xuanhai felt a headache coming on... Just a moment ago, when they first met, Lu Ye addressed Su Yuqing as Senior Sister. Now that he's aware of the importance, he calls her Yuqing. This person is too realistic.

Taking a few deep breaths, Chen Xuanhai finally managed to steady his somewhat chaotic breathing. After pondering for a while, he said, "This matter is of great importance, it must be immediately reported to the others."

He also knew that Lu Ye's refining of the core origin was not intentional, because according to Lu Ye's previous accounts, it was the Origin Consciousness guiding him. Otherwise, how could Lu Ye, a Moon Jade Mid-Stage, possibly refine the core?

When Mount Fangcun was intact in the past, it wasn't that no Insect Race Sun Blaze from the Dwarf Race tried refining the origin, but none succeeded.

Mount Fangcun... that is a stellar space supreme treasure! How could it be casually refined by someone?

Lu Ye's refining was a huge coincidence, the erosion of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, the weakening of the Origin Consciousness, and the choice at the critical moment of life and death, all these created the reality of a Moon Jade Mid-Stage achieving the status of the core master.

Looking throughout history, such an event has never happened before.

But no matter what, this monumental event still needs to be immediately reported to the Sun Blaze of the other two divisions, and at this moment, surely everyone is waiting for their news.

With a flushed face, Su Yuqing nodded slightly, then turned to Lu Ye and said, "Go to the core."

Lu Ye felt a pinch in the palm of his hand and immediately nodded, "Then let's go."

The group then hurried towards the core area again.

Halfway there, Su Yuqing transmitted an audio message: "Don't worry, since you've refined the origin, you are the rightful Origin Lord. When Mount Fangcun merges in the future, you will also be the master of the entire Mount Fangcun. The Dwarf Race will not be hostile towards you, but this matter is of great significance, and they need some time to accept it."

Lu Ye nodded, "I'm not worried."

He actually hadn't realized these issues before, but after hearing Su Yuqing's explanation, he understood how significant his refining of the origin was to the Dwarf Race.

From another perspective, if a foreign clan cultivator suddenly refined the origin of the Nine Provinces and became the master of the Nine Provinces, Lu Ye and other cultivators would certainly find it hard to remain calm, even if that foreign clan cultivator made great contributions to the Nine Provinces.

In a short while, they reached a spacious area in the Core World.

Lu Ye stood quietly to the side, waiting. Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai were busy setting up a complex big array.

Lu Ye knew that cultivators of each division in Mount Fangcun could travel back and forth at some cost. Previously, he had traveled from the Western Region to the Eastern Region.

But such travel not only required resources but also certain special methods, and only the Dwarf Race could utilize these methods within Mount Fangcun.

No one else could use them.

The formation being set up in front of them was undoubtedly something like a bridge.

After being busy for several days, the two Sun Blaze finally completed their work. Su Yuqing looked up towards Lu Ye, "You just wait outside."

Lu Ye nodded.

The next moment, the two Sun Blaze's Mental Consciousness surged, and as the powerful Soul Power fluctuated and spread, Lu Ye immediately felt immense pressure and couldn't help but step back.

The array runes of the setup big array shimmered and gradually transformed into light, enveloping the figures of the two Sun Blaze.

In a phantom hall, the blurred figures of Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing began to appear, and only after they completely solidified did they transmit a message through special means.

Soon, one after another, illusory figures similar to theirs appeared in the hall.

Months later, the Sun Blaze from the three divisions gathered again.

Someone urgently asked, "Have you arrived? What is the situation now?"

Before Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing could answer, someone responded, "Since Senior Brother Chen and Junior Sister Su can project here, they must already be at the core. Our Junior Brother Lu is truly amazing, he actually managed to bring out the core, hahaha!"

Upon these words, the emotions of the many Sun Blaze reached a high. Just as the person said, since Chen Xuanhai and Su Yuqing could project themselves here, they must have entered the Core World; otherwise, such a feat would not be possible.

Moreover, considering the timing, they indeed should have reached the Jade Conch by now.

For a moment, the atmosphere was warm, and the Sun Blaze from each division were in good spirits.

"Senior Brother Chen, go ahead?" said the first Sun Blaze to speak.

Chen Xuanhai nodded and began to recount the information he had learned from Lu Ye. Many Sun Blaze listened attentively.

When they heard that Lu Ye had actually refined the core and now became the Origin Lord, the group of Sun Blaze was instantly dumbfounded.
