============================================================
Chapter 1819: Chapter 1819 1817: Dao Tree Lineage
============================================================

It's like a missing girl in the family; for various reasons, an outsider was sent to gather information, and the outsider did an excellent job, not only bringing the missing girl back but also taking her as his wife!

The key issue isn't just about a missing girl from the family, refining the core means directly becoming the master of all Mount Fangcun!

The Sun Blaze cannot accept it; no one can allow such an existence to sit over the entire clan, nor can they hand over the clan's future to this outsider.

"This is outrageous, how dare that boy, how could he dare!" One Sun Blaze beat his chest and stomped his feet, heartbroken, as if a family girl had been married off by an outsider.

Inside the illusory hall, a chaotic scene unfolded. The core origin being refined clearly caused a massive shock to the Sun Blaze. As Sun Blaze, their disposition and cultivation were exceptional; normal events couldn't stir such emotional upheaval. But today's events concerned the clan's future, so it's understandable.

Chen Xuanhai watched coldly and couldn't help sighing; he knew things would develop this way.

A passionate Sun Blaze, in a fit of anger, shouted, "Kill that boy, and the core will have no master!"

Immediately, someone objected, "That's inappropriate. The Dwarf Race regained the long-lost core, and the three divisions have now merged, which is a great achievement. We can't even express gratitude, let alone resort to murder. If that's the case, what is our Dwarf Race becoming? Besides, he isn't completely unrelated to our clan."

After all, Lu Ye is the Dao companion of Su Yuqing from the Eastern Region.

The Sun Blaze who spoke earlier realized he was too blunt and looked towards Su Yuqing, "Junior Sister, don't mind. I have a habit of speaking without restraint."

Su Yuqing said lightly, "Then it's best for you to change this habit; causing misunderstandings wouldn't be good."

Killing is not an option, but letting things develop like this leaves everyone without a sense of security. For a moment, the Sun Blaze seemed at a loss for what to do.

After a while, someone spoke slowly, "I'm curious about one thing. As far as I know, this Junior Brother Lu only has cultivation at Moon Jade Mid-Stage, right? Even with assistance from the Origin Consciousness during the core refining, it should not have been so easy. The Origin Consciousness, even the awareness in Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, is not easily refined. Even among us Sun Blaze, who can guarantee success? Additionally, how did he refine Blood Ancestor's treasure blood? The terrifying contamination power of Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, once in the Core World, even a drop of Blood Rain would gradually transform one into a Blood Race. How did he, a mere Moon Jade, manage to be unaffected and refine it?"

Hearing this, all the Sun Blaze turned to look at Chen Xuanhai.

Chen Xuanhai was stunned, and then shook his head slowly, "I neglected to ask about this." Mainly upon learning that Lu Ye had refined the origin to become the Origin Lord, the news was so shocking that he only thought of informing the other Sun Blaze and didn't think to ask these questions.

"Additionally," the previous Sun Blaze continued, "according to Junior Brother Lu's account, at the last moment, the Origin Consciousness actively sought him out to help with the refining. In other words, regardless of how we view this, the Origin Consciousness favors him. Why? What special qualities does he have that make the Origin Consciousness entrust the outcome of battling the treasure blood in him?"

The Origin Consciousness is not a living being, but in terms of knowledge and experience, it surpasses any Sun Blaze present, perhaps even more powerful. So this matter is very odd. Why did the Origin Consciousness make that choice? What does Lu Ye possess for the Origin Consciousness to value, or was it simply a desperate measure out of necessity?

However, this is evidently unreasonable. In truth, many cultivators with greater cultivation than Lu Ye could've been chosen at the time, such as Yang Ling and Hu Dequan, who have been in the Core World for far longer, having obvious advantages, more likely to gain the origin's recognition.

Yet, the origin didn't choose them; rather, it chose Lu Ye, who had only recently entered the Core World.

Therefore, the most likely reason is that Lu Ye possesses some special quality that caught the origin's attention.

"Could I trouble Junior Brother Chen and Junior Sister Su to bring Junior Brother Lu here, so that we might question him ourselves?" that Sun Blaze suggested, thinking it was simpler to ask directly than guess blindly. After saying this, he turned to Su Yuqing, "Junior Sister Su, rest assured, regardless of the outcome, I guarantee that unless Junior Brother Lu is already contaminated by the treasure blood and turned into a Blood Race, his life will be unharmed."

The Sun Blaze speaking is from the Southern Region and is the oldest and most respected Sun Blaze present; his guarantee certainly carries weight.

Chen Xuanhai looked at Su Yuqing.

Su Yuqing pondered briefly, then nodded, "Please wait a moment, I will bring him here."

Saying that, the figure faded.

In the Core World, Lu Ye had already retreated far away, waiting silently, when suddenly Su Yuqing's voice reached his ear, "Lu Ye, come over!"

Upon hearing this, Lu Ye quickly flew forward, and at the same time, Su Yuqing's Mental Consciousness enveloped him, relieving his pressure.

Shortly after, Lu Ye stood in front of Su Yuqing; she grabbed his hand and said, "Don't resist; I'm taking you somewhere. Our clan's Sun Blaze have some questions for you."

"Alright!" Lu Ye nodded.

Su Yuqing, still uneasy, asked again, "Have you been contaminated by the power of Blood Ancestor's treasure blood?"

"No."

Su Yuqing looked at him directly, "Don't lie to me."

"Really not," Lu Ye reiterated, "Let me put it this way, I have a unique refining ability; anything harmful to me in this world can be refined away."

Su Yuqing was taken aback: "What kind of ability is that?" Such a terrifying refining power shouldn't belong to someone at Moon Jade stage.

Lu Ye thought for a moment and said, "I can't really say clearly." The name Talent Tree was something he came up with himself, so he didn't know how to explain it to Su Yuqing. Suddenly, a spirit light flashed in his mind, and he said, "When the core origin contacted me, it mentioned the Dao Tree lineage. From its words, it seemed to think I belonged to this lineage."

"What?" Su Yuqing's pupils suddenly contracted: "The Origin Consciousness thinks you are from the Dao Tree lineage?"

"I'm not sure if that's the case, but it just mentioned it casually. Besides, throughout my cultivation, I've refined many things. All harmful substances were entirely refined away, and when I looked within myself, there indeed seems to be a tree inside."

Su Yuqing's heart was shaken; the ability to refine anything harmful, the Dao Tree lineage...

She slowly nodded: "I understand, you stand aside for now."

There was no longer a need for Lu Ye to personally inquire with the Sun Blaze of his clan.

Following her words, Lu Ye stepped back, and moments later, Su Yuqing's figure appeared again in the ethereal grand hall.

Seeing her return alone, a group of Sun Blaze appeared puzzled.

Su Yuqing's voice arose: "Lu Ye is a descendant of the Dao Tree lineage, I just learned of this!"

In the grand hall, a brief silence ensued, quickly followed by exclamations: "A descendant of the Dao Tree lineage? Junior Sister, are you sure?"

"Is there a new descendant of the Dao Tree lineage in the world?"

"I see!"

...

Many Sun Blaze looked as if they had never seen the world, exclaiming repeatedly. Even Chen Xuanhai gazed at Su Yuqing in shock, almost doubting his own hearing.

"Everyone quiet down, what are you doing?" The highest-ranking Sun Blaze in the Southern Region spoke sternly, looking at Su Yuqing: "Junior Sister, can this matter be confirmed?"

Su Yuqing replied, "Lu Ye told me that when he previously encountered the Origin Consciousness, it mentioned the Dao Tree lineage. Also, Lu Ye said that since he began cultivating, he has refined many things, all detrimental substances have been refined away, and upon introspection, there is indeed a tree inside him, moreover... he is of fire element!"

The Sun Blaze of the Southern Region nodded slightly: "The Dao Tree lineage, there is nothing in the world it cannot refine. If this is true, then it explains everything."

Evidently, when the Origin Consciousness interacted with Lu Ye, it sensed he was a descendant of the Dao Tree lineage, which gave it confidence to assist him in refining the origin, because even the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood could be refined by the Dao Tree lineage.

"If it's the descendant of the Dao Tree lineage who refined the core origin..." The Sun Blaze of the Southern Region pondered and then turned to the others, "Isn't this somewhat acceptable?"

The Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race's shock regarding Lu Ye becoming the Origin Lord was primarily due to Lu Ye's current weak cultivation, even though his potential seemed good, no one could predict what he might grow into in the future, and he was from a Foreign Clan.

But the descendant of the Dao Tree lineage was undoubtedly worth anticipating.

Su Yuqing spoke unhurriedly, "When I first met him, he was only at the Constellation Early Stage, and that was just over a decade ago."

A group of Sun Blaze couldn't help but be shaken.

A Constellation Early Stage cultivator over a decade ago, and now in the Moon Jade Mid-Stage in such a short span—such a terrifying pace of cultivation, perhaps only a descendant of the Dao Tree lineage could achieve it in this world.

Indeed, the future looks promising!

After a silent moment, the Sun Blaze of the Southern Region spoke, "The core has been refined, and unless we quench our humanity and disregard such an enormous achievement by eliminating Junior Brother Lu before he can rise, I suppose none of us here would do such a thing. Fortunately, Junior Brother Lu is considered one of us, and since the core is refined, let it be. Moreover, from what we know, Junior Brother Lu's character and morality are trustworthy. I suggest, we observe the situation quietly."

"I second that!" A Sun Blaze followed.

"I second that!"

"I second that!"

...

The three departments of Sun Blaze successively expressed agreement, thus concluding the refinement of the core matter once and for all.

The Sun Blaze from the Southern Region looked again at Su Yuqing: "Junior Sister, Junior Brother Lu will be entrusted to your care. The potential for growth in the Dao Tree lineage is undeniably immense, but we must ensure he doesn't stray onto a dark path. The downfall of the Nine Provinces thousands of years ago serves as a lesson, and we must remain vigilant; I do not wish for our clan to repeat the same mistakes one day!"

"I understand, I will take good care of him." Su Yuqing nodded solemnly.



============================================================
Chapter 1820: Chapter 1820 1818: The Domain Outside Is the Nine Provinces (Happy National Day)
============================================================

In the Core World, under Lu Ye's watchful gaze, he saw Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai gradually regain their senses, as the terrifying fluctuations of soul power gradually subsided.

Chen Xuanhai glanced in the direction where Lu Ye stood, his expression slightly complicated, and said, "Junior Sister, it's up to you."

Su Yuqing nodded.

Only then did Chen Xuanhai take flight, soaring out of the domain.

Lu Ye glanced in the direction of his departure, then stepped toward Su Yuqing, stopping before her and asking, "What's going on?"

Chen Xuanhai had looked at him with a somewhat peculiar expression earlier.

Su Yuqing pondered for a moment, then extended a hand to Lu Ye, softly saying, "Come."

Lu Ye placed his hand in her palm, and in the next instant, pure mana enveloped him, propelling the two of them toward the nearest spirit mountaintop.

A moment later, on that spirit mountaintop, Su Yuqing brought out two chairs, and they sat facing each other.

Lu Ye felt she might have something very important to discuss with him; otherwise, she wouldn't have made such a serious gesture. But since Su Yuqing hadn't brought it up yet, he didn't want to rush her, so he quietly waited.

After a while, Su Yuqing finally spoke, "How much do you know about the Dao Tree lineage?"

Lu Ye shook his head, "Not at all."

He had only heard this term from Veteran Fang, but back then Veteran Fang hadn't said much. So he asked in return, "Do you know?"

When he had mentioned the Dao Tree lineage previously, Su Yuqing had clearly reacted differently, evidently having heard of it.

"I've heard a bit. In fact, Xiyuan Pavilion has records about the Dao Tree lineage." Su Yuqing nodded.

Lu Ye was surprised, "Why didn't I see them?" When he first entered Mount Fangcun, he had stayed in Xiyuan Pavilion for several months, imprinting a large amount of information about stellar space and bringing it back to the Nine Provinces, filling the Nine Provinces' knowledge gap about stellar space.

Su Yuqing said, "Some secrets in Xiyuan Pavilion are not open to outsiders."

Lu Ye understood; that explained why he hadn't seen any such records.

"Tell me about it." Lu Ye sat up straight, actually quite interested in his inheritance. Moreover, he had asked Number Nine about this matter back in the day, but unfortunately, Number Nine couldn't provide any answers, only telling him that Lu Ye was not the first to receive this inheritance. Before him, several Nine Provinces cultivators had also obtained it, but none managed to grow.

Su Yuqing's voice came forth, "What I know are things recorded by my clan's ancestors, never witnessed with my own eyes, so just take a listen. Some things require your own judgment."

Lu Ye nodded solemnly.

"The Dao Tree is a path of inheritance and a very powerful one at that, with only one successor in each generation. Its specific form is likely as you described before—a tree within the body visible through inner sight. The last successor of the Dao Tree lineage appeared millennia ago, during a time when there was an exceptionally famous top-class domain belonging to the human race. Compared to the current Yellow Dragon World, it was even more formidable, and could be said to be the undisputed overlord domain of the human race. Unfortunately... such a top-class domain was ultimately destroyed because of the Dao Tree lineage."

"Why?" Lu Ye frowned.

He didn't fully grasp how powerful the Yellow Dragon World was, but after mixing in the All Phenomena Ocean for years, he had heard of the Yellow Dragon World's reputation numerous times. Nowadays, in the All Phenomena Ocean, the Yellow Dragon World solely occupied a top-class Spirit Island.

The overlord domain of the human race from a millennium ago was actually even stronger than the Yellow Dragon World, but such a domain was destroyed because of the Dao Tree lineage. This puzzled Lu Ye; he didn't understand what kind of causal relationship existed.

Su Yuqing said, "The Dao Tree successor of that generation was a cultivator from that top-class domain. He rose from obscurity to fame in stellar space, growing at an incredibly rapid pace. However, he committed acts that enraged the heavens and people, angering many forces. Not only did his reputation become notorious, but even his birth domain was implicated."

At this point, she sighed and gave Lu Ye a meaningful glance, "The Dao Tree lineage, in the vast world, nothing is there that it cannot refine. Your cultivation speed is so fast, it should be related to your inheritance. You must also know how much assistance this inheritance has provided you in your growth."

Lu Ye solemnly nodded.

Without the Talent Tree, he would never have achieved his current accomplishments.

"As you grew, did you ever use the power of the Dao Tree to refine living beings?" When she posed this question, Su Yuqing's expression was extremely serious.

Lu Ye decisively shook his head, "Never have."

"Can you confirm?"

"I can confirm!" Lu Ye nodded.

Actually, right after the first metamorphosis of the Talent Tree, Lu Ye had already discovered this matter. Since he could harness the power of the Talent Tree to refine the Spirit Stone, he could completely refine the spirit force within the cultivators for his own use, and even refine their blood Qi altogether.

Doing so would mean that every cultivator would become a cultivation resource he could refine.

But Lu Ye had never done so because he felt that it was no different from consuming people, which was psychologically hard to accept, so to date, no matter how many enemies he has slain, even though some of them were not from the human race, he has never refined their spirit force.

"That's good!" Su Yuqing took a deep breath, completely alleviating her concerns. She was really worried that Lu Ye might have done something similar.

"Is there any hidden danger in doing this?" Lu Ye saw her change in expression and vaguely guessed.

Su Yuqing nodded: "There is hidden danger, and quite significant. The Dao Tree lineage can refine all, but there is one thing that cannot be refined, or rather, cannot be completely refined!"

"What is it?" Lu Ye was incredibly curious. In his cultivation journey so far, he hadn't encountered anything that couldn't be refined; anything that could assist in his growth seemed to be refinable?

"Seven emotions and six desires!" Su Yuqing's red lips gently parted, "Or rather, the emotions of living beings with flesh and blood. Ten thousand years ago, the successor of the Dao Tree lineage didn't have exceptional aptitude, quite poor, in fact. But he soon discovered a method to rapidly enhance his aptitude: killing enemies and then refining them. This refinement not only improved his strength, but also his aptitude seemed to enhance as if the Dao Tree could strip away others' aptitudes to strengthen itself. Using this method, his strength grew stronger and his aptitude more outstanding, yet the more beings he refined, the more sinister his temperament became. Every enemy he killed was filled with various negative emotions before they died, and the Dao Tree couldn't completely purify these emotions, accumulating them within him."

"Later, in pursuit of greater strength and aptitude, he secretly harmed cultivators from many powerful factions, including successors from top-class domains. These people were all exceptionally talented, greatly aiding his growth. He ventured further and further down this dark path, leading to more and more slaughter, ultimately losing himself, and he brought calamity to his home domain as a result."

"After the incident was exposed, countless powerful factions allied to besiege that domain. Numerous Sun Blaze masters participated, making the domain a living hell for its inhabitants. If it weren't for the domain's warriors preparing beforehand and crafting a mysterious treasure to teleport the domain away, the whole domain might have been shattered by the battle!"

"Hmm?" Lu Ye originally listened as if it were an old story from ten thousand years ago, the predecessors' experiences cautioning him. But hearing this, he suddenly felt a strong sense of familiarity.

A certain domain's warriors prepared in advance, crafting a mysterious treasure to teleport the entire domain away at a critical moment…

He quickly asked: "What was the name of the Dao Tree successor from ten thousand years ago? Which domain did he come from?"

Su Yuqing thought for a moment and said, "That person was named Chao Nian, and the domain he came from was called Nine Provinces!" With these words, she reached out to grasp Lu Ye's hand, looking at him earnestly: "Lu Ye, you must heed Chao Nian's lesson. With the Dao Tree, you possess a faster growth rate than anyone else. Never succumb to the temptation to refine living beings casually; it will only harm you, never benefit you."

Lu Ye certainly won't do such things; if he were inclined to, he would've done it much earlier. Moreover, cultivation for him is simple; as long as the Talent Tree has ample fuel reserves, all he needs to do is dive into All Phenomena Ocean, so why refine living beings?

Since he hasn't embarked on this dark path earlier, he won't tread it in the future.

"I understand." Lu Ye nodded and looked at Su Yuqing, "Yuqing, there's something I need to tell you."

"Speak." Su Yuqing looked at him seriously.

Lu Ye gave a thumbs up: "The domain I come from outside is indeed Nine Provinces!"

Su Yuqing blinked her big eyes: "Isn't it Nine Heavens?"

She remembered Lu Ye previously claimed to be Lu Yiye of the Nine Heavens…

"Nine Heavens is just the public moniker. A senior once advised us to never mention the name Nine Provinces when traveling outside, hence the cultivators from our home domain always claim to be from Nine Heavens."

This matter was bound to be unhideable from the Dwarf Race. Once Mount Fangcun merges, the truth about Nine Provinces will eventually be known.

Facing Su Yuqing, Lu Ye had no intention of hiding it.

Su Yuqing was momentarily stunned before reacting, "Your Nine Provinces and Chao Nian's Nine Provinces…"

Lu Ye nodded: "Presumably, it is the same Nine Provinces!"

When he first met Number Nine, Number Nine used a means to let him see the scene of the previous Nine Provinces being besieged. At that time, he didn't know what sort of heinous act the previous Nine Provinces committed to provoke such formidable enemies to attack. Unfortunately, Number Nine couldn't explain to him either, as before the previous Nine Provinces were besieged, Number Nine had not yet developed spiritual intelligence.

The reason it could let Lu Ye witness that scene was primarily because the earth-shattering battle left too deep a mark on the origin of Nine Provinces. As the Heaven's Augury Compass Artifact Spirit combined with Nine Provinces' origin, it could naturally recall from Nine Provinces' origin.

Now he understands that the disaster for the previous Nine Provinces originated from Chao Nian, who went down a dark path and offended too many powerful factions, leading them to unite against the previous Nine Provinces.



============================================================
Chapter 1821: Chapter 1821 1819: Sorting Out the Core
============================================================

The former Nine Provinces where Chao Nian resided was a top-tier domain, but unfortunately, a single relocation nearly depleted the domain's foundation, causing the Nine Provinces to weaken, and only in recent years did it barely ascend to a large-scale domain.

Nowadays, everything is developing in a positive direction. The cultivators of the Nine Provinces have walked out of the stellar space, integrating with the All Phenomena Ocean, and the Nine Provinces itself is also supported by the Flower World. The two complement each other, and coupled with Number Nine's unique existence, the Nine Provinces has leaped into a rapidly growing large-scale domain.

This is an advantage that no other domain in the stellar space can match. It can be said that the future of the Nine Provinces is worth anticipating.

In front of Lu Ye, Su Yuqing suddenly realized: "So, ten thousand years ago, although Chao Nian died, the legacy of the Dao Tree lineage still remained in the Nine Provinces?"

"That's probably correct." Lu Ye nodded.

This legacy may have had other owners before Chao Nian, and several owners after him, until it was obtained by Lu Ye in recent years.

"I see!" Su Yuqing murmured.

Lu Ye looked at her: "Did you think of something?"

Su Yuqing said: "Actually, when I saw these records about the Nine Provinces and Chao Nian back then, I was puzzled by one thing. The Nine Provinces was, after all, the pinnacle domain occupied by the human race at that time. No matter how many evil deeds Chao Nian committed, those many forces only needed to kill Chao Nian to avenge themselves—so why did they rally to attack the Nine Provinces? In retrospect, Chao Nian might have merely been an inducement. The real purpose of these forces was the Dao Tree's legacy. They must have known by then that the Dao Tree legacy still resided in the Nine Provinces!

Simple grievances weren't enough to target the Nine Provinces in such a way, but with enough benefits, it's different.

The temptation of the Dao Tree legacy was too great, and Chao Nian's actions provided them with sufficient reasons and excuses, so a grand play of many forces joining hands to siege the Nine Provinces began.

If it weren't for the strong ones of the former Nine Provinces having been prepared, expending massive energy and resources to create the Heaven's Augury Compass, and using the power of the Compass to relocate the Nine Provinces, the entire Nine Provinces would have been excavated three feet deep after that battle.

"Lu Ye." Su Yuqing spoke solemnly, "What the elder you mentioned advised was correct. When you go out, you must never mention the Nine Provinces. Ten thousand years is a long time, but to those major forces, it isn't that long. The name of the Nine Provinces and the legacy of the Dao Tree could invite catastrophe."

Lu Ye nodded.

"As for the Dwarf Race over here, for now, only our Sun Blaze is aware of this matter. The information won't leak, so you can rest easy."

Now Lu Ye is the Master of Core Origin, destined to become the lord of Mount Fangcun in the future, which basically binds him with Mount Fangcun. They share weal and woe, and hence, the Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race certainly won't do anything against his interests.

Lu Ye isn't worried about this. However, after today's chat with Su Yuqing, he has learned some secrets closely related to himself.

Suddenly, he remembered something: "By the way, if the three parts of Mount Fangcun are to be merged, roughly how long will it take?"

Su Yuqing calculated slightly and replied: "We in the Eastern Region are the closest, probably need less than three years, the Southern Region takes over ten years, and the Western Region, being the furthest, might need at least thirty to forty years."

"Then I'd better hurry." Lu Ye thought to himself, the Southern and Western Regions have ample time to merge, but the Eastern Region requires less than three years, which is quite urgent.

"What's wrong?" Su Yuqing was puzzled.

Lu Ye explained: "Although I've refined the Origin and the consciousness of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, the erosion of one drop of treasure blood on the Core World is everywhere. Now, throughout the Core World, the power of the treasure blood still lingers. I need to sort it out thoroughly and cleanse the remaining power of the treasure blood. Only then, when Mount Fangcun merges, the Dwarf side will not have worries."

"Will three years be enough?" Su Yuqing's expression tightened. She clearly realized that if the residual power of the treasure blood is not thoroughly sorted out, it would lead to dire consequences.

"Roughly enough. If not, it doesn't matter; I'll then seal the core, preventing the Eastern Region from merging."

He had sealed the core before, and doing so again would be no challenge.

"Then thank you for your hard work." Su Yuqing nodded.

Lu Ye looked at her beautiful visage, blinking: "It is quite hard, but if there's a reward, I'd be more motivated!"

Su Yuqing gave a charming smile, slowly rose: "Wait until you are done sorting the core!"

With that, her figure shot up, headed beyond the realm, with Lu Ye's voice trailing behind her: "Remember you said it!"

Watching Su Yuqing depart, Lu Ye finally composed himself, shortly thereafter, his figure flickered, entering the origin space.

Gazing throughout, the Core Origin stood tall like a great sun, but unlike when first seen, the origin now is no longer shrouded in red but appears pure and flawless.

The origin was intact, yet the entire domain still needed sorting.

Lu Ye directly leaped onto the origin, sitting cross-legged, relying on his status as the Master of Core Origin, examining the entire Core World, extending the power of the Talent Tree, refining the remaining treasure blood power bit by bit.

On the Nine Provinces side, he had no worries. Not to mention there are now four Moon Jade Late Stage cultivators stationed in the Nine Provinces, even Sun Blaze counts two, Lu Ye believes that while he's sorting the Core World, Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai will take good care of the Nine Provinces.

Day after day, year after year.

Sorting the domain was extremely tedious, yet Lu Ye couldn't afford any negligence, otherwise, any residual power of the treasure blood could lead to unforeseeable consequences.

As the residual power of the treasure blood continued to be refined, Lu Ye felt his saintliness growing steadily. He wondered how much strength Lih Tian could exert if he were not dead and stood before him, suppressed by his saintliness.

Before refining the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, his saintliness was already unmatched by any Blood Race. Now, after refining a drop of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, his saintliness had grown terrifyingly, making such suppression lethal to the Blood Race.

Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai occasionally came to the Core World to check on things, but they never disturbed him. Only once did Lu Ye take the initiative to contact Su Yuqing and learn that they were staying in the Nine Provinces, living peacefully and leisurely.

For the two of them, all they could do now was wait, because before long, the East would integrate under the core's guidance.

Once the Southern Region and Western Region return one after another in the future, the unification of the Dwarf Race will occur, something both Sun Blaze are eagerly anticipating.

Mount Fangcun had been divided for so long, but their generation finally had the opportunity to revive their ancestors' glory, and everyone shared in that honor.

Three years passed by slowly.

Until this day, in the Origin space, Lu Ye, after several careful explorations and searches, confirmed that there was no residual treasure blood power left in the core space, he let out a long breath.

Counting the three years spent refining the treasure blood before, he had devoted six years of time for the matters of the Core World.

During this period, he did not cultivate, and his strength barely grew, but he believed it was all worth it.

Speaking of his own gains, though his strength hadn't grown, his saintliness had undergone a monumental change. In the future, when facing the Blood Race, even the Sun Blaze, he could handle them with ease.

Moreover, he had become the Master of Core Origin, and in the future, he would truly be the World Lord of Mount Fangcun!

In this way, the Dwarf Race would become the strongest backing for the Nine Provinces, and during his travels, he wouldn't need to worry about any problems occurring in the Nine Provinces.

The six years of effort brought such rewards; it was well worth it!

As for his own strength, once these matters are concluded, he could replenish it by taking a trip to the All Phenomena Ocean, and after these years of settling, his cultivation in the Moon Jade Mid-Stage was stable enough.

Buoyed by joy, Lu Ye exited seclusion.

With a flicker, he left the Core World.

"Venerable Lord!" A familiar voice immediately reached him.

Lu Ye turned and saw it was Xiang Yin and sister, who had been guarding here.

Lu Ye nodded slightly and turned to look in a direction. In that moment, he could sense something incredibly close rushing towards him, something that seemed to be a missing part of himself.

He suddenly understood that the Eastern Mount Fangcun was approaching rapidly, and the feeling of missing was perceived as the Origin Lord, not a lack within himself.

"Brother Chen Xuanhai and Sister Su Yuqing, where are they?" Lu Ye inquired.

Xiang Yin immediately replied, "The two masters left recently to welcome the Eastern Mount Fangcun. Mistress said this integration might cause some upheaval, so they need to be stationed in the east, and asked me to convey the message for the Venerable Lord to maintain stability in the core."

Lu Ye nodded, "I understand."

After a careful sense, he confirmed that in a few days, the Eastern Mount Fangcun would integrate, prompting Lu Ye to decide to wait in the core.

He instructed, "You may leave now, there's no need for you here."

"Understood!" Xiang Yin and sister complied, heading straight back in the direction of the Nine Provinces.

Lu Ye looked up at the Blood Refinement World spanning the Void in the distance, suppressing a sudden wave of anxiety. Regardless, the integration of Mount Fangcun was a priority, so it must be addressed first.

He then flickered and entered the Core World once more, quietly waiting.

Several days passed swiftly, the stationed in the core Lu Ye suddenly opened his eyes, even though he couldn't see anything, he could clearly sense that the Eastern Mount Fangcun had arrived!

Almost instantly as the thought emerged, the world changed.

A massive buzzing sound emanated from all directions, the space within the Core World became distorted. The entire world seemed to become more complete, the domain rapidly expanding...not expanding, but rather like missing pieces of a puzzle similar assembling.

This assembly caused the core world and even the east to shake uneasily.

Lu Ye raised his hand, his thoughts moving, Origin Power deployed, like an invisible large hand, smoothing over the turbulent areas, in an instant, tranquility restored!

The turbulence from the integration of the Eastern Mount Fangcun with the core lasted a full fortnight, and when all settled after the fortnight, Lu Ye clearly sensed that the Core World had expanded many times over, with many familiar landscapes now added, those originally belonging to the Eastern Mount Fangcun.



============================================================
Chapter 1819: Chapter 1819 1817: Dao Tree Lineage
============================================================

It's like a missing girl in the family; for various reasons, an outsider was sent to gather information, and the outsider did an excellent job, not only bringing the missing girl back but also taking her as his wife!

The key issue isn't just about a missing girl from the family, refining the core means directly becoming the master of all Mount Fangcun!

The Sun Blaze cannot accept it; no one can allow such an existence to sit over the entire clan, nor can they hand over the clan's future to this outsider.

"This is outrageous, how dare that boy, how could he dare!" One Sun Blaze beat his chest and stomped his feet, heartbroken, as if a family girl had been married off by an outsider.

Inside the illusory hall, a chaotic scene unfolded. The core origin being refined clearly caused a massive shock to the Sun Blaze. As Sun Blaze, their disposition and cultivation were exceptional; normal events couldn't stir such emotional upheaval. But today's events concerned the clan's future, so it's understandable.

Chen Xuanhai watched coldly and couldn't help sighing; he knew things would develop this way.

A passionate Sun Blaze, in a fit of anger, shouted, "Kill that boy, and the core will have no master!"

Immediately, someone objected, "That's inappropriate. The Dwarf Race regained the long-lost core, and the three divisions have now merged, which is a great achievement. We can't even express gratitude, let alone resort to murder. If that's the case, what is our Dwarf Race becoming? Besides, he isn't completely unrelated to our clan."

After all, Lu Ye is the Dao companion of Su Yuqing from the Eastern Region.

The Sun Blaze who spoke earlier realized he was too blunt and looked towards Su Yuqing, "Junior Sister, don't mind. I have a habit of speaking without restraint."

Su Yuqing said lightly, "Then it's best for you to change this habit; causing misunderstandings wouldn't be good."

Killing is not an option, but letting things develop like this leaves everyone without a sense of security. For a moment, the Sun Blaze seemed at a loss for what to do.

After a while, someone spoke slowly, "I'm curious about one thing. As far as I know, this Junior Brother Lu only has cultivation at Moon Jade Mid-Stage, right? Even with assistance from the Origin Consciousness during the core refining, it should not have been so easy. The Origin Consciousness, even the awareness in Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, is not easily refined. Even among us Sun Blaze, who can guarantee success? Additionally, how did he refine Blood Ancestor's treasure blood? The terrifying contamination power of Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, once in the Core World, even a drop of Blood Rain would gradually transform one into a Blood Race. How did he, a mere Moon Jade, manage to be unaffected and refine it?"

Hearing this, all the Sun Blaze turned to look at Chen Xuanhai.

Chen Xuanhai was stunned, and then shook his head slowly, "I neglected to ask about this." Mainly upon learning that Lu Ye had refined the origin to become the Origin Lord, the news was so shocking that he only thought of informing the other Sun Blaze and didn't think to ask these questions.

"Additionally," the previous Sun Blaze continued, "according to Junior Brother Lu's account, at the last moment, the Origin Consciousness actively sought him out to help with the refining. In other words, regardless of how we view this, the Origin Consciousness favors him. Why? What special qualities does he have that make the Origin Consciousness entrust the outcome of battling the treasure blood in him?"

The Origin Consciousness is not a living being, but in terms of knowledge and experience, it surpasses any Sun Blaze present, perhaps even more powerful. So this matter is very odd. Why did the Origin Consciousness make that choice? What does Lu Ye possess for the Origin Consciousness to value, or was it simply a desperate measure out of necessity?

However, this is evidently unreasonable. In truth, many cultivators with greater cultivation than Lu Ye could've been chosen at the time, such as Yang Ling and Hu Dequan, who have been in the Core World for far longer, having obvious advantages, more likely to gain the origin's recognition.

Yet, the origin didn't choose them; rather, it chose Lu Ye, who had only recently entered the Core World.

Therefore, the most likely reason is that Lu Ye possesses some special quality that caught the origin's attention.

"Could I trouble Junior Brother Chen and Junior Sister Su to bring Junior Brother Lu here, so that we might question him ourselves?" that Sun Blaze suggested, thinking it was simpler to ask directly than guess blindly. After saying this, he turned to Su Yuqing, "Junior Sister Su, rest assured, regardless of the outcome, I guarantee that unless Junior Brother Lu is already contaminated by the treasure blood and turned into a Blood Race, his life will be unharmed."

The Sun Blaze speaking is from the Southern Region and is the oldest and most respected Sun Blaze present; his guarantee certainly carries weight.

Chen Xuanhai looked at Su Yuqing.

Su Yuqing pondered briefly, then nodded, "Please wait a moment, I will bring him here."

Saying that, the figure faded.

In the Core World, Lu Ye had already retreated far away, waiting silently, when suddenly Su Yuqing's voice reached his ear, "Lu Ye, come over!"

Upon hearing this, Lu Ye quickly flew forward, and at the same time, Su Yuqing's Mental Consciousness enveloped him, relieving his pressure.

Shortly after, Lu Ye stood in front of Su Yuqing; she grabbed his hand and said, "Don't resist; I'm taking you somewhere. Our clan's Sun Blaze have some questions for you."

"Alright!" Lu Ye nodded.

Su Yuqing, still uneasy, asked again, "Have you been contaminated by the power of Blood Ancestor's treasure blood?"

"No."

Su Yuqing looked at him directly, "Don't lie to me."

"Really not," Lu Ye reiterated, "Let me put it this way, I have a unique refining ability; anything harmful to me in this world can be refined away."

Su Yuqing was taken aback: "What kind of ability is that?" Such a terrifying refining power shouldn't belong to someone at Moon Jade stage.

Lu Ye thought for a moment and said, "I can't really say clearly." The name Talent Tree was something he came up with himself, so he didn't know how to explain it to Su Yuqing. Suddenly, a spirit light flashed in his mind, and he said, "When the core origin contacted me, it mentioned the Dao Tree lineage. From its words, it seemed to think I belonged to this lineage."

"What?" Su Yuqing's pupils suddenly contracted: "The Origin Consciousness thinks you are from the Dao Tree lineage?"

"I'm not sure if that's the case, but it just mentioned it casually. Besides, throughout my cultivation, I've refined many things. All harmful substances were entirely refined away, and when I looked within myself, there indeed seems to be a tree inside."

Su Yuqing's heart was shaken; the ability to refine anything harmful, the Dao Tree lineage...

She slowly nodded: "I understand, you stand aside for now."

There was no longer a need for Lu Ye to personally inquire with the Sun Blaze of his clan.

Following her words, Lu Ye stepped back, and moments later, Su Yuqing's figure appeared again in the ethereal grand hall.

Seeing her return alone, a group of Sun Blaze appeared puzzled.

Su Yuqing's voice arose: "Lu Ye is a descendant of the Dao Tree lineage, I just learned of this!"

In the grand hall, a brief silence ensued, quickly followed by exclamations: "A descendant of the Dao Tree lineage? Junior Sister, are you sure?"

"Is there a new descendant of the Dao Tree lineage in the world?"

"I see!"

...

Many Sun Blaze looked as if they had never seen the world, exclaiming repeatedly. Even Chen Xuanhai gazed at Su Yuqing in shock, almost doubting his own hearing.

"Everyone quiet down, what are you doing?" The highest-ranking Sun Blaze in the Southern Region spoke sternly, looking at Su Yuqing: "Junior Sister, can this matter be confirmed?"

Su Yuqing replied, "Lu Ye told me that when he previously encountered the Origin Consciousness, it mentioned the Dao Tree lineage. Also, Lu Ye said that since he began cultivating, he has refined many things, all detrimental substances have been refined away, and upon introspection, there is indeed a tree inside him, moreover... he is of fire element!"

The Sun Blaze of the Southern Region nodded slightly: "The Dao Tree lineage, there is nothing in the world it cannot refine. If this is true, then it explains everything."

Evidently, when the Origin Consciousness interacted with Lu Ye, it sensed he was a descendant of the Dao Tree lineage, which gave it confidence to assist him in refining the origin, because even the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood could be refined by the Dao Tree lineage.

"If it's the descendant of the Dao Tree lineage who refined the core origin..." The Sun Blaze of the Southern Region pondered and then turned to the others, "Isn't this somewhat acceptable?"

The Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race's shock regarding Lu Ye becoming the Origin Lord was primarily due to Lu Ye's current weak cultivation, even though his potential seemed good, no one could predict what he might grow into in the future, and he was from a Foreign Clan.

But the descendant of the Dao Tree lineage was undoubtedly worth anticipating.

Su Yuqing spoke unhurriedly, "When I first met him, he was only at the Constellation Early Stage, and that was just over a decade ago."

A group of Sun Blaze couldn't help but be shaken.

A Constellation Early Stage cultivator over a decade ago, and now in the Moon Jade Mid-Stage in such a short span—such a terrifying pace of cultivation, perhaps only a descendant of the Dao Tree lineage could achieve it in this world.

Indeed, the future looks promising!

After a silent moment, the Sun Blaze of the Southern Region spoke, "The core has been refined, and unless we quench our humanity and disregard such an enormous achievement by eliminating Junior Brother Lu before he can rise, I suppose none of us here would do such a thing. Fortunately, Junior Brother Lu is considered one of us, and since the core is refined, let it be. Moreover, from what we know, Junior Brother Lu's character and morality are trustworthy. I suggest, we observe the situation quietly."

"I second that!" A Sun Blaze followed.

"I second that!"

"I second that!"

...

The three departments of Sun Blaze successively expressed agreement, thus concluding the refinement of the core matter once and for all.

The Sun Blaze from the Southern Region looked again at Su Yuqing: "Junior Sister, Junior Brother Lu will be entrusted to your care. The potential for growth in the Dao Tree lineage is undeniably immense, but we must ensure he doesn't stray onto a dark path. The downfall of the Nine Provinces thousands of years ago serves as a lesson, and we must remain vigilant; I do not wish for our clan to repeat the same mistakes one day!"

"I understand, I will take good care of him." Su Yuqing nodded solemnly.



============================================================
Chapter 1820: Chapter 1820 1818: The Domain Outside Is the Nine Provinces (Happy National Day)
============================================================

In the Core World, under Lu Ye's watchful gaze, he saw Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai gradually regain their senses, as the terrifying fluctuations of soul power gradually subsided.

Chen Xuanhai glanced in the direction where Lu Ye stood, his expression slightly complicated, and said, "Junior Sister, it's up to you."

Su Yuqing nodded.

Only then did Chen Xuanhai take flight, soaring out of the domain.

Lu Ye glanced in the direction of his departure, then stepped toward Su Yuqing, stopping before her and asking, "What's going on?"

Chen Xuanhai had looked at him with a somewhat peculiar expression earlier.

Su Yuqing pondered for a moment, then extended a hand to Lu Ye, softly saying, "Come."

Lu Ye placed his hand in her palm, and in the next instant, pure mana enveloped him, propelling the two of them toward the nearest spirit mountaintop.

A moment later, on that spirit mountaintop, Su Yuqing brought out two chairs, and they sat facing each other.

Lu Ye felt she might have something very important to discuss with him; otherwise, she wouldn't have made such a serious gesture. But since Su Yuqing hadn't brought it up yet, he didn't want to rush her, so he quietly waited.

After a while, Su Yuqing finally spoke, "How much do you know about the Dao Tree lineage?"

Lu Ye shook his head, "Not at all."

He had only heard this term from Veteran Fang, but back then Veteran Fang hadn't said much. So he asked in return, "Do you know?"

When he had mentioned the Dao Tree lineage previously, Su Yuqing had clearly reacted differently, evidently having heard of it.

"I've heard a bit. In fact, Xiyuan Pavilion has records about the Dao Tree lineage." Su Yuqing nodded.

Lu Ye was surprised, "Why didn't I see them?" When he first entered Mount Fangcun, he had stayed in Xiyuan Pavilion for several months, imprinting a large amount of information about stellar space and bringing it back to the Nine Provinces, filling the Nine Provinces' knowledge gap about stellar space.

Su Yuqing said, "Some secrets in Xiyuan Pavilion are not open to outsiders."

Lu Ye understood; that explained why he hadn't seen any such records.

"Tell me about it." Lu Ye sat up straight, actually quite interested in his inheritance. Moreover, he had asked Number Nine about this matter back in the day, but unfortunately, Number Nine couldn't provide any answers, only telling him that Lu Ye was not the first to receive this inheritance. Before him, several Nine Provinces cultivators had also obtained it, but none managed to grow.

Su Yuqing's voice came forth, "What I know are things recorded by my clan's ancestors, never witnessed with my own eyes, so just take a listen. Some things require your own judgment."

Lu Ye nodded solemnly.

"The Dao Tree is a path of inheritance and a very powerful one at that, with only one successor in each generation. Its specific form is likely as you described before—a tree within the body visible through inner sight. The last successor of the Dao Tree lineage appeared millennia ago, during a time when there was an exceptionally famous top-class domain belonging to the human race. Compared to the current Yellow Dragon World, it was even more formidable, and could be said to be the undisputed overlord domain of the human race. Unfortunately... such a top-class domain was ultimately destroyed because of the Dao Tree lineage."

"Why?" Lu Ye frowned.

He didn't fully grasp how powerful the Yellow Dragon World was, but after mixing in the All Phenomena Ocean for years, he had heard of the Yellow Dragon World's reputation numerous times. Nowadays, in the All Phenomena Ocean, the Yellow Dragon World solely occupied a top-class Spirit Island.

The overlord domain of the human race from a millennium ago was actually even stronger than the Yellow Dragon World, but such a domain was destroyed because of the Dao Tree lineage. This puzzled Lu Ye; he didn't understand what kind of causal relationship existed.

Su Yuqing said, "The Dao Tree successor of that generation was a cultivator from that top-class domain. He rose from obscurity to fame in stellar space, growing at an incredibly rapid pace. However, he committed acts that enraged the heavens and people, angering many forces. Not only did his reputation become notorious, but even his birth domain was implicated."

At this point, she sighed and gave Lu Ye a meaningful glance, "The Dao Tree lineage, in the vast world, nothing is there that it cannot refine. Your cultivation speed is so fast, it should be related to your inheritance. You must also know how much assistance this inheritance has provided you in your growth."

Lu Ye solemnly nodded.

Without the Talent Tree, he would never have achieved his current accomplishments.

"As you grew, did you ever use the power of the Dao Tree to refine living beings?" When she posed this question, Su Yuqing's expression was extremely serious.

Lu Ye decisively shook his head, "Never have."

"Can you confirm?"

"I can confirm!" Lu Ye nodded.

Actually, right after the first metamorphosis of the Talent Tree, Lu Ye had already discovered this matter. Since he could harness the power of the Talent Tree to refine the Spirit Stone, he could completely refine the spirit force within the cultivators for his own use, and even refine their blood Qi altogether.

Doing so would mean that every cultivator would become a cultivation resource he could refine.

But Lu Ye had never done so because he felt that it was no different from consuming people, which was psychologically hard to accept, so to date, no matter how many enemies he has slain, even though some of them were not from the human race, he has never refined their spirit force.

"That's good!" Su Yuqing took a deep breath, completely alleviating her concerns. She was really worried that Lu Ye might have done something similar.

"Is there any hidden danger in doing this?" Lu Ye saw her change in expression and vaguely guessed.

Su Yuqing nodded: "There is hidden danger, and quite significant. The Dao Tree lineage can refine all, but there is one thing that cannot be refined, or rather, cannot be completely refined!"

"What is it?" Lu Ye was incredibly curious. In his cultivation journey so far, he hadn't encountered anything that couldn't be refined; anything that could assist in his growth seemed to be refinable?

"Seven emotions and six desires!" Su Yuqing's red lips gently parted, "Or rather, the emotions of living beings with flesh and blood. Ten thousand years ago, the successor of the Dao Tree lineage didn't have exceptional aptitude, quite poor, in fact. But he soon discovered a method to rapidly enhance his aptitude: killing enemies and then refining them. This refinement not only improved his strength, but also his aptitude seemed to enhance as if the Dao Tree could strip away others' aptitudes to strengthen itself. Using this method, his strength grew stronger and his aptitude more outstanding, yet the more beings he refined, the more sinister his temperament became. Every enemy he killed was filled with various negative emotions before they died, and the Dao Tree couldn't completely purify these emotions, accumulating them within him."

"Later, in pursuit of greater strength and aptitude, he secretly harmed cultivators from many powerful factions, including successors from top-class domains. These people were all exceptionally talented, greatly aiding his growth. He ventured further and further down this dark path, leading to more and more slaughter, ultimately losing himself, and he brought calamity to his home domain as a result."

"After the incident was exposed, countless powerful factions allied to besiege that domain. Numerous Sun Blaze masters participated, making the domain a living hell for its inhabitants. If it weren't for the domain's warriors preparing beforehand and crafting a mysterious treasure to teleport the domain away, the whole domain might have been shattered by the battle!"

"Hmm?" Lu Ye originally listened as if it were an old story from ten thousand years ago, the predecessors' experiences cautioning him. But hearing this, he suddenly felt a strong sense of familiarity.

A certain domain's warriors prepared in advance, crafting a mysterious treasure to teleport the entire domain away at a critical moment…

He quickly asked: "What was the name of the Dao Tree successor from ten thousand years ago? Which domain did he come from?"

Su Yuqing thought for a moment and said, "That person was named Chao Nian, and the domain he came from was called Nine Provinces!" With these words, she reached out to grasp Lu Ye's hand, looking at him earnestly: "Lu Ye, you must heed Chao Nian's lesson. With the Dao Tree, you possess a faster growth rate than anyone else. Never succumb to the temptation to refine living beings casually; it will only harm you, never benefit you."

Lu Ye certainly won't do such things; if he were inclined to, he would've done it much earlier. Moreover, cultivation for him is simple; as long as the Talent Tree has ample fuel reserves, all he needs to do is dive into All Phenomena Ocean, so why refine living beings?

Since he hasn't embarked on this dark path earlier, he won't tread it in the future.

"I understand." Lu Ye nodded and looked at Su Yuqing, "Yuqing, there's something I need to tell you."

"Speak." Su Yuqing looked at him seriously.

Lu Ye gave a thumbs up: "The domain I come from outside is indeed Nine Provinces!"

Su Yuqing blinked her big eyes: "Isn't it Nine Heavens?"

She remembered Lu Ye previously claimed to be Lu Yiye of the Nine Heavens…

"Nine Heavens is just the public moniker. A senior once advised us to never mention the name Nine Provinces when traveling outside, hence the cultivators from our home domain always claim to be from Nine Heavens."

This matter was bound to be unhideable from the Dwarf Race. Once Mount Fangcun merges, the truth about Nine Provinces will eventually be known.

Facing Su Yuqing, Lu Ye had no intention of hiding it.

Su Yuqing was momentarily stunned before reacting, "Your Nine Provinces and Chao Nian's Nine Provinces…"

Lu Ye nodded: "Presumably, it is the same Nine Provinces!"

When he first met Number Nine, Number Nine used a means to let him see the scene of the previous Nine Provinces being besieged. At that time, he didn't know what sort of heinous act the previous Nine Provinces committed to provoke such formidable enemies to attack. Unfortunately, Number Nine couldn't explain to him either, as before the previous Nine Provinces were besieged, Number Nine had not yet developed spiritual intelligence.

The reason it could let Lu Ye witness that scene was primarily because the earth-shattering battle left too deep a mark on the origin of Nine Provinces. As the Heaven's Augury Compass Artifact Spirit combined with Nine Provinces' origin, it could naturally recall from Nine Provinces' origin.

Now he understands that the disaster for the previous Nine Provinces originated from Chao Nian, who went down a dark path and offended too many powerful factions, leading them to unite against the previous Nine Provinces.



============================================================
Chapter 1821: Chapter 1821 1819: Sorting Out the Core
============================================================

The former Nine Provinces where Chao Nian resided was a top-tier domain, but unfortunately, a single relocation nearly depleted the domain's foundation, causing the Nine Provinces to weaken, and only in recent years did it barely ascend to a large-scale domain.

Nowadays, everything is developing in a positive direction. The cultivators of the Nine Provinces have walked out of the stellar space, integrating with the All Phenomena Ocean, and the Nine Provinces itself is also supported by the Flower World. The two complement each other, and coupled with Number Nine's unique existence, the Nine Provinces has leaped into a rapidly growing large-scale domain.

This is an advantage that no other domain in the stellar space can match. It can be said that the future of the Nine Provinces is worth anticipating.

In front of Lu Ye, Su Yuqing suddenly realized: "So, ten thousand years ago, although Chao Nian died, the legacy of the Dao Tree lineage still remained in the Nine Provinces?"

"That's probably correct." Lu Ye nodded.

This legacy may have had other owners before Chao Nian, and several owners after him, until it was obtained by Lu Ye in recent years.

"I see!" Su Yuqing murmured.

Lu Ye looked at her: "Did you think of something?"

Su Yuqing said: "Actually, when I saw these records about the Nine Provinces and Chao Nian back then, I was puzzled by one thing. The Nine Provinces was, after all, the pinnacle domain occupied by the human race at that time. No matter how many evil deeds Chao Nian committed, those many forces only needed to kill Chao Nian to avenge themselves—so why did they rally to attack the Nine Provinces? In retrospect, Chao Nian might have merely been an inducement. The real purpose of these forces was the Dao Tree's legacy. They must have known by then that the Dao Tree legacy still resided in the Nine Provinces!

Simple grievances weren't enough to target the Nine Provinces in such a way, but with enough benefits, it's different.

The temptation of the Dao Tree legacy was too great, and Chao Nian's actions provided them with sufficient reasons and excuses, so a grand play of many forces joining hands to siege the Nine Provinces began.

If it weren't for the strong ones of the former Nine Provinces having been prepared, expending massive energy and resources to create the Heaven's Augury Compass, and using the power of the Compass to relocate the Nine Provinces, the entire Nine Provinces would have been excavated three feet deep after that battle.

"Lu Ye." Su Yuqing spoke solemnly, "What the elder you mentioned advised was correct. When you go out, you must never mention the Nine Provinces. Ten thousand years is a long time, but to those major forces, it isn't that long. The name of the Nine Provinces and the legacy of the Dao Tree could invite catastrophe."

Lu Ye nodded.

"As for the Dwarf Race over here, for now, only our Sun Blaze is aware of this matter. The information won't leak, so you can rest easy."

Now Lu Ye is the Master of Core Origin, destined to become the lord of Mount Fangcun in the future, which basically binds him with Mount Fangcun. They share weal and woe, and hence, the Sun Blaze of the Dwarf Race certainly won't do anything against his interests.

Lu Ye isn't worried about this. However, after today's chat with Su Yuqing, he has learned some secrets closely related to himself.

Suddenly, he remembered something: "By the way, if the three parts of Mount Fangcun are to be merged, roughly how long will it take?"

Su Yuqing calculated slightly and replied: "We in the Eastern Region are the closest, probably need less than three years, the Southern Region takes over ten years, and the Western Region, being the furthest, might need at least thirty to forty years."

"Then I'd better hurry." Lu Ye thought to himself, the Southern and Western Regions have ample time to merge, but the Eastern Region requires less than three years, which is quite urgent.

"What's wrong?" Su Yuqing was puzzled.

Lu Ye explained: "Although I've refined the Origin and the consciousness of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, the erosion of one drop of treasure blood on the Core World is everywhere. Now, throughout the Core World, the power of the treasure blood still lingers. I need to sort it out thoroughly and cleanse the remaining power of the treasure blood. Only then, when Mount Fangcun merges, the Dwarf side will not have worries."

"Will three years be enough?" Su Yuqing's expression tightened. She clearly realized that if the residual power of the treasure blood is not thoroughly sorted out, it would lead to dire consequences.

"Roughly enough. If not, it doesn't matter; I'll then seal the core, preventing the Eastern Region from merging."

He had sealed the core before, and doing so again would be no challenge.

"Then thank you for your hard work." Su Yuqing nodded.

Lu Ye looked at her beautiful visage, blinking: "It is quite hard, but if there's a reward, I'd be more motivated!"

Su Yuqing gave a charming smile, slowly rose: "Wait until you are done sorting the core!"

With that, her figure shot up, headed beyond the realm, with Lu Ye's voice trailing behind her: "Remember you said it!"

Watching Su Yuqing depart, Lu Ye finally composed himself, shortly thereafter, his figure flickered, entering the origin space.

Gazing throughout, the Core Origin stood tall like a great sun, but unlike when first seen, the origin now is no longer shrouded in red but appears pure and flawless.

The origin was intact, yet the entire domain still needed sorting.

Lu Ye directly leaped onto the origin, sitting cross-legged, relying on his status as the Master of Core Origin, examining the entire Core World, extending the power of the Talent Tree, refining the remaining treasure blood power bit by bit.

On the Nine Provinces side, he had no worries. Not to mention there are now four Moon Jade Late Stage cultivators stationed in the Nine Provinces, even Sun Blaze counts two, Lu Ye believes that while he's sorting the Core World, Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai will take good care of the Nine Provinces.

Day after day, year after year.

Sorting the domain was extremely tedious, yet Lu Ye couldn't afford any negligence, otherwise, any residual power of the treasure blood could lead to unforeseeable consequences.

As the residual power of the treasure blood continued to be refined, Lu Ye felt his saintliness growing steadily. He wondered how much strength Lih Tian could exert if he were not dead and stood before him, suppressed by his saintliness.

Before refining the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, his saintliness was already unmatched by any Blood Race. Now, after refining a drop of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, his saintliness had grown terrifyingly, making such suppression lethal to the Blood Race.

Su Yuqing and Chen Xuanhai occasionally came to the Core World to check on things, but they never disturbed him. Only once did Lu Ye take the initiative to contact Su Yuqing and learn that they were staying in the Nine Provinces, living peacefully and leisurely.

For the two of them, all they could do now was wait, because before long, the East would integrate under the core's guidance.

Once the Southern Region and Western Region return one after another in the future, the unification of the Dwarf Race will occur, something both Sun Blaze are eagerly anticipating.

Mount Fangcun had been divided for so long, but their generation finally had the opportunity to revive their ancestors' glory, and everyone shared in that honor.

Three years passed by slowly.

Until this day, in the Origin space, Lu Ye, after several careful explorations and searches, confirmed that there was no residual treasure blood power left in the core space, he let out a long breath.

Counting the three years spent refining the treasure blood before, he had devoted six years of time for the matters of the Core World.

During this period, he did not cultivate, and his strength barely grew, but he believed it was all worth it.

Speaking of his own gains, though his strength hadn't grown, his saintliness had undergone a monumental change. In the future, when facing the Blood Race, even the Sun Blaze, he could handle them with ease.

Moreover, he had become the Master of Core Origin, and in the future, he would truly be the World Lord of Mount Fangcun!

In this way, the Dwarf Race would become the strongest backing for the Nine Provinces, and during his travels, he wouldn't need to worry about any problems occurring in the Nine Provinces.

The six years of effort brought such rewards; it was well worth it!

As for his own strength, once these matters are concluded, he could replenish it by taking a trip to the All Phenomena Ocean, and after these years of settling, his cultivation in the Moon Jade Mid-Stage was stable enough.

Buoyed by joy, Lu Ye exited seclusion.

With a flicker, he left the Core World.

"Venerable Lord!" A familiar voice immediately reached him.

Lu Ye turned and saw it was Xiang Yin and sister, who had been guarding here.

Lu Ye nodded slightly and turned to look in a direction. In that moment, he could sense something incredibly close rushing towards him, something that seemed to be a missing part of himself.

He suddenly understood that the Eastern Mount Fangcun was approaching rapidly, and the feeling of missing was perceived as the Origin Lord, not a lack within himself.

"Brother Chen Xuanhai and Sister Su Yuqing, where are they?" Lu Ye inquired.

Xiang Yin immediately replied, "The two masters left recently to welcome the Eastern Mount Fangcun. Mistress said this integration might cause some upheaval, so they need to be stationed in the east, and asked me to convey the message for the Venerable Lord to maintain stability in the core."

Lu Ye nodded, "I understand."

After a careful sense, he confirmed that in a few days, the Eastern Mount Fangcun would integrate, prompting Lu Ye to decide to wait in the core.

He instructed, "You may leave now, there's no need for you here."

"Understood!" Xiang Yin and sister complied, heading straight back in the direction of the Nine Provinces.

Lu Ye looked up at the Blood Refinement World spanning the Void in the distance, suppressing a sudden wave of anxiety. Regardless, the integration of Mount Fangcun was a priority, so it must be addressed first.

He then flickered and entered the Core World once more, quietly waiting.

Several days passed swiftly, the stationed in the core Lu Ye suddenly opened his eyes, even though he couldn't see anything, he could clearly sense that the Eastern Mount Fangcun had arrived!

Almost instantly as the thought emerged, the world changed.

A massive buzzing sound emanated from all directions, the space within the Core World became distorted. The entire world seemed to become more complete, the domain rapidly expanding...not expanding, but rather like missing pieces of a puzzle similar assembling.

This assembly caused the core world and even the east to shake uneasily.

Lu Ye raised his hand, his thoughts moving, Origin Power deployed, like an invisible large hand, smoothing over the turbulent areas, in an instant, tranquility restored!

The turbulence from the integration of the Eastern Mount Fangcun with the core lasted a full fortnight, and when all settled after the fortnight, Lu Ye clearly sensed that the Core World had expanded many times over, with many familiar landscapes now added, those originally belonging to the Eastern Mount Fangcun.



============================================================
Chapter 1820: Chapter 1820 1818: The Domain Outside Is the Nine Provinces (Happy National Day)
============================================================
